# CHANGES

Substantive behavioral deviations of pypdfbox vs upstream Apache PDFBox.
Per-release notes go here; trivial naming changes (camelCase → snake_case) are not listed.

## Format

```
- pypdfbox/<path>: <one-line description of deviation>
  upstream: PDFBox <version> <java path>
  reason: <why we deviate>
```

## Project-wide deviations vs upstream

- **No `preflight` module.** Apache PDFBox 4.0 removes Preflight; we follow that decision. PDF/A and PDF/UA validation is performed via external veraPDF / PAC.
- **No commons-logging / log4j.** Python `logging` (stdlib) is used throughout.
- **Method naming.** Java camelCase → Python snake_case across the entire API surface. Semantics unchanged.

## Per-file deviations

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_appearance_content_stream.py`: dashed borders without explicit `/D` materialize the default `[3]` dash pattern.
- `pypdfbox/loader.py`: exposes Java-style `loadPDF`, `loadFDF`, and `loadXFDF` aliases.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/afm_loader.py`: bundled AFM resources load through `importlib.resources` handles instead of filesystem paths.
- `pypdfbox/io/scratch_file.py`: exposes main-memory-only ScratchFile factory aliases.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/taggedpdf/pd_print_field_attribute_object.py`: print-field role and checked-state getters accept COS string-backed names.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_acro_form.py`: form flattening guards against cyclic `/Kids` graphs.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/image/`: image factories expose Java-style PDFBox creation aliases.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/ttf_data_stream.py`: `read_unsigned_int()` treats any negative byte as EOF.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/pd_encryption.py`, `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/pd_crypt_filter_dictionary.py`: dictionary wrappers expose `get_cos_dictionary()`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pd_metadata.py`: filtered metadata size reports decoded XMP byte length.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_file_attachment.py`: exposes PDFBox attachment-name aliases, including the legacy misspelled setter.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_icc_based.py`: malformed ICCBased `/Range` arrays default component ranges to `(0.0, 1.0)`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_font_factory.py`: embedded font-program headers are read from decoded stream bytes.
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py`: lenient parsing attempts shifted-offset recovery before rejecting out-of-bounds `startxref`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/filespecification/pd_embedded_file.py`: malformed PDF date timezone offsets return `None`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_viewer_preferences.py`: includes the long-form deprecated `UseOC` non-full-screen page mode constant.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_stream.py`: `stop_filters` canonicalizes standard filter aliases before comparison.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_cid_system_info.py`: string rendering uses Java-style `null` for missing registry or ordering.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pd_number_tree_node.py`: switching a number tree node to kids clears stale `/Nums` and refreshes ancestor limits.
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: incremental saves track absolute output offsets after copied source bytes.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_java_script.py`: stream-form `/JS` actions decode through `COSStream.to_text_string()`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/destination/`: default coordinate-based destination constructors include optional coordinate slots as `COSNull`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_content_stream.py`: `move_text_position_and_set_leading()` requires an active text block.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_dictionary.py`: raw `get_item` supports the PDFBox alternate-key overload shape.
- `pypdfbox/filter/flate_decode.py`: Flate encode/decode flushes output sinks after writing.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_border_effect_dictionary.py`: `set_style(None)` clears optional `/S`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_cal_rgb.py`: missing or cleared `/Matrix` returns the identity matrix.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/encoding/dictionary_encoding.py`: symbolic reader-mode encodings without a valid base or built-in encoding fail explicitly.
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_stream_parser.py`: inline-image parsing only treats exact `ID` as image data, leaving `I` and longer operator names as normal operators.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/pd_function_type4.py`: Type 4 function parsing rejects missing and stray closing braces.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_choice.py`: one-element nested `/Opt` entries are preserved in display values so tolerated malformed option arrays keep export/display alignment.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/true_type_font.py`: synthesized header metadata preserves `head.created` and `head.modified` as UTC `datetime` values.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_structure_node.py`: direct structure-element kid append/remove operations maintain the child's `/P` parent pointer.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/form/pd_transparency_group_attributes.py`: cached `/CS` color spaces are invalidated when the raw COS source is externally replaced or removed.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/security_provider.py`: `/Adobe.PubSec` resolves through the public-key security handler factory.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/image/pd_image_x_object.py`: stencil image XObjects now treat missing `/ColorSpace` as implicit `DeviceGray`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/measurement/pd_media_clip.py`, `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/measurement/pd_rendition.py`: media clip and rendition factories dereference indirect objects and treat unresolved or null references as absent.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/outline/pd_outline_item.py`, `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/outline/pd_outline_node.py`: sibling insertion rewrites inserted item parents consistently.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/cff/cff_font.py`: empty or unparsed CFF fonts return safe width/path fallbacks.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/fdf/fdf_annotation_line.py`: FDF line annotations expose `/L` accessors and malformed coordinate arrays read as absent.
- `pypdfbox/io/random_access_read_buffer.py`: wraps `io.BytesIO` instead of reimplementing PDFBox's chunked-list storage. Observable behavior is identical; implementation is C-backed and ~25 lines instead of ~120. Justification: PRD §3.7 (stdlib-first for generic infrastructure).
- `pypdfbox/io/random_access_read_buffered_file.py`: wraps `io.BufferedReader` over a raw file fd. Stdlib provides the read-ahead buffering that upstream's `RandomAccessReadBufferedFile` implements manually. Justification: PRD §3.7.
- `pypdfbox/io/random_access_read_memory_mapped.py`: net-new optional implementation backed by `mmap.mmap`. No upstream counterpart; offered as opt-in for very large files where kernel paging beats userspace buffering. Justification: PRD §3.7 — use stdlib affordances when they fit.
- `pypdfbox/io/random_access_read_view.py`: original slice-view implementation. Mirrors the upstream `RandomAccessReadView` API; storage strategy is direct seek-on-parent rather than upstream's bounded-stream wrapper.
- `pypdfbox/io/scratch_file.py`: backed by `tempfile.SpooledTemporaryFile` (mixed mode), `tempfile.TemporaryFile` (temp-file-only), or `io.BytesIO` (memory-only). Upstream uses page-based scratch storage; we delegate spill-to-disk policy to stdlib. Behavior visible to callers (read/write/seek/clear) is identical. Justification: PRD §3.7. Default spill threshold in MIXED mode without an explicit cap is 16 MiB.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_font_like.py`, `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_vector_font.py`: upstream Java `interface`s modelled as `typing.Protocol` (runtime-checkable) so existing duck-typed font classes satisfy `isinstance(...)` without inheritance — Python idiom, no observable behaviour change. AWT-typed returns (`Matrix`, `BoundingBox`, `Vector`, `GeneralPath`) are widened to `Any` since pypdfbox is AWT-free.

## Backfill — aligned with upstream test expectations

Driven by porting upstream JUnit tests (PRD §12.1):

- `pypdfbox/io/random_access_read.py`: added `read_fully(buf, offset, length)` (raises `EOFError` on premature EOF) and `skip(n)` (clamps to length). Mirrors upstream `RandomAccessRead.readFully` / `skip`.
- `pypdfbox/io/random_access_read_buffer.py`, `_buffered_file.py`, `_memory_mapped.py`, `_view.py`: `seek(negative)` now raises `OSError` (was `ValueError`), `seek(past_end)` clamps to length and leaves the stream at EOF (was: raised `ValueError`). Matches upstream PDFBox semantics; required by ported `seek*` tests.
- `pypdfbox/io/random_access_read_view.py`: removed `start_position + length > parent_length` validation (upstream allows logical views past parent end; reads simply stop at parent EOF). `create_view()` on a view raises `OSError` (upstream forbids).
- `pypdfbox/io/random_access_read_buffered_file.py` / `_memory_mapped.py`: `create_view()` overrides the ABC default to mirror upstream — opens a fresh sibling underlying handle/mapping and constructs the view with `close_parent=True`, so view reads do not contend with the parent's seek cursor and the sibling is released on view close.
- `pypdfbox/io/scratch_file.py::ScratchFileBuffer.create_view()` raises `NotImplementedError` (upstream's `UnsupportedOperationException`).
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_number.py`: new abstract base `COSNumber` (parses string → `COSInteger`/`COSFloat`, handling exponential notation and Java-Long-out-of-range markers). `COSInteger`/`COSFloat` now extend `COSNumber`.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_float.py`: values are now clamped to **IEEE-754 single precision** (`float32`) on both `__init__` paths to match Java `float` semantics — required for upstream parity tests on `equals()`/`hashCode()`. `_normalize_negatives` recovers from PDFBOX-2990 / -3369 / -3500 / -4289 misplaced-`-` cases (`--16.33` → `-16.33`, `0.-262` → `-0.262`, `0.00000-33917698` → `-0.0000033917698`); raises `OSError` on unrecoverable double-`-`.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_integer.py`: added `is_valid()` / `set_valid()` for PDFBOX-5176 large-integer-out-of-Long-range marking.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_string.py`: `parse_hex` raises `OSError` (was `ValueError`) to mirror upstream `IOException`. Added `to_hex_string()`.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_stream.py`: `create_raw_input_stream()` raises `OSError` when no body. `create_input_stream(stop_filters=None)` and `create_output_stream(filters=None)` now wire up to `pypdfbox.filter.FilterFactory` and run the `/Filter` chain on read / encode it on close. Encryption-aware stream wrapping (`COSStream.create_view` over an encrypted scratch buffer) is still deferred. `/Predictor` encode + decode are both supported via `FlateDecode` / `LZWDecode` (PNG 10-15 incl. Optimum, TIFF 2).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pd_stream.py`: `create_input_stream` and `create_output_stream` now delegate to `COSStream` (single source of truth for filter plumbing). `to_byte_array()` returns `b""` for an empty stream (upstream raises `IOException`); empty `create_input_stream()` returns an empty `BytesIO` rather than raising — `PDStream` is a typed handle that legitimately wraps fresh-and-empty streams. `get_length()` returns `int | None` (was `int`); `None` indicates no `/Length` entry *and* no body.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_array.py`: added `remove_object`, `remove_all`, `retain_all`, `grow_to_size`, typed `set_name`/`get_name`/`set_int`/`get_int`/`set_string`/`get_string`, `set_float_array`/`to_float_array`, `to_cos_*_list` converters, factory classmethods `of_cos_names`/`of_cos_strings`/`of_cos_integers`/`of_cos_floats`. All match upstream signatures.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_document.py`: added `add_xref_table`, `get_objects_by_type`, `get_linearized_dictionary` — now returns a typed `PDLinearizationDictionary` wrapper (PDF 32000-1 Annex F: `/Linearized /L /H /O /E /N /T`) by scanning the object pool for the first dictionary carrying a truthy `/Linearized` entry; result is cached. `None` when the document is not linearized.
- `pypdfbox/cos/pd_linearization_dictionary.py`: new typed wrapper around the linearization parameter dictionary. Upstream PDFBox parses the same fields inline inside `PDDocument`; pypdfbox extracts them into a dedicated class so the COS-level entry point (`COSDocument.get_linearized_dictionary`) returns a structured value rather than a raw `COSDictionary`.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_name.py`: added single-letter and short-name constants (`A`, `B`, `C`, `D`, `T`, `BE`, `PARAMS`, `FLATE_DECODE`, `ASCII85_DECODE`, `STANDARD_ENCODING`) referenced by ported tests.
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/base_parser.py::read_name`: a `#` not followed by two hex digits is now kept literally rather than raising `PDFParseError`. Matches upstream `TestBaseParser.testInvalidHexSequence`.

## Filter module + Loader (parallel wave)

- `pypdfbox/filter/ascii85_decode.py`: encode/decode delegate to stdlib `base64.a85encode` / `a85decode` (which already implements PDF's base-85 + `z` shortcut + adobe `<~ ... ~>` framing). Original wrapper handles whitespace pre-cleaning, `~>` terminator stripping, and per-spec error reporting (`OSError`).
- `pypdfbox/filter/flate_decode.py`: `zlib` wrapper. PNG predictors 10-15 + TIFF predictor 2 supported on both decode and encode; predictor 15 (Optimum) picks the per-row filter type that minimises the sum of signed-absolute byte values (RFC 2083 §9.6 heuristic).
- `pypdfbox/filter/ascii_hex_decode.py`: `binascii` wrapper. Whitespace ignored, odd-digit pad with `0`, terminates on `>`.
- `pypdfbox/filter/run_length_decode.py`: ported line-for-line so encoded bytes match upstream byte-identical.
- `pypdfbox/filter/lzw_decode.py`: PDF-flavored LZW (9-12 bit codes, MSB-first, EarlyChange honored on decode; encoder always emits EarlyChange=1 with the PDFBOX-1977 final-EOD-width fix).
- `pypdfbox/filter/ccitt_fax_decode.py`: T.4 (Group 3, K=0 / K>0) and T.6 (Group 4, K<0) decode by wrapping the encoded strip in a synthetic little-endian TIFF and handing it to libtiff via Pillow. `/Columns`, `/Rows`, `/K`, `/BlackIs1`, `/EncodedByteAlign` honored; `/EndOfLine`, `/EndOfBlock`, `/DamagedRowsBeforeError` accepted but inert (libtiff handles framing). `/Rows` omitted → libtiff fills a generous over-allocated height with zero-padding past actual end-of-data; callers should supply `/Rows` from the image XObject's `/Height` for a tight buffer. Decode-only (no encoder use case yet — `encode()` raises `NotImplementedError`). Output is raw bit-packed scanlines (rows padded to whole bytes, MSB-first), the same shape PDImageXObject's decoded body expects.
- `pypdfbox/filter/jbig2_decode.py`: `/JBIG2Decode` (ISO 32000-1 §7.4.7) decode via the Rust-backed `jbig2-parser` library (MIT, newly approved dependency). `/JBIG2Globals` from `/DecodeParms` (single dict or array indexed by filter position; `/DP` short-form alias also accepted) is decoded through its own `/Filter` chain via `COSStream.to_byte_array()` and prepended to the per-image segments before handoff to `jbig2_parser.parse_jbig2`. The parser returns a PNG buffer; we re-decode it through Pillow to recover raw bilevel sample bytes. JBIG2 is bilevel by ITU-T T.88 definition, so `DecodeResult.parameters` is always populated with `/BitsPerComponent = 1` and `/ColorComponents = 1` plus the codestream's intrinsic `/Width` and `/Height`. PDF spec defines no short-name abbreviation for `/JBIG2Decode` — only the long name is registered. Decode-only (`encode()` raises `NotImplementedError`); a malformed `/JBIG2Globals` value of the wrong COS type is silently ignored rather than crashing the image decode.
- `pypdfbox/filter/_predictor.py` (new): shared PNG/TIFF predictor encode (`predict`) + decode (`unpredict`) helpers, used by both `FlateDecode` and `LZWDecode`. Replaces the previously-duplicated inline `_unpredict` blocks in each filter. Supports predictors 1, 2, 10-15 across 1/2/4/8/16-bit components and any colors/columns combo.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_document.py`: optional `source: RandomAccessRead | None` parameter / instance attribute so `Loader` can attach the file handle it created and have `doc.close()` close it. Caller-supplied sources stay caller-owned.
- `pypdfbox/loader.py`: top-level `Loader.load_pdf()` accepts path / `bytes` / `bytearray` / `memoryview` / `BinaryIO` / `RandomAccessRead`. Mirrors `org.apache.pdfbox.Loader.loadPDF()`. Encryption / password / `MemoryUsageSetting` parameters deferred until those features ship.
- `pypdfbox/__init__.py`: exports `Loader` so `from pypdfbox import Loader` works (matches PRD §7).
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_stream_parser.py`: extends `COSParser`. Surfaces an `Operator` value type carrying the operator name plus optional `image_parameters` / `image_data` for inline-image (`BI` ... `ID` ... `EI`) sequences. Lenient PDFBox quirks preserved: stray `]` returns `COSNull`, isolated `+` returns `COSNull`, internal `-` in numbers dropped (PDFBOX-4064), Type-3 `d0`/`d1` operator suffix accepted.

## pdfwriter cluster #1 (full-save, traditional xref)

- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: cluster #1 covers full-save mode only. The following upstream paths are stubbed and raise `NotImplementedError` until later clusters land:
  - `incremental=True` constructor flag → cluster #2 (incremental save).
  - Xref-stream output (`writeXrefStream` and friends) → cluster #3.
  - Object-stream packing (`COSWriterObjectStream`) → cluster #3.
  - Encrypted documents (`is_encrypted()` → `True`) → security cluster.
  - Signatures (`SignatureInterface`, `/ByteRange` ranges) → cluster #2.
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: `write(document)` accepts a `COSDocument` directly. Upstream's overloads also take `PDDocument` / `FDFDocument`; those wrappers are not yet ported (`PDDocument` → PRD §6.6 cluster).
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: `/ID` synthesis uses `hashlib.sha256(time_ns + secrets.token_bytes(16))[:16]` instead of upstream's `Long.toString(idTime) + info-dict-values` digest. Same shape (two 16-byte hex strings) and same purpose; we don't have a `PDDocument.getDocumentId()` to thread in yet.

## pdfwriter cluster #2 (incremental save)

- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: `COSWriter(..., incremental=True, incremental_input=...)` now ships. The writer copies the source bytes to the output verbatim and appends only objects whose resolved value (or its `COSObject` wrapper) carries `is_needs_to_be_updated()=True`. The appended xref section lists only the changed/new objects, the trailer carries `/Prev = old_startxref`, `/Size = max_obj_num + 1`, and preserves `/ID` exactly as the source had it. Mirrors upstream `doWriteIncrement` + `prepareIncrement` + `doWriteXRefInc`.
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: digital-signature re-signing is **not** implemented. When a source signature dict (`/Type /Sig` or `/DocTimeStamp`) contains a `/ByteRange [0 0 0 0]` placeholder (or any byterange whose third entry doesn't extend past the original file end), `save_incremental` raises `NotImplementedError` rather than silently corrupt the signature. The actual digest pipeline lands with the security cluster.
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: `save_incremental` on a document with **no** dirty objects produces an output **byte-for-byte identical to the source**. Upstream's behaviour matches: nothing extra is appended. Unlike full-save mode, no `/ID` synthesis happens in incremental mode — the source's `/ID` array (if any) stays exactly as it was.
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: an in-memory `BytesIO` increment buffer accumulates the appended objects + xref + trailer; the real output sink only sees source-bytes followed by buffer-contents at the very end. Mirrors upstream's `ByteArrayOutputStream` → `incrementalOutput` pipeline. The buffer is initialised with `position=0`; absolute byte offsets in the new xref are computed as `source_length + buffer_offset` at emit time (upstream cheats by seeding `position` with `inputData.length()` on the `COSStandardOutputStream`; functionally identical, easier to test in isolation).
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: a CRLF separator is emitted at the very start of the increment buffer when there is at least one dirty object. This matches upstream's `getStandardOutput().writeCRLF()` at the top of `visitFromDocument` in incremental mode and guarantees an unambiguous boundary between the source's trailing `%%EOF` and the appended block. When nothing is dirty the separator is **not** emitted (preserving the byte-for-byte-identical contract).
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_document.py`: added `get_source()` (read-only accessor for the parser-attached `RandomAccessRead`), `get_start_xref()` / `set_start_xref(offset)` (the offset of the trailing xref section, used by the incremental writer for `/Prev`).
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py`: after parsing the trailing `startxref` value, calls `document.set_start_xref(...)` so the incremental writer can find it later.

## pdfwriter cluster #3 (xref-stream + object-stream output)

- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: `COSWriter(..., xref_stream=True)` (with `set_xref_stream(b)` / `is_xref_stream_output()` toggles) emits a single `/Type /XRef` indirect-object stream in place of the traditional `xref` keyword + `trailer` keyword pair (PDF 32000-1 §7.5.8). Trailer entries (`/Root`, `/Info`, `/Encrypt`, `/ID`) are folded into the xref-stream dictionary as required by §7.5.8.4. `/W` field widths are computed dynamically (`w1=1`, `w2=ceil_log256(max_offset)`, `w3=2`); `/Index` always lists the contiguous object-number ranges. The xref-stream object goes through the regular `visit_from_stream` path so its body is FlateDecode-compressed and — when an active security handler is staged — encrypted with its own per-object key. Default remains the traditional xref table.
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: `COSWriter(..., object_stream=True)` (with `set_object_stream(b)` / `is_object_stream_output()` toggles) packs eligible non-stream indirect objects into one or more `/Type /ObjStm` streams (PDF 32000-1 §7.5.7), capped at 100 objects per ObjStm to mirror upstream PDFBox's `COSWriterObjectStream` ceiling. Streams, the `/Encrypt` dictionary, and signature dictionaries (`/Type /Sig`, `/Type /DocTimeStamp`) are excluded by spec. Type-2 xref entries are emitted in the surrounding xref stream; the regular indirect-object frame for a packed object is suppressed. Object-stream packing requires xref-stream output (the cluster does not auto-promote — callers must set both flags).
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: hybrid xref tables (`/XRefStm` pointing back at a traditional xref) — supported by upstream for backward compatibility with PDF-1.4-only readers — are not yet emitted. Callers that need that fallback should save with `xref_stream=False`.

- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator.py`: operands list is stored on the `Operator` instance (`get_operands()` / `set_operands()`). Upstream keeps the operand stack on `PDFStreamEngine` / `PDFStreamParser`; pypdfbox attaches operands directly to the `Operator` returned by the parser as a convenience for token consumers (the parser already does this — see `pdf_stream_parser.py`). The cached singletons returned by `Operator.get_operator(name)` for ordinary operators must therefore be treated as flyweights — do not mutate operands on a cached instance you did not just receive from the parser.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator.py`: cache uses a plain `dict` plus a `threading.Lock` instead of upstream `ConcurrentHashMap.putIfAbsent`. Functionally identical under the GIL.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/pd_content_stream.py`: `get_matrix()` is typed `Any` rather than `Matrix` because `pypdfbox.util.Matrix` is not yet ported (it lands with the rendering cluster). Subclasses may return a `COSArray` (the on-disk form) until then.

## pdmodel cluster #3 (PDStream + XObject family)

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pd_stream.py`: stream construction/output with `filters` records the `/Filter` chain but stores caller-supplied bytes as-is. Upstream writes through `COSStream.createOutputStream(filters)` and therefore encodes on write; pypdfbox defers encode-on-write until the filter encoding surface is widened. Decoding existing filtered bytes is supported through `FilterFactory`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/image/pd_image_x_object.py`: image decoding, color-space wrapping, array color spaces, and rendered image conversion are deferred to rendering / graphics-color clusters. Cluster #3 exposes image metadata, raw `/ColorSpace` names, filter access, and decoded byte streams only.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/form/pd_form_x_object.py`: `get_matrix()` returns a plain six-float list until `pypdfbox.util.Matrix` lands with the rendering cluster.

## pdmodel cluster #5 lite (annotations)

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation.py`: factory dispatch is intentionally truncated to Link/Text/Square/Circle plus `PDAnnotationUnknown`; Widget, Markup, and heavier annotation subclasses are deferred to forms/rendering clusters.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_link.py`: action and destination accessors return raw COS objects until `PDAction` and the full `PDDestination` family land in pdmodel cluster #7.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_square_circle.py`: inherits directly from `PDAnnotation` instead of upstream `PDAnnotationMarkup`; border style, border effect, and interior color use raw COS containers until their typed wrappers land.

## pdmodel cluster #7 partial (outlines / destinations / actions)

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/outline/*`: outline tree/list mechanics are present, with typed destination/action accessors for the common action and destination wrappers in this cluster.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/destination/*`: ships named, Fit/FitB, FitH/FitBH, FitV/FitBV, FitR, and XYZ destinations. Page destinations resolve integer indices plus direct or indirect page objects when a `PDDocument`/`PDPageTree` context is supplied.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/destination/pd_destination_name_tree_node.py`: lightweight destination name-tree wrapper supports flat `/Names` arrays only. Broader destination-specific adoption of generic `PDNameTreeNode` remains deferred.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pd_name_tree_node.py` + `pd_string_name_tree_node.py`: generic `/Names`-tree base + string-keyed concrete subclass; `IOException` → `OSError`; `/Limits` placeholder slots use `COSNull.NULL` since `COSArray` slots are typed `COSBase` (Java's literal `null` has no Python equivalent); `COSArrayList` not used (`get_kids()` returns a plain `list`). `PDStringNameTreeNode.convert_value_to_cos` is additive (upstream omits the value→COS direction).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pd_number_tree_node.py`: int-keyed analog of `PDNameTreeNode` (used by `/PageLabels`, `/ParentTree`). Mirrors PDNameTreeNode's Generic[T] + ABC pattern instead of upstream's reflection-based `convertCOSToPD`. `setKids` does not round-trip through `COSArrayList`; returns a plain `list`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_name_dictionary.py` + `pd_document_name_destination_dictionary.py` + `pd_embedded_files_name_tree_node.py` + `pd_javascript_name_tree_node.py`: typed catalog `/Names` wrapper plus its embedded-files / javascript / dests sub-wrappers. `PDJavascriptNameTreeNode` leaf type is Python `str` (the JS source body) rather than `PDActionJavaScript`. Catalog categories `/AP`, `/Pages`, `/Templates`, `/IDS`, `/URLS`, `/AlternatePresentations`, `/Renditions` are deferred (rarely used; mostly absent in upstream too).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_catalog.py`: `get_names()` now returns the typed `PDDocumentNameDictionary` wrapper (was `NotImplementedError` stub).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_widget.py`: typed widget annotation. `/AA`, `/BS`, `/MK`, `/Parent` accessors return raw COSDictionary — typed `PDFormFieldAdditionalActions`, `PDBorderStyleDictionary`, `PDAppearanceCharacteristicsDictionary`, and typed `PDField` parent are deferred (the parent typing in particular avoids a form↔annotation circular import).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/*`: scaffold ports of `PDStructureTreeRoot`, `PDStructureElement`, `PDMarkInfo`. Upstream `PDStructureNode` base collapsed (root + element wrap COSDictionary directly until typed parent chain is needed). `getKids()` returns raw `COSBase` list (no `PDStructureElement`/`PDMarkedContentReference` typed dispatch). `getParentTree()` returns raw COS (no typed `PDNumberTreeNode<PDParentTreeValue>`). `getClassMap()` returns raw entries (no typed `PDAttributeObject`). `PDStructureElement` `/A` attributes, `/C` class names, `getStandardStructureType()`, `getPage()`/`setPage()`, the four `appendKid` overloads + `insertBefore` + `removeKid` — all deferred. `PDMarkInfo`: upstream's `setSuspect(false)`-only bug is fixed here (we write the actual value). `PDStructureTreeRoot.get_id_tree()` uses a private `PDStructureElementNameTreeNode` colocated subclass mirroring upstream's class.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_catalog.py`: `get_struct_tree_root()`, `get_mark_info()`, `get_oc_properties()` now return their typed wrappers (was `NotImplementedError` stubs).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_text_field.py` + `pd_button.py` + `pd_push_button.py` + `pd_radio_button.py` + `pd_check_box.py` + `pd_choice.py` + `pd_combo_box.py` + `pd_list_box.py` + `pd_signature_field.py` + `pd_variable_text.py`: typed PDField subclasses replacing `PDFieldStub` for known `/FT`. Deferred surface: `PDTextField` rich-text DOM serialization to `/RV`; `PDCheckBox.get_on_value` walks first widget kid only (falls back to `"Yes"`); `PDVariableText.get_rich_text_value` reads stream payload as best-effort UTF-8.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_catalog.py`: `get_acro_form()` now returns the typed `PDAcroForm` wrapper (was `NotImplementedError` stub).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_output_intent.py`: lite port of `PDOutputIntent`. `/DestOutputProfile` exposed as typed `PDStream` (raw `COSStream` accessor preserved as `get_dest_output_profile_cos`). `set_data(profile_bytes, num_components=3)` embeds raw ICC bytes and writes `/N`; sniffs the ICC `acsp` magic at offset 36 (ICC.1:2010 §7.2 table 17) and warns lenient on miss. Full ICC profile parsing / `PDICCBased` typed colour-space integration still deferred.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_sound.py`: `set_custom_appearance_handler()` is supported, but the built-in upstream `PDSoundAppearanceHandler` default path is still a no-op until sound appearance generation is ported. Custom handlers are invoked normally.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_choice.py`: `set_value` now validates selections against `/Opt` when options exist, rejects multiple selected values unless `/MultiSelect` is set, and synchronizes `/I` selected option indices. Editable combo boxes still accept free-text values that are absent from `/Opt`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_text_field.py` + `pd_combo_box.py`: upstream-shaped `construct_appearances()` regenerates widget appearances through `PDAppearanceGenerator`, matching PDFBox's `AppearanceGeneratorHelper` path. `PDButton.construct_appearances()` mirrors upstream by syncing `/AS` against existing `/AP /N` states only; `PDPushButton.construct_appearances()` and `PDSignatureField.construct_appearances()` intentionally do not synthesize appearances, matching upstream's TODO/no-op behavior.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_signature_field.py`: fresh construction now mirrors upstream by auto-generating a unique `SignatureN` partial name from existing signature fields and marking the merged widget annotation printed + locked.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_catalog.py`: `get_output_intents()` returns `list[PDOutputIntent]` (was `NotImplementedError` stub); `add_output_intent(intent)` appends to `/OutputIntents` array.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_form_field_additional_actions.py` + `pd_annotation_additional_actions.py`: typed `/AA` wrappers exposing the K/F/V/C (form field) and E/X/D/U/Fo/Bl/PO/PC/PV/PI (annotation) trigger accessors. `PDAnnotationWidget.get_actions/set_actions` and the new `PDField.get_actions/set_actions` now return/accept `PDFormFieldAdditionalActions` (was raw COSDictionary).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_sound.py` + `pd_action_movie.py` + `pd_action_rendition.py` + `pd_action_transition.py` + `pd_action_embedded_go_to.py`: typed PDAction subtypes for /Sound, /Movie, /Rendition, /Trans, /GoToE. `PDActionSound.get_sound/set_sound` round-trips through `PDSoundStream` (new `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/sound/pd_sound_stream.py`; setter still accepts raw COSBase for back-compat). `PDActionTransition.get_trans/set_trans` round-trips through `PDTransition`. `PDActionEmbeddedGoTo.get_file/set_file` round-trips through `PDFileSpecification.create_fs` and `get_d/set_d` through `PDDestination.create`. `PDActionRendition.get_annotation/set_annotation` round-trips `/AN` through `PDAnnotation.create` (Screen-subtype falls back to `PDAnnotationUnknown` until a typed `PDAnnotationScreen` lands), and `get_rendition/set_rendition` round-trips `/R` through `PDRendition.create`; raw `get_an/set_an` and `get_r/set_r` accessors retained for back-compat. Deferred typed wrappers (returned as raw COS): PDAnnotationMovie (`/Annotation`), PDTargetDirectory (`/T`).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_border_style_dictionary.py`: typed `/BS`. `/D` (line dash pattern) returns raw `COSArray` until `PDLineDashPattern` (graphics cluster) lands. Wired into `PDAnnotationLink`, `PDAnnotationWidget`, `PDAnnotationSquareCircle` `get_border_style/set_border_style`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_appearance_characteristics_dictionary.py`: typed `/MK`. `/BC`/`/BG` colours return raw `COSArray` (typed `PDColor` deferred). `/I`/`/RI`/`/IX` icons return raw `COSStream` (typed `PDFormXObject` deferred). Wired into `PDAnnotationWidget.get_appearance_characteristics/set_appearance_characteristics`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_appearance_dictionary.py` + `pd_appearance_entry.py` + `pd_appearance_stream.py`: typed `/AP` plus dual-form `/N`/`/R`/`/D` entries (single stream OR state→stream dict). `PDAppearanceStream` does NOT yet extend `PDFormXObject` (rendering cluster). Added `PDAnnotation.get_appearance_dictionary/set_appearance_dictionary` for `/AP`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_line.py` + `pd_annotation_free_text.py`: Line + FreeText annotations. Deferred per-subtype: `/LLO`, callout-line `/CL` geometry, FreeText `/LE`, BS/BE styling, measurement intents.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_file_attachment.py` + `pd_annotation_rubber_stamp.py` + `pd_annotation_popup.py`: FileAttachment (`/FS` typed via `PDFileSpecification.create_fs`), RubberStamp/Stamp, Popup. Popup `/Parent` returns raw COSBase (typed PDAnnotationMarkup parent deferred to avoid circular imports).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_markup.py` + `pd_annotation_text_markup.py` + 8 concrete markup subtypes (`pd_annotation_highlight.py`, `pd_annotation_underline.py`, `pd_annotation_strikeout.py`, `pd_annotation_squiggly.py`, `pd_annotation_caret.py`, `pd_annotation_ink.py`, `pd_annotation_polygon.py`, `pd_annotation_polyline.py`): markup base + typed text-markup intermediate exposing `/QuadPoints`. `PDAnnotationMarkup.get_in_reply_to()` returns raw COSBase (avoids recursive factory dispatch). Per-subtype deferred: `/Popup`, `/RC` rich contents, `/IC` interior color, `/BS`, measure dictionary, custom appearance handlers.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_document_catalog_additional_actions.py`: catalog `/AA` typed wrapper exposing WC/WS/DS/WP/DP triggers. Wired into `PDDocumentCatalog.get_actions/set_actions`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pd_metadata.py`: typed catalog `/Metadata` wrapper extending `PDStream`. Multi-arg `__init__` dispatches None/COSStream/bytes/str/PDDocument-like. `get_metadata_as_string()` is the bridge to xmpbox; no `XMPMetadata`-returning accessor yet. `PDDocumentCatalog.get_metadata/set_metadata` wired (was the last `NotImplementedError` stub).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_color.py` + `pd_color_space.py` + `pd_device_color_space.py` + `pd_device_gray.py` + `pd_device_rgb.py` + `pd_device_cmyk.py`: foundational color model. Each device color space exposes `INSTANCE` singleton. Deferred: `PDColorSpace.create()` factory, `to_rgb`/`to_rgb_image` rendering conversion, `PDDeviceN`, `PDPattern`, `PDIndexed`, `PDSeparation`, `PDICCBased`, `PDLab`, `PDCalGray`, `PDCalRGB`, default-color-space lookup.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_target_directory.py`: typed `/T` target dictionary for `PDActionEmbeddedGoTo`. Per PDF 32000-1 Table 202: `get_target_filename/set_target_filename` access `/N` (embedded-file name in target catalog `/EmbeddedFiles`); `get_page_number/set_page_number` access `/P` integer page-index form; `get_named_destination/set_named_destination` access `/P` named-destination string form (`/P` may legally carry either type).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/*`: scaffold port of `PDFont` (abstract) + `PDSimpleFont` (intermediate) + `PDType1Font` + `PDTrueTypeFont` + `PDType0Font` + `PDFontDescriptor` + `PDFontFactory`. Lite — actual font program parsing (PFB/TTF/CFF/OpenType), encoding lookup, glyph metrics, character mapping, `PDCIDFont` family, `PDType3Font`/`PDMMType1Font`/`PDType1CFont`, `getFontMatrix`/`getDisplacement`/`isVertical`, Standard 14 AFM, and font subsetting are deferred.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/pd_line_dash_pattern.py`: typed `/D` dash pattern. Wired into `PDBorderStyleDictionary.get/set_dash_style` and `PDExtendedGraphicsState.get/set_line_dash_pattern` (both setters accept either typed wrapper or raw `COSArray` for backwards compat). Phase accepts `float` (upstream uses `int`).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/state/pd_extended_graphics_state.py`: typed `/ExtGState` wrapper exposing /LW /LC /LJ /ML /D /RI /CA /ca /BM /SMask(raw) /AIS /TK /SA /OP /op /OPM /SM /FL accessors. `/Font` exposes only `get_font_size` helper (full `PDFontSetting` deferred). `/SMask`/`/TR`/`/TR2`/`copy_into_graphics_state` deferred. `/BM` blend mode raw `COSName | str` (typed `BlendMode` enum deferred).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_xfa_resource.py`: typed `/XFA` wrapper. `is_dynamic()` (upstream has no such method) inspects the parsed XFA payload via stdlib `xml.etree.ElementTree`, locates the `<template>` packet and its first `<subform>` child (namespaced or not), and returns `True` when the `layout` attribute is set and not `"position"`; falls back to a substring heuristic (`<xfa:datasets`, `<xdp:xdp`, `subform name="form1"`) on malformed XML or missing template/subform. Result is cached on the instance. `get_document()` returns a stdlib `xml.etree.ElementTree.Element` (root) instead of upstream's W3C `org.w3c.dom.Document`; result is cached on the instance and parsing is lazy. Added `get_document_as_xml()` returning the UTF-8-decoded payload. `PDAcroForm.xfa()` returns the typed wrapper.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/*`: lite ports of `PDSignature`, `PDSeedValue`, `PDSignatureLock`. `PDSignatureField.get_signature/set_value/get_seed_value/set_seed_value/get_lock/set_lock` now return/accept typed wrappers (or raw `COSDictionary` for backwards compat). Actual signing/PKCS#7/timestamp generation deferred.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/pd_property_list.py` + `pd_optional_content_membership_dictionary.py`: `PDPropertyList` abstract base + `PDOCMD`. `PDOptionalContentGroup` now extends `PDPropertyList` (was: didn't, called out in earlier wave). `PDPropertyList.create()` returns `None` for unknown `/Type` (upstream returns a bare `PDPropertyList`). `/VE` visibility-expression tree parsing deferred per upstream.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_pattern.py` + `pd_indexed.py` + `pd_separation.py` + `pd_device_n.py` + `pd_icc_based.py` + `pd_cal_gray.py` + `pd_cal_rgb.py` + `pd_lab.py`: 8 new color spaces extending `PDColorSpace`. Plus `PDColorSpace.create()` static factory dispatching on `COSName` / `COSArray`. ICC profile parsing/embedding, `to_rgb` conversion, pattern/tint-transform evaluation, gamut mapping deferred. `PDIndexed` lookup table now consumes the `/Filter` chain via `COSStream.create_input_stream` when `/Lookup` is a stream, returning decoded palette bytes; raw `COSString` lookups pass through unchanged. Output length is clamped to `(hival + 1) * base_components` (truncate-or-zero-pad) per upstream's lenient handling.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_icc_based.py` + `pd_separation.py` + `pd_device_n.py` + `pd_pattern.py` + `pd_color.py`: `to_rgb(components)` added on each color space; `PDColor.to_rgb` now delegates for ICCBased/Separation/DeviceN/Pattern. `PDICCBased` falls back to `/Alternate` (or one inferred from `/N` ∈ {1,3,4} → DeviceGray/DeviceRGB/DeviceCMYK) — embedded ICC profile parsing remains deferred (library-first per CLAUDE.md). `PDSeparation` and `PDDeviceN` evaluate the tint transform via `PDFunction.create(...).eval(...)` and forward to the alternate. `PDPattern.to_rgb` recurses into the underlying CS for uncolored tiling; colored patterns (no underlying) return `None` so `PDColor.to_rgb` raises `NotImplementedError` — full pattern/shading rendering belongs to the rendering module. `PDDeviceN` gains `get/set_tint_transform` accessors mirroring `PDSeparation` (upstream has both).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_structure_node.py` + `pd_attribute_object.py` + `revisions.py`: struct base + attribute object + Revisions[T] helper. `PDStructureElement` gains `/A` and `/C` typed accessors. Typed `PDAttributeObject` owner subclasses (`PDLayoutAttributeObject` etc.) deferred. `PDStructureTreeRoot` and `PDStructureElement` extend `PDStructureNode` — `/K` kid mechanics (`get_kids`/`set_kids`/`append_kid`/`remove_kid`) live on the base; subclasses keep `_root`/`_element` as backwards-compat aliases for the inherited `_dictionary`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/destination/pd_page_destination.py`: added `find_page_number()` + `retrieve_page_number()` returning the integer index when `/D[0]` is `COSInteger`; direct page dictionaries and indirect page objects now resolve by COS dictionary identity when a `PDDocument` or `PDPageTree` context is supplied. `get_page()` return type narrowed from `COSBase | None` to `COSDictionary | None`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_remote_go_to.py`: added `get_named_destination` / `set_named_destination` for the string-form `/D` named-destination case.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/filespecification/*`: lite ports of `PDFileSpecification`, `PDComplexFileSpecification`, `PDSimpleFileSpecification`, `PDEmbeddedFile`. `PDEmbeddedFile.get/set_creation_date/mod_date` use raw `COSString` PDF date strings (no `datetime` conversion until a cos date helper lands). `PDEmbeddedFile.set_check_sum` stores via `COSString` (no `setEmbeddedString` helper yet). `PDEmbeddedFile` constructor variants `(PDDocument, InputStream[, COSName filter])` collapsed into a single dispatching `__init__` mirroring our `PDStream` constructor pattern. Small private `_get/_set_embedded_int/_string` helpers live in `pd_embedded_file.py` because `COSDictionary` does not yet expose `getEmbeddedInt`/`getEmbeddedString` — promote later.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/optionalcontent/*`: lite ports of `PDOptionalContentGroup` + `PDOptionalContentProperties`. `get_render_state(destination)` accepts a string ("Print"/"View"/"Export") since upstream `RenderDestination` enum lives in `org.apache.pdfbox.rendering` (not yet ported). `BaseState`/`RenderState` enums collapsed to plain strings. `PDOptionalContentGroup` does not extend `PDPropertyList` (parent class not yet ported). `PDOptionalContentProperties.add_group` defensively sets `/Type /OCG` on the supplied dict (slight superset of upstream). `compute_visible_ocgs(destination=None)` resolves /D BaseState + /ON + /OFF to a set of `id(ocg)` ready for `PDOptionalContentMembershipDictionary.is_visible`; when `destination` ("View"/"Print"/"Export") is supplied, the /D /AS auto-state usage array (PDF 32000-1 §8.11.4.4 Table 102) is now applied as a final pass — for each /AS entry whose /Event matches the destination, each OCG's /Usage/<category>/<Event>State is consulted in spec /Category order (first non-"Unchanged" wins) and the visible set is updated ("ON" adds, "OFF" discards, "Unchanged" leaves prior decision). "Unchanged" /D /BaseState is still treated as "ON" baseline at first call (no per-session state preserved).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/pagenavigation/*`: lite port of `PDTransition` plus `PDTransitionStyle`/`Motion`/`Dimension`/`Direction` as plain classes with constants instead of `enum.Enum`, mirroring `PDActionXxx.SUB_TYPE` pattern. `get_direction()` returns `int` with `-1` sentinel for `/None` rather than the raw `COSBase`. Upstream `setFlyAreaOpaque(boolean)` is exposed as `set_fly_area_to_show(b)` (key `/B` unchanged) per local naming.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/*`: scaffold port of `PDAcroForm`, `PDField`, `PDNonTerminalField`, `PDTerminalField`, `PDFieldFactory`, plus a generic `PDFieldStub` returned for all terminal fields until typed subclasses land. **Deferred upstream surface:** `PDAcroForm.flatten`, `refresh_appearances`, `import_fdf`/`export_fdf`, `get/set_default_resources`, `get/set_default_appearance`, `get/set_q`, `get/set_calc_order`, `get/set_scripting_handler`, `get_field_iterator`/`get_field_tree` (`PDFieldTree` not ported — recursive walk inlined in `get_field`), `set_cache_fields`/`is_caching_fields`, typed `PDXFAResource` (`xfa()` returns raw COS); `PDField.get/set_value`/`get_value_as_string`, typed `PDFormFieldAdditionalActions` (`/AA`), per-field `export_fdf`; `PDNonTerminalField.get_value/get_default_value` inheritance helpers; `PDTerminalField.set_actions/set_widgets/apply_change/construct_appearances/import_fdf/export_fdf` plus `PDAnnotationWidget` typing (`get_widgets()` returns raw `COSDictionary` list); `PDFieldFactory` per-`/FT` dispatch (Tx/Btn/Ch/Sig) — all terminal fields currently return `PDFieldStub`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/*`: ships base/factory plus GoTo, URI, Named, Launch, RemoteGoTo, JavaScript, SubmitForm, ResetForm, ImportData, Hide, Thread, and Unknown wrappers. SubmitForm/ResetForm/ImportData/Hide/Thread expose raw COS entries where upstream depends on deferred wrappers such as file specifications, destinations, or article beads. Richer actions (Sound, Movie, Rendition, Trans, GoToE) are deferred and currently preserve as `PDActionUnknown`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_page_additional_actions.py`: ships page-open `/O` and page-close `/C` triggers. Other additional-actions dictionaries for annotations/forms are deferred to their owning clusters.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_catalog.py`: `get_dests()` returns the lightweight `PDDestinationNameTreeNode` wrapper for `/Dests` dictionaries.

## Wave 7 — fonts, encoding, patterns, shading, taggedpdf, content stream writer

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/standard14_fonts.py`: 14 base fonts + ~30 aliases. `get_average_widths` returns 256-element flat table (600 monospace, 500 others). Per-glyph AFM widths + kerning deferred to AFM-bundling cluster. **(Superseded — see "Standard 14 AFM bundling" below.)**
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/encoding/*`: Encoding (abstract) + DictionaryEncoding + 6 predefined singletons. 256-entry tables imported from existing `pypdfbox.fontbox.encoding._TABLE` constants (byte-identical to upstream).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/pattern/*`: PDAbstractPattern + PDTilingPattern (type 1) + PDShadingPattern (type 2). PDAbstractPattern.create() factory dispatches on /PatternType.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/shading/*`: PDShading abstract base + 7 shading types. Mesh-data decoding for types 4-7, function evaluation, AWT bridges deferred (rendering cluster).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/taggedpdf/*`: 7 typed PDAttributeObject subclasses (PDStandardAttributeObject base + Layout/List/PrintField/Table/ExportFormat/User). PDAttributeObject.create() factory wired to dispatch on /O. PDUserAttributeObject exposes /P entries as plain dicts (`{N,V,F,H}`) instead of upstream's PDUserProperty wrapper.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_structure_tree_root.py` + `pd_structure_element.py`: now properly extend PDStructureNode (deferred from wave 6). PDStructureTreeRoot.get_kids() returns `[]` instead of `None` when /K absent (matches upstream contract).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_target_directory.py`: spec deviation fixed. `/N` accessors renamed to `get_target_filename/set_target_filename`. New `get_named_destination/set_named_destination` accesses `/P` string form (per Table 202).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_content_stream.py`: high-level user-facing drawing API. Path/text/color/graphics-state/XObject operators. Auto-allocates resource keys (F0/Im0/Form0). Supports AppendMode-style overwrite/append/prepend and optional FlateDecode compression on close. Deferred: actual font.encode (uses Latin-1/UTF-16BE fallback), bytes-level show_text, strict graphics-state stacking, BMC/BDC/EMC.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_stream.py`: replaced filter NotImplementedError stubs. `create_input_stream(stop_filters=None)` walks /Filter chain through FilterFactory. `create_output_stream(filters=None)` returns encoding stream for chained filters. `to_byte_array()` / `to_raw_byte_array()` / `set_data(data, filters)`. Encryption-aware streams deferred. Encode-side predictor now wired through `pypdfbox.filter._predictor` (PNG 10-15, TIFF 2).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pd_stream.py`: refactored to delegate to COSStream. Added get/set_decode_parms, get/set_metadata, broadened get_length to int|None.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_information.py`: get_metadata_keys() now returns sorted `list[str]` (was `set[str]`).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_labels.py`: STYLE_* constants, get_label_for_page(index), get_label_ranges(), set_label_range, to_roman/to_letters helpers.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/*`: lite operator dispatch scaffold — OperatorProcessor abstract base + OperatorRegistry + 13 base no-op handlers (Tj/TJ/'/"/Tf/Td/TD/Tm/q/Q/m/l). Real semantics live in engine-coupled handlers (rendering / text-extraction clusters).

## fontbox CMap cluster

- `pypdfbox/fontbox/cmap/cmap_parser.py`: predefined CMap loading currently supports only programmatic `Identity-H` and `Identity-V`; file-backed predefined CMaps such as `Adobe-Japan1-UCS2` are deferred.

## fontbox TrueType font program + PDTrueTypeFont width lookup

- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/true_type_font.py`: SFNT/TTF/OTF parsing is delegated to the (MIT-licensed) `fontTools.ttLib` library instead of the original hand-rolled directory walker, per the project's library-first rule for generic font/format concerns. The PDFBox-faithful accessor surface (`get_units_per_em`, `get_number_of_glyphs`, `get_advance_width`, `get_unicode_cmap_subtable`, `get_header` / `get_horizontal_header` / `get_maximum_profile` / `get_horizontal_metrics`, `get_table_map`) is preserved unchanged, and the existing typed-table classes (`HeaderTable`, `HorizontalHeaderTable`, `HorizontalMetricsTable`, `MaximumProfileTable`) are still returned, populated from fontTools' parse output. fontTools is imported lazily on first TTF construction so callers that never touch a TTF stream don't pay its import cost. Convenience attribute-style accessors `unitsPerEm` / `numGlyphs` / `advance_widths` were added to expose the same data without a getter call. Glyph outlines (`glyf`/`loca`), GSUB / GPOS, kerning, name-table accessors, and the full `TTFParser` / `TrueTypeCollection` surface are still deferred.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_true_type_font.py`: `get_glyph_width(code) -> float` now resolves widths in PDF spec §9.7.3 order — `/Widths` (within `[FirstChar, LastChar]`) wins, otherwise the embedded `/FontFile2` is parsed and its `hmtx` advance is scaled by `1000 / unitsPerEm`. Returns `0.0` when neither source is available. CIDToGIDMap and richer Type1-style fallbacks are deferred.

## tools cluster #1

- `pypdfbox/tools/merge.py`: cluster #1 performs naive page-list concatenation and does not remap cross-document references such as links, named destinations, structure-tree owners, or form resources. This is replaced by `PDFMergerUtility` semantics when the multipdf cluster lands.
- `pypdfbox/tools/split.py`: cluster #1 copies page COS dictionaries into fresh documents without remapping references to sibling pages or document-level structures.
- `pypdfbox/tools/decrypt.py`: cluster #1 is pass-through for unencrypted PDFs and returns non-zero for encrypted inputs; real security removal depends on pdmodel cluster #10.
- `pypdfbox/tools/version.py`: prints Python/runtime package metadata in addition to the upstream-style version string.

## pdmodel viewer preferences enrichment

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_viewer_preferences.py`: adds accessors not present in upstream PDFBox 3.0 — `pick_tray_by_pdf_size`/`set_pick_tray_by_pdf_size`, `get_num_copies`/`set_num_copies` (default 1), `get_print_page_range`/`set_print_page_range` (raw `COSArray` of int pairs), `get_enforce`/`set_enforce` (PDF 2.0). Covers PDF 32000-1 / 32000-2 Table 150 entries upstream omits.

## Wave 8 — fonts (CID, Type3/MMType1/Type1C), name trees, function family, MCR/OBJR, operators, enrichment

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_cid_font.py` + `pd_cid_font_type0.py` + `pd_cid_font_type2.py` + `pd_cid_system_info.py`: PDCIDFont abstract + Type0/Type2 + system info. Wired into `PDType0Font.get_descendant_font()` (was raw COSDictionary). CID width lookup via `/W` + `/DW` and Type2 `/CIDToGIDMap` byte interpretation are present; full TrueType font-program metrics are deferred.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_cid_font.py`: parses `/W` and `/W2` per PDF 32000-1 §9.7.4.3 — `get_widths()` (CID → width map), `get_glyph_width(cid)` (with `/DW` fallback), `get_default_width()`, `get_widths2()` (CID → (w1y, v_x, v_y) triples), `get_default_position_vector()` (defaults to spec `(880, -1000)`). Mirrors PDFBox `PDCIDFont.readWidths()` / `readVerticalDisplacements()` — same lenient interleaved-form parsing, same lazy caching.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type3_font.py` + `pd_mm_type1_font.py` + `pd_type1c_font.py`: remaining font subtypes. PDFontFactory now dispatches Type3 + MMType1. Type1C still routes to PDType1Font from factory because /Subtype is /Type1 — auto-dispatch from /FontDescriptor /FontFile3 /Subtype /Type1C deferred.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_font_factory.py`: dispatch now inspects `/FontDescriptor /FontFile3 /Subtype` so `/Type1` with a Type1C-marked FontFile3 routes to `PDType1CFont`, and `/CIDFontType0` with a `CIDFontType0C`-marked FontFile3 routes to `PDCIDFontType0` (previously the factory returned `None` and Type1C was reachable only via direct construction). Plain `/Type1` (no FontFile3, or FontFile3 of `/Subtype /OpenType` etc.) still returns `PDType1Font`; bare `/CIDFontType0` without the CFF marker still returns `None` (reached via the Type0 descendant path). Closes the deferred dispatch noted in the "Type 1 / CFF font program parsing" section below.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/*`: PDFunction abstract + Type0/Type2/Type3/Type4. PDFunction.create() factory dispatches on /FunctionType. Numeric `eval()`, Type 4 PostScript instruction parsing, Type 0 sampled-table decoding deferred.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_pages_name_tree_node.py` + `pd_templates_name_tree_node.py` + `pd_ids_name_tree_node.py` + `pd_urls_name_tree_node.py` + `pd_alternate_presentations_name_tree_node.py` + `pd_renditions_name_tree_node.py`: 6 typed catalog `/Names` sub-trees. Wired into PDDocumentNameDictionary (was deferred). PDIDSNameTreeNode leaf type is `bytes` (deviates from upstream `String`).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/outline/pd_outline_item.py`: enrichment — FLAG_ITALIC/FLAG_BOLD constants, get/set_text_color (RGB tuple or None), get/set_text_flags + is_italic/is_bold, get/set_structure_element (raw COSDictionary; typed PDStructureElement deferred to avoid circular import), get/set_count + is_collapsed, find_destination_page(document) resolver.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_viewer_preferences.py`: enrichment — pick_tray_by_pdf_size, get/set_num_copies, get/set_print_page_range, get/set_enforce. (Already documented in earlier section.)
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/*`: 41 more no-op operator stubs (path c/v/y/h/re/S/s/f/f*/F/B/b/B*/b*/n/W/W*, text-state Tr/Ts/Tc/Tw/Tz/TL/T*, color CS/cs/SC/SCN/sc/scn/G/g/RG/rg/K/k, marked-content BMC/BDC/EMC/MP/DP). Default registry now exposes 53 operators (12 prior + 41 new).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/filespecification/pd_embedded_file.py`: enrichment — datetime conversion for /CreationDate /ModDate (was raw COSString), checksum bytes (with hex-form encoding), size as int|None (was -1 sentinel), creator accessor, mac_subtype/mac_creator, mac_resource_fork as COSStream (was string).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_marked_content_reference.py` + `pd_object_reference.py`: PDMarkedContentReference (/MCR) + PDObjectReference (/OBJR) typed kid wrappers. PDStructureNode.wrap_kid() static helper auto-dispatches /K entries based on /Type (StructElem → PDStructureElement, MCR → PDMarkedContentReference, OBJR → PDObjectReference, COSInteger → MCID int).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_label_range.py`: enrichment — start_index field, set_style validates against STYLE_* constants, compute_label_for_offset(offset) renders label using existing to_roman/to_letters helpers. PDPageLabels.get_label_ranges() now returns `list[PDPageLabelRange]` (was list of dicts).

## Encryption integration wiring (cluster #10)

- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_stream.py`: added `set_security_handler(handler, obj_num, gen_num)` and an encryption-aware decode path in `create_input_stream`. When a handler is attached, raw bytes are decrypted in-place before the `/Filter` chain runs; a `_decrypted` flag prevents double-undo. Mirrors the upstream `COSStream` decryption hook.
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py`: added `get_encryption_dictionary()` and `get_document_id()` accessors for the trailer-level `/Encrypt` and `/ID[0]` entries — needed by `PDDocument.decrypt` for file-encryption-key derivation.
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py`: added `set_password()`, `get_password()`, `get_security_handler()`, `has_encrypted_xref_streams()` for the early-decryption hook needed by encrypted xref-stream PDFs (PDF 1.5+). When a password is staged the parser instantiates a `StandardSecurityHandler` the moment the trailer + `/Encrypt` + `/ID` are visible — *before* xref-stream entries are decoded — so the cluster-#4 xref-stream decoder (when it lands) can decipher the body. The legacy lazy flow (no password staged → `PDDocument.decrypt` walks the pool retroactively) still works unchanged. Xref-stream *entry* decoding itself remains deferred to parser cluster #4; encrypted xref-stream parsing currently sets `has_encrypted_xref_streams() = True` and stages the handler before falling through to the cluster-#4 placeholder.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document.py`: `is_encrypted` (already present) joined by `decrypt(password)`, `protect(StandardProtectionPolicy)`, `get_encryption() → PDEncryption | None`, `set_encryption_dictionary`, `get_current_access_permission`. `decrypt` instantiates `StandardSecurityHandler`, runs `prepare_for_decryption`, then attaches the handler to every `COSStream` in the object pool. `protect` only accepts `StandardProtectionPolicy`; public-key handler dispatch raises `NotImplementedError` (deferred to the public-key cluster). `save()` honours `set_all_security_to_be_removed(True)` by forcing a decode pass on every loaded stream and stripping `/Encrypt` from the trailer before delegating to the writer.
- `pypdfbox/loader.py`: `Loader.load_pdf` accepts an optional `password` positional argument. When the parsed document carries `/Encrypt` and a password is supplied (empty string counts), a transient `PDDocument` wrapper invokes `decrypt(password)` before the `COSDocument` is returned. `PDDocument.load` mirrors the password parameter. Encrypted documents loaded without a password are returned encrypted — callers can wrap and call `decrypt` manually.

## Wave 9 — encryption cluster + typed wrappers + PDFunction.eval

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/pd_encryption.py` + `access_permission.py` + `protection_policy.py` + `standard_protection_policy.py`: PDEncryption (/Encrypt wrapper) + AccessPermission (permission flag wrapper, NOT COSDictionary-backed; wraps an int) + ProtectionPolicy (abstract) + StandardProtectionPolicy. AccessPermission constants exposed as 1-based bit *positions* for readability while the wrapped int stores conventional masks.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/security_handler.py` + `standard_security_handler.py` + `security_provider.py`: SecurityHandler abstract + StandardSecurityHandler covering revisions 2-6 (RC4-40, RC4-128, AES-128 CBC, AES-256, AES-256+SHA-384+PBKDF2) using the `cryptography` library. `is_aes()` keys off `/StmF` name (`AESV2` / `AESV3`); `/CF` crypt-filter sub-dictionary parsing deferred. Per-revision key-length validation (r2 must be 40, r3-r4 must be 40-128) deferred — trusts dictionary. PDInvalidPasswordException raised on no-match. Used `cryptography.hazmat.decrepit.ciphers.algorithms.ARC4` to silence deprecation.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/public_key_security_handler.py` + 3 companions: PublicKeySecurityHandler decrypt path using `cryptography.hazmat.primitives.serialization.pkcs7.pkcs7_decrypt_der`. `prepare_document` (encrypt path) raises NotImplementedError — full CMS envelope construction deferred.
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_stream.py`: encryption-aware `create_input_stream` decrypts raw bytes via attached SecurityHandler before running the /Filter chain. New `set_security_handler(handler, obj_num, gen_num)` setter.
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py`: added `get_encryption_dictionary()` and `get_document_id()` accessors over the trailer.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document.py`: `is_encrypted()`, `decrypt(password)`, `protect(StandardProtectionPolicy)`, `get_current_access_permission()`, `set_all_security_to_be_removed(b)`. `save()` honors strip-on-save by decoding streams + dropping /Encrypt.
- `pypdfbox/loader.py`: `Loader.load_pdf(source, password=None)` — auto-decrypts when document is encrypted and password is supplied.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/pd_signature.py`: `verify(document_bytes) -> SignatureValidationResult` extracts signer cert via `cryptography.pkcs7.load_der_pkcs7_certificates`. **Returns `is_valid=False` with a deferred-feature error** because cryptography's `pkcs7` module exposes only signing builders; full SignedData chain validation needs `asn1crypto` (deferred).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_ink_list.py` + `pd_path_info.py` + `pd_line_info.py` + `pd_vertices.py`: typed wrappers for /InkList, /Vertices, /L geometry. PDAnnotationInk.get_ink_list now returns PDInkList (was raw COSArray); polygon/polyline get_vertices kept returning `list[float]` for backwards compat — typed PDVertices is exported separately.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/`: PDFunction.eval(input) abstract + PDFunctionType2.eval (exponential interpolation per §7.10.3) + PDFunctionType3.eval (stitching per §7.10.4). Plus clip_input / clip_output / get_ranges_for_inputs / get_ranges_for_outputs helpers. Type 0 sampled-table eval and Type 4 PostScript eval deferred.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/{imagecontent,graphics}/*` + `state/{set_dash_pattern,set_flatness,set_rendering_intent,set_graphics_state_parameters}.py`: 9 more no-op operator handler stubs (BI, ID, EI, Do, cm, d, i, ri, gs). Default registry now exposes 62 handlers.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/taggedpdf/pd_four_colours.py` + helpers in pd_standard_attribute_object.py: PDFourColours typed wrapper (4-side color array for /BorderColor etc.). PDLayoutAttributeObject get_background_color/get_color now return `tuple[float, ...]` (was raw COSArray); new get_border_color returns PDFourColours.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_embedded_go_to.py`: `walk_to_target() -> list[TargetStep]` walks the chained /T target dictionaries. TargetStep dataclass exposes (relationship, target_filename, page_number, named_destination, annotation_number). Cycle detection deferred.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_embedded_go_to.py`: `resolve_target(source_document, target_document=None) -> tuple[PDDocument, PDPageDestination | PDPage] | None` walks the /T chain through /Names /EmbeddedFiles, opens each embedded file as a fresh PDDocument, and resolves the action's /D against the final scope's /Names /Dests name tree. /R="P" steps pop to the supplied target_document; missing /N or unreadable embedded bytes return None gracefully (no raise).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_remote_go_to.py`: `get_destination()` typed dispatch — returns PDDestination for COSArray /D, str for COSString/COSName /D, None when absent.

## /CF crypt-filter dispatch

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/pd_crypt_filter_dictionary.py` (NEW): typed `PDCryptFilterDictionary` wrapper. Fresh instances are tagged `/Type /CryptFilter`; wrapping a parsed dictionary leaves entries untouched. `/Length` reads in **bytes** (default 5 = 40-bit RC4) per §7.6.5 Table 25 — note this differs from `PDEncryption.get_length()` which reports bits.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/pd_encryption.py`: added `/CF` dispatch — `get_std_crypt_filter_dictionary` / `set_std_crypt_filter_dictionary`, `get_default_crypt_filter_dictionary` / `set_default_crypt_filter_dictionary`, `get_crypt_filter_dictionary(name)` / `set_crypt_filter_dictionary(name, dict)`, `remove_v45_filters` (strips /CF /StmF /StrF /EFF for downgrade to V<=3). Crypt-filter entries are stored as direct objects per PDFBOX-4436.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/standard_security_handler.py`: `is_aes()` for V=4 now resolves through `/CF/<StmF>/CFM` first (authoritative per spec), falling back to the legacy `/StmF`-name heuristic only when `/CF` is absent — fixes detection on documents that use a custom crypt-filter name. Added `get_stream_filter_name(encryption)` / `get_string_filter_name(encryption)` static helpers.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/pd_encryption.py`: added `get_eff()` / `set_eff()` accessors for the `/EFF` (default embedded-file crypt-filter name) entry — needed by per-object dispatch so embedded files can pick a different cipher than ordinary streams (PDF 32000-1 §7.6.5).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/standard_security_handler.py`: per-object crypt-filter dispatch — `prepare_for_decryption` and `prepare_document` now resolve `/StmF`, `/StrF` and `/EFF` through `/CF` at init time and cache the resulting `/CFM` per slot. `decrypt_string` / `encrypt_string` / `decrypt_stream` / `encrypt_stream` (the last two grew an `is_embedded_file=False` flag) dispatch to RC4 (`V2`), AES-128-CBC (`AESV2`), AES-256-CBC (`AESV3`) or pass-through (`Identity`/`None`) according to the cached routing table. For V<4 documents the routing table stays empty and the legacy single-algorithm path inherited from `SecurityHandler` runs unchanged. Write side: `prepare_document` now installs `/CF/StdCF` + `/StmF` + `/StrF` for V=4 and V=5 outputs so the read side rebuilds the same routing table on reload. `/EFF` is intentionally left absent on writes so embedded files inherit `/StmF` per the spec default.

## Public-key encrypt path

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/public_key_security_handler.py`: `prepare_document` now wires the encrypt side. Generates a 20-byte random seed, builds a one-recipient PKCS#7 envelope per `PublicKeyRecipient` via `cryptography.hazmat.primitives.serialization.pkcs7.PKCS7EnvelopeBuilder` (AES-128 / `adbe.pkcs7.s4` for 128-bit policies, AES-256 / `adbe.pkcs7.s5` for 256-bit), serialises the envelopes as DER, populates `/Encrypt` (`/Filter /Adobe.PubSec`, `/SubFilter`, `/V`, `/R`, `/Length`, `/Recipients`, `/CF /DefaultCryptFilter` + `/StmF` + `/StrF`), and derives the file key per §7.6.5 (SHA-256 for V>=5, SHA-1 for V=4) so the existing per-object cipher dispatch works straight away. Constructor accepts an optional `protection_policy` mirroring `StandardSecurityHandler`. Deferred: per-recipient algorithm negotiation, the `/AdbeRecipientInfo` extension that lets one envelope carry many recipients, and multi-recipient policies whose recipients have *different* permission flags (the spec wants one envelope per distinct permission set; we currently emit one envelope per recipient regardless).

## PDFunctionType4 PostScript eval

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/pd_function_type4.py`: `eval(input)` now ships per PDF 32000-1 §7.10.5. Body bytes are read through `COSStream.create_input_stream` (so `/Filter` chains decode), tokenised whitespace+brace, parsed into a nested instruction sequence (each `{...}` block becomes a Python `list`), and run through a minimal stack machine. Operator coverage: arithmetic (add/sub/mul/div/idiv/mod/neg/abs/ceiling/floor/round/truncate/sqrt/sin/cos/atan/exp/ln/log/cvi/cvr), stack (dup/exch/pop/copy/index/roll), boolean (eq/ne/lt/le/gt/ge/and/or/xor/not/bitshift/true/false), conditional (if/ifelse). `def`, `forall`, `for`, dictionaries, and other operators not allowed in Type 4 are intentionally rejected (raise `OSError`). Numeric stability uses Python `float`; booleans live on the same stack as numbers per spec and are coerced to `1.0`/`0.0` on the way out for `/Range` clipping. Stack underflow / type mismatch / unknown operator all surface as `OSError` (mirrors upstream `IOException`). Deferred: instruction-sequence caching (we re-parse on every `eval` call), richer error-recovery semantics, and cross-checking numeric edge cases against Java's IEEE-754 single-precision rounding.

## PDResourceCache + PDDocument resource_cache wiring

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_resource_cache.py` (NEW): abstract `PDResourceCache` (port of upstream `ResourceCache`) plus concrete `DefaultResourceCache` (port of upstream `DefaultResourceCache`). Per-category dicts keyed by indirect `COSObject` ref, identity-cached so repeat lookups round-trip the same wrapper. **Eviction differs from upstream**: PDFBox uses `SoftReference`-keyed maps that the JVM can reclaim under memory pressure; we hold strong refs and expose an explicit `clear()` instead. Subclass and override the `put_*` methods if a workload needs LRU/soft-ref semantics. The `DefaultResourceCache(enable_stable_cache=True)` constructor flag and `MAX_REMOVALS = 3` class constant are exposed for API parity, and `is_stable_cache_enabled()` reads the flag back; the stable-cache "ignore removals after N attempts" behaviour itself is a no-op until the SoftReference eviction path is implemented (see eviction note above).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document.py`: `get_resource_cache()` now lazily allocates a `DefaultResourceCache` on first call (was `NotImplementedError`). `set_resource_cache(cache)` stores the supplied cache and accepts `None` to disable caching (a subsequent `get_resource_cache` re-allocates a fresh default). `add_signature(...)` shipped in the digitalsignature write-side pipeline (see "PDSignature write-side pipeline" below) — it now stages a `PDSignature` + `SignatureInterface` for the next `save_incremental` call and only raises `TypeError` when the first arg isn't a `PDSignature`. `register_true_type_font_for_closing(font)` becomes a no-op append onto an internal `_fonts_to_close` list — Python GC handles TTF lifetimes, so we don't drive teardown; the list is preserved so future font-subsetting work has a registration log to drain.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_resources.py`: typed indirect resource lookups now consult the document resource cache for fonts, XObjects, color spaces, patterns, shadings, graphics states, and property lists. Direct `get_font()` entries and raw `get_xobject()` still return dereferenced COS entries.

## PDStructureElement page wiring + role-map resolution

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_structure_element.py`: `get_page()` / `set_page(page)` now ship — `/Pg` round-trips through a typed `PDPage` (set accepts a `PDPage` or raw `COSDictionary`; `None` removes the entry). `get_standard_structure_type()` walks the `/P` parent chain to the `StructTreeRoot`, reads its `/RoleMap`, and follows the chain (default → mapped → mapped → ...) until a fixed point. Cycles are bounded by both a `seen` set and a depth cap of 16 hops (mirrors upstream's role-map ceiling and protects against pathological PDFs); the parent walk is similarly capped against malformed cyclic `/P`. Non-name `/RoleMap` values are skipped (cannot resolve to a standard structure type).

## PDFTextStripper — /Differences decode + width-based word spacing

- `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper.py`: added a typed-font lookup cache that resolves each `Tf` resource name through `PDFontFactory`. When the active font lacks a `/ToUnicode` CMap but is a `PDSimpleFont` (Type1/TrueType/Type3) with an `/Encoding` dictionary, show-text bytes are now decoded via `PDSimpleFont.decode` — which threads each byte through the typed `Encoding` (including `/Differences` overlays) and the Adobe Glyph List. Resolution order: `/ToUnicode` first (most authoritative), then `PDSimpleFont.decode`, then Latin-1 fallback. Mirrors upstream's `PDFont.toUnicode` / `PDSimpleFont.toUnicode` cascade.
- `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper.py`: per-character horizontal advance now derives from the active font's `/Widths` array when available — `_compute_avg_advance` converts `PDSimpleFont.get_average_font_width()` (thousandths of an em) to user-space units at the current `font_size`. Both the `_emit` cursor advance and `_format_positions` right-edge calculation share this metric, so the word-gap heuristic adapts to wide vs narrow fonts. Falls back to the legacy 0.5-em monospace estimate when the font has no usable `/Widths` (preserves the no-resources test case).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_simple_font.py`: added `get_average_font_width()` returning the arithmetic mean of non-zero `/Widths` entries in thousandths of an em. Skipping zero-width entries avoids dragging the mean toward zero on sparsely-mapped fonts (most slots are `.notdef = 0`). Mirrors upstream `PDSimpleFont.getAverageFontWidth`.

## tools/merge wave-13 upgrade — import_page + intra-source link remap

- `pypdfbox/tools/merge.py`: pages are now deep-copied via `PDDocument.import_page` instead of being re-parented in place. After each source's pages land in the target, the merger walks each new page's `/Annots` in lockstep with the source page's `/Annots`, and for every `/Subtype /Link` annotation rewrites `/Dest[0]` (and `/A` `/D[0]` when `/A` is a GoTo action) to the imported target page when the original `/D[0]` resolved to a same-source page that was also imported in this batch. Cross-source / out-of-batch references are left as-is (the link will dangle — preferable to silently rewriting it to the wrong page).
- `pypdfbox/tools/merge.py`: supported catalog `/Names` trees (`/Dests`, `/EmbeddedFiles`, `/JavaScript`) are merged into flat output name trees. Duplicate names are preserved by suffixing later entries as `#2`, `#3`, ...; Link annotations that target renamed named destinations are rewritten to the suffixed name. Full `PDFMergerUtility` reconciliation of forms, outlines, structure trees, and destination-module internals remains deferred.

## Encrypted xref-stream round-trip (wave-13 fix)

- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py::visit_from_stream`: cross-reference streams (`/Type /XRef`) are now exempted from the per-object encryption pass per ISO 32000-2 §7.6.2 ("All cross-reference streams in the file shall not be encrypted"). The dictionary block is also bracketed with `_in_encrypt_subtree=True` so the embedded `/ID` strings stay cleartext — required because the standard handler folds `/ID[0]` into the file-encryption-key derivation. Previously the writer emitted ciphertext xref-stream bodies, which the parser could not bootstrap (FlateDecode would see ciphertext before any handler was built). Tests: `tests/pdfwriter/test_xref_stream_output.py::test_xref_stream_body_stays_plaintext_when_handler_active` (renamed from `..._is_encrypted_when_handler_active`, inverted assertion to match the spec).
- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_stream.py`: added `set_skip_encryption(bool)` / `is_skip_encryption()` plus an auto-detect branch in `set_security_handler` that flips the skip flag when the stream's dict carries `/Type /XRef`. Closes the gap where the parser marks one xref-stream COSStream during `_handle_xref_stream_at` but a later lazy-loader materialises a different instance from disk — the auto-detect ensures the document-level `PDDocument.decrypt` walk doesn't garble it either way.
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py`: `_handle_xref_stream_at` now (a) marks the xref stream skip-encryption before any decode, (b) decodes the entry table BEFORE running the handler bootstrap (so `/Encrypt`'s xref entry is registered when `_resolve_dict_entry` looks it up), and (c) `_resolve_dict_entry` accepts `XrefType.STREAM` entries (uncompressed — they carry a real byte offset) so the eager bootstrap can resolve `/Encrypt` from a pure-xref-stream document. Previously the resolver only honoured `XrefType.TABLE`, which made the eager bootstrap dormant for every PDF 1.5+ document.
- `pypdfbox/loader.py::Loader.load_pdf`: stages the password on the parser via `parser.set_password(password)` before `parse()` runs. Required for documents whose xref *itself* lives in a stream — the security handler must be ready by the time the bootstrap reaches downstream indirect streams.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page.py::_stream_bytes`: switched from `create_raw_input_stream` to `create_input_stream` so the security handler decrypts and the `/Filter` chain (typically `/FlateDecode` for content streams emitted by our writer) is unwound before the bytes hit `PDFTextStripper`. Returning still-encrypted or still-compressed bytes here masked the bug above for traditional encrypted PDFs in earlier waves.
- `tests/integration/test_end_to_end.py::test_encrypt_and_xref_stream_combined_roundtrip`: removed the wave-12 `pytest.skip` — the parser can now re-decrypt encrypted xref streams, so the round-trip is asserted unconditionally.

## AcroForm field-value APIs

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_text_field.py`: `get_value` / `set_value` / `get_value_as_string` already shipped — `/V` is a `COSString`. `get_value` returns `""` (not `None`) when absent, matching upstream. Inheritance from `/Parent` is automatic via `PDField.get_inheritable_attribute` per PDF 32000-1 §12.7.4 (so a child with no own `/V` returns the parent's value).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_button.py`: `get_value` / `set_value` / `get_value_as_string` already shipped — `/V` is a `COSName` (the on-state name). Inherited unchanged by `PDCheckBox` and `PDRadioButton`. `PDPushButton` overrides the read side to return `""` per upstream (push buttons hold no value); `set_value` is intentionally not overridden so callers don't trip on no-op assignment.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_choice.py`: added `get_value_as_string` returning the comma-joined view of the multi-value list (mirrors upstream `PDChoice.getValueAsString`). `get_value` / `set_value` accept single-string or `list[str]` and auto-collapse to `COSString` for length-1 selections vs `COSArray` for multi-select.
