- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_signature_field.py`: added `get_value_as_string` returning `""` per upstream — signatures have no single textual representation; consumers wanting metadata should call `get_signature()` and inspect `/Name` / `/Reason` / `/Location`. Typed `PDSignature` wrapping for `get_value` already shipped; full `PDSignature.verify` cluster (signing + verification) remains deferred per PRD §6.10.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_non_terminal_field.py`: added `get_value` / `set_value` / `get_value_as_string`. `get_value` returns the raw `COSBase` of own `/V` per upstream (children inherit `/V` lazily through `PDField.get_inheritable_attribute`, so this is intentionally non-recursive — consumers needing an effective value should iterate `get_children()` and call `get_value` on each typed leaf). `get_value_as_string` returns the string form when `/V` is a `COSString` or `COSName`, else `""`.

## PDAcroForm.flatten

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_acro_form.py`: added `flatten(fields=None, refresh_appearances=False)` per PDF 32000-1 §12.7.5.5. Walks every terminal descendant of the requested fields (defaulting to the whole form), pulls each widget's `/AP /N` (honouring `/AS` when `/N` is a state subdictionary), registers it as a Form XObject under the host page's `/Resources /XObject` (collisions resolved by allocating fresh `Fm<n>` keys), and appends a `q a 0 0 d e f cm /<name> Do Q` snippet to the page's `/Contents` (single-stream `/Contents` is promoted to a 2-element array — no in-place stream rewrite). The CTM maps the form's transformed `/BBox` to the widget's `/Rect`; rotated/skewed `/Matrix` entries are approximated by the axis-aligned bounding box of the transformed corners (full upstream parity would emit a non-uniform CTM). Widgets without a usable `/AP /N` and without a resolvable host page are silently skipped (matches upstream's `hasValidAppearance` guard). Host page resolution prefers the widget's `/P` back-pointer and falls back to scanning every page's `/Annots` when absent. When `fields=None` the catalog's `/AcroForm` entry is removed; otherwise only the named fields are stripped from `/Fields`. `refresh_appearances=True` raises `NotImplementedError` (rebuilding `/AP /N` from `/V` requires per-`/FT` widget-appearance construction — deferred).

## PDSignature write-side pipeline

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document.py`: `add_signature(sig, signature_interface, options=None)` now ships. Accepts a typed `PDSignature` plus a `SignatureInterface` callback. Wires the signature dict into `/AcroForm /Fields` inside an invisible signature widget (`/T = "Signature{N}"`, `/Rect = [0 0 0 0]`, `/Subtype /Widget`, `/F = 132`), anchors the widget to the first page's `/Annots`, sets `/SigFlags = 3` (SignaturesExist | AppendOnly), and stages the signer for the next `save_incremental`. Defaults `/Filter Adobe.PPKLite` + `/SubFilter adbe.pkcs7.detached` when caller didn't set them. Does **not** create a new field name slot when one already exists — it picks the next free `Signature{N}`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document.py`: `save_incremental` now drives the signing pipeline when `add_signature(...)` has staged a pending signature. Pre-flight phase reserves a `/Contents <0×16384>` placeholder (8192 raw bytes, headroom for typical RSA-2048 PKCS#7 detached blobs + chain) and a `/ByteRange [0 9999999999 9999999999 9999999999]` placeholder, runs the writer into a `BytesIO`, locates the placeholder, computes the real `/ByteRange [0 X Y Z]` bracketing everything outside the hex `<…>` (the angle brackets themselves stay inside the hashed range per ISO 32000-1 §12.8.1), splices the real ByteRange in place (trailing-space pad keeps width identical), invokes `signature_interface.sign(io.BytesIO(bracketed_bytes))` to produce the DER PKCS#7 blob, and patches the hex-encoded blob into the `/Contents` slot (zero-pads to placeholder length). The bracketed-bytes math is `(X-0) + (Z-(Y-1)) = file_size - hex_placeholder_len`. Final bytes are drained to the user-supplied `target` (path / `BinaryIO` / `RandomAccessWrite`).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document.py`: `save_incremental_for_external_signing(output) -> ExternalSigningSupport` runs the same pipeline minus the `signature_interface.sign` call. Returns an `ExternalSigningSupport` handle exposing `get_content() -> bytes` (the bracketed bytes the caller hashes + signs, e.g. via an HSM) and `set_signature(pkcs7_der: bytes) -> None` (splices the blob in, drains to `output`). `add_signature` may be called with `signature_interface=None` to use this path.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document.py`: new `ExternalSigningSupport` helper class (no upstream-specific equivalent in pypdfbox — the upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.interactive.digitalsignature.ExternalSigningSupport` is mirrored here as a small dataclass-ish shim).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/signature_interface.py` (NEW): abstract `SignatureInterface.sign(content) -> bytes` callback contract — port of upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.interactive.digitalsignature.SignatureInterface`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/pkcs7_signature.py` (NEW): concrete `Pkcs7Signature(SignatureInterface)` wrapping `cryptography.hazmat.primitives.serialization.pkcs7.PKCS7SignatureBuilder`. Defaults to SHA-256 and emits `[PKCS7Options.DetachedSignature, PKCS7Options.Binary]` so the document bytes stay OUT of the SignedData blob (required for PDF signing per ISO 32000-1 §12.8.3.3) and SMIME-style CRLF rewriting is suppressed. Library-first per CLAUDE.md — no ASN.1 hand-rolling, PyCA wraps OpenSSL.
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: new `allow_signing_placeholders=False` constructor flag. When `True`, the safety guard that normally rejects re-saving a source-side signature with a `[0 0 0 0]` ByteRange placeholder (`_reject_signed_with_byterange_placeholder`) is bypassed. `PDDocument`'s signing pipeline sets this because it owns the placeholder + post-write splice; everyone else stays protected against accidentally invalidating an existing signature.

## Type 1 / CFF font program parsing — fontTools-backed

- `pypdfbox/fontbox/type1/type1_font.py` (NEW): thin wrapper over `fontTools.t1Lib.T1Font`. Exposes `Type1Font.from_bytes(raw)` (PDF `/FontFile` stream form — cleartext header + binary eexec + trailing zeros, NOT PFB-wrapped), `units_per_em` (derived as `1 / FontMatrix[0]`), `font_matrix`, `has_glyph(name)`, `get_width(name)` (forces a `.draw()` against `fontTools.pens.basePen.NullPen` to populate the T1CharString's `.width` attribute, then memoises), and `get_path(name)` returning the simple list-of-tuples format `("moveto", x, y)` / `("lineto", x, y)` / `("curveto", x1, y1, x2, y2, x, y)` / `("closepath",)`. fontTools' `T1Font` normally requires a file path — we bypass that by setting `data` + `encoding` directly on a `__new__`-built instance and triggering `parse()` on first dict access. Library-first per CLAUDE.md MEMORY.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/cff/cff_font.py` (NEW): thin wrapper over `fontTools.cffLib.CFFFontSet`. Exposes `CFFFont.from_bytes(raw)` (PDF `/FontFile3 /Subtype /Type1C` stream form), `font_names`, `name`, `units_per_em` (derived as `1 / FontMatrix[0]`, default 1000 for the standard CFF matrix `[0.001 0 0 0.001 0 0]`), `font_matrix`, `has_glyph(name)`, `get_width(name)` (uses `fontTools.misc.psCharStrings.T2WidthExtractor` with `nominalWidthX` / `defaultWidthX` from the CFF Private DICT — interprets the leading charstring operand as `width - nominalWidthX` per CFF §3.1), and `get_path(name)` in the same list-of-tuples format.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type1_font.py`: extended `get_glyph_width(code)` to consult the embedded font program (parsed lazily from `/FontFile` via `Type1Font.from_bytes`) **after** `/Widths` and **before** the Standard 14 AFM fallback. Added `get_glyph_path(code) -> list[tuple]` returning the program's outline for `code` in font units (empty list when no program / unmapped). Added `set_font_program(font: Type1Font | None)` injector mirroring the TTF-side `set_true_type_font` — lets callers that already have the program in hand bypass `/FontFile` parsing, and lets tests skip the byte-level fixture round-trip. Code → glyph-name resolution honours `/Encoding` (with `/Differences` overlay) via the existing `get_encoding_typed()` chain.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type1c_font.py`: graduated from a marker subclass to a working CFF-backed font wrapper. Overrides `_program_width(code)` and `get_glyph_path(code)` to source widths and outlines from the embedded `/FontFile3` (`/Subtype /Type1C`) stream via `CFFFont.from_bytes`. `set_font_program(font: CFFFont | None)` injector mirrors PDType1Font. `/Widths` precedence and Standard 14 AFM fallback continue to flow through the inherited `PDType1Font.get_glyph_width`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_mm_type1_font.py`: still a pure marker subclass — `set_font_program` / `get_glyph_width` / `get_glyph_path` inherit unchanged from `PDType1Font`. Multiple-Master variant axis interpolation is deferred (PDFBox upstream also delegates to the Type 1 path for these methods).
- Deferred: auto-dispatch of `PDType1CFont` from `PDFontFactory` based on FontDescriptor `/FontFile3 /Subtype /Type1C` inspection (today the wrapper is reachable only via direct construction); CID-keyed CFF (`/Subtype /CIDFontType0C`) parsing through the same CFFFont primitive (planned alongside PDCIDFontType0 enrichment); rendering integration (`PDFRenderer` will start consuming `get_glyph_path` once text ops are wired up — see Rendering cluster #1 deferral note).

## Standard 14 AFM bundling

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/afm/` (NEW): bundles the 14 Adobe Core AFM files (Times-Roman / -Bold / -Italic / -BoldItalic, Helvetica / -Bold / -Oblique / -BoldOblique, Courier / -Bold / -Oblique / -BoldOblique, Symbol, ZapfDingbats) verbatim from `pdfbox/src/main/resources/org/apache/pdfbox/resources/afm/`. Loaded via `importlib.resources` so the lookup works from wheels, editable installs, and source checkouts. License + Adobe redistribution notice in `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/afm/LICENSE.txt`; root `NOTICE` updated to acknowledge the Adobe Core 14 AFM bundle.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/afm_loader.py` (NEW, original): thin wrapper over `fontTools.afmLib.AFM`. Exposes `load_standard14(name) -> AfmMetrics` (per-name singleton cache — same instance returned on every call, mirroring upstream `Standard14Fonts.getAFM`), plus `AfmMetrics.get_glyph_width(name) -> float` and `AfmMetrics.get_font_metrics() -> dict` (FontName / FontBBox / ItalicAngle / Ascent / Descent / CapHeight / XHeight / StemV / IsFixedPitch). `StemV` is sourced from AFM `StdVW` (the AFM names for vertical-stem-width).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/standard14_fonts.py`: per-glyph widths and font-descriptor numerics (FontBBox, ItalicAngle, Ascent, Descent, CapHeight, XHeight, StemV) now load from the bundled AFM via `afm_loader.load_standard14`. The static `_FAMILY_METRICS` dict of placeholder averages is gone; only the `Flags` bits (computed from family heuristics) and the alias map stay static. `get_average_widths(name)` builds the 256-element table by mapping each code through the font's default encoding (StandardEncoding for Times / Helvetica / Courier, SymbolEncoding for Symbol, ZapfDingbatsEncoding for ZapfDingbats per PDF 32000-1 §9.6.2.4) and looking the glyph name up in the AFM. Codes resolving to `.notdef` get `0.0`. The 256-element table is cached per canonical name; callers receive a fresh copy. New `Standard14Fonts.get_afm(name)` and `Standard14Fonts.get_glyph_width(name, glyph_name)` mirror the upstream FontMetrics surface.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type1_font.py`: `get_glyph_width(code)` routes through `/Widths` first (PDF 32000-1 §9.6.6.4 — `/Widths` overrides AFM even for the Standard 14), then the embedded font program if any, then the bundled AFM via `Standard14Fonts.get_glyph_width` for the canonical fonts (with optional `/Encoding` overlay), then `0.0`.

## Rendering cluster #1 — Pillow + aggdraw page rasteriser

- `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` (NEW): `PDFRenderer(document)` mirrors `org.apache.pdfbox.rendering.PDFRenderer`. Subclasses `PDFStreamEngine` and folds the page-drawing logic that upstream splits into `PageDrawer` directly into operator handlers. Backend is **Pillow + aggdraw** — aggdraw provides anti-aliased AGG-quality stroking, native cubic Bezier path segments, and PIL-style `(a, b, c, d, e, f)` affine transforms via `Draw.settransform(...)`. Operators implemented: path construction (`m`, `l`, `c`, `v`, `y`, `re`, `h`), painting (`S`, `s`, `f`/`F`, `f*`, `B`, `B*`, `b`, `b*`, `n`), graphics state (`q`/`Q` push/pop CTM + colour + line width), transform (`cm`), colour (`RG`/`rg`/`G`/`g`/`K`/`k` for DeviceRGB/DeviceGray/DeviceCMYK), line width (`w`), and image XObject `Do` for `/Subtype /Image` (JPEGs via `/Filter /DCTDecode` open through PIL after stop-filtering at DCTDecode; raw 8-bpc DeviceRGB / DeviceGray rasters via `Image.frombytes`). Even-odd fill rule (`f*`/`B*`/`b*`) is implemented by flattening Beziers and XOR-merging per-subpath PIL polygon masks (aggdraw's path fill is non-zero only); the resulting binary mask loses sub-pixel AA on the outer edge, a documented limitation. Initial CTM bakes the PDF→PIL Y-axis flip plus DPI scale plus media-box origin offset into a single 6-tuple. Per-render aggdraw `Draw` is rebuilt after any direct PIL paste so its internal pixel buffer never overwrites pasted-mutation regions on `flush()`. Deferred to text/font cluster: text operators (`BT`/`ET`/`Tj`/`TJ`/`'`/`"`) are silently skipped — real glyph rendering needs the font cluster's `fontTools` glyph paths. Deferred entirely (silent skip): shadings, patterns, transparency groups, soft masks, blend modes, line dash/cap/join, clipping paths, form XObjects, inline images. `render_image(page_index, scale=1.0)` and `render_image_with_dpi(page_index, dpi=72.0)` mirror upstream's two entry points.

## Rendering cluster #2 — text + form XObjects + clip + inline images

- `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py`: extended with four operator families.
  - **Text**: `BT`/`ET`/`Tf`/`Tc`/`Tw`/`TL`/`Tz`/`Ts`/`Td`/`TD`/`Tm`/`T*`/`Tj`/`TJ`/`'`/`"`. The `_GState` dataclass now carries text state (font, font size, text matrix, text line matrix, char spacing, word spacing, leading, rise, horizontal scaling). Glyph outlines for embedded TrueType fonts come through fontTools (`tt.getGlyphSet()[name].draw(pen)`) into a custom `_AggdrawPathPen` that scales coordinates to unit-em and emits aggdraw `Path.curveto`/`lineto`/`moveto`/`close`. Quadratic TT segments are converted to exact cubic Beziers via the standard 1/3 control-point elevation. `qCurveTo`'s implicit-on-curve walk follows fontTools' TT convention (consecutive off-curves get a halfway implicit on-curve). `PDType0Font` with a `CIDFontType2` descendant pulls the descendant's `/FontDescriptor /FontFile2` and reuses the same path. `PDType1Font` / `PDType3Font` / Standard 14 (no embedded program) silently fall back to a faint placeholder rectangle covering the glyph's advance × ~0.7 em — non-fatal, no crash. Per-font lookups are cached on `(id(resources), font_key)` so `Tf` doesn't re-parse the embedded TTF on every text run.
  - **Form XObjects** (`Do` for `/Subtype /Form`): saves the GS, post-multiplies the form's `/Matrix` onto the CTM, intersects the form's `/BBox` into the current clip mask, swaps `_resources` for the form's own `/Resources` if present, then re-feeds the form's content-stream bytes through the engine's dispatch loop via a small `_process_form_bytes` helper (a thin wrapper around `PDFStreamParser` over a `RandomAccessReadBuffer` — the form is not yet a `PDContentStream` subclass).
  - **Clip** (`W` / `W*`): a `_pending_clip` flag is set; the next `n` (or any path-paint operator) builds a polygon mask in device space (Beziers flattened by 16-step sampling, even-odd via `ImageChops.logical_xor` per subpath, non-zero via per-subpath polygon union), intersects it with any existing GS clip via `ImageChops.multiply`, and stores the result on `_GState.clip_mask`. Subsequent paint operators render into a transparent RGBA layer and composite back through `clip_mask`. Image pastes mask their bbox by `(rect_mask × clip_mask)`.
  - **Inline images** (`BI` … `ID` … `EI`): the parser already collapses the triplet into a single `BI` operator carrying both `image_parameters` (the dict) and `image_data` (the raw bytes). `_op_inline_image` synthesises a transient PIL image from those, recognising the abbreviated keys per PDF spec §8.9.7 Table 92 (`W`/`H`/`CS`/`BPC`/`F`) and the abbreviated colour-space + filter names (`G`/`RGB`/`CMYK`, `DCT`/`JPX`/`Fl`/`A85`/`AHx`/`CCF`/`LZW`/`RL`), then routes through the same `_paste_image` path as `Do`-image.
  - **Deferred (silent skip)**: shadings, patterns, transparency groups, soft masks, blend modes, line dash/cap/join, `Tr` text rendering modes (clipping/stroke), Type1/Type3/Standard 14 glyph outlines (placeholder rectangle).

## Rendering cluster #3 — Type1 / Type1C (CFF) text rasterisation

- `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py`: glyph dispatch in `_show_string` / `_draw_glyph` now branches on font kind. The TTF branch (cluster #2) is preserved unchanged. New branch: when the resolved PDFont is a `PDType1Font` (PFB-backed embedded Type 1) or `PDType1CFont` (CFF / Type1C — `/FontFile3 /Subtype /Type1C`), the renderer pulls the per-glyph command tuples from `font.get_glyph_path(code)` (Wave 17 fontTools-backed APIs), feeds them into a small `_build_aggdraw_path_from_commands` helper that converts (`moveto`, `lineto`, `curveto`, `closepath`) into `aggdraw.Path` segments scaled by `1 / units_per_em`, and reuses the same `_fill_aggdraw_path` pipeline as the TTF branch (clip-mask-aware fill onto the device CTM). `units_per_em` is sourced from `Type1Font.units_per_em` / `CFFFont.units_per_em` (typically 1000 for the canonical Type 1 font matrix `[0.001 0 0 0.001 0 0]`). Subclasses of `PDType1Font` (`PDMMType1Font`, `PDType1CFont`) are matched via isinstance and ride the same code path.
- **Standard 14 substitution remains deferred.** When a font names a Standard 14 family (Helvetica, Times-Roman, Courier, Symbol, ZapfDingbats, …) but ships *no* embedded program (no `/FontFile`, no `/FontFile3`), `get_glyph_path` returns `[]` and we still emit the cluster #2 placeholder rectangle. To make the gap explicit, the renderer now logs **once per font** at `DEBUG` (`"Standard 14 ... using placeholder rectangle (Liberation TTF substitution not yet bundled — see CHANGES.md)"`) — tracked on `_warned_standard14_fonts: set[id(font)]`. Two viable substitution paths remain on the table for a future cluster: (a) bundling Liberation TTFs from PDFBox's resources (SIL OFL — permissive but the OFL font-rename clause adds NOTICE complexity), or (b) deferring further until users hit the gap with a real corpus. Trade-off: Liberation gives PDFBox-parity Standard-14 rendering at the cost of ~2 MB of bundled fonts and an OFL attribution row in NOTICE; deferring keeps the wheel lean but means Helvetica/Times/Courier render as faint outline boxes.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_object_reference.py`: added typed `get_referenced_object()` (resolves `/Obj` to a `PDAnnotation` subclass via `PDAnnotation.create`, or to `PDFormXObject`/`PDImageXObject` for `/Subtype /Form` / `/Image` streams) and `set_referenced_object(obj)` (typed setter accepting a `PDAnnotation`/`PDXObject` wrapper or `None`). Raw `get_obj` / `set_obj` accessors stay for back-compat. Local imports avoid the cos→pdmodel→annotation/XObject cycle.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/state/pd_font_setting.py`: typed wrapper over the ExtGState `/Font` 2-element array. `get_font()` resolves slot 0 via `PDFontFactory.create_font` (returns `None` when slot is absent / not a font dictionary — upstream returns the raw `PDFont` only when `/Subtype` is recognised); `set_font(None)` writes `COSNull.NULL` rather than removing the slot so the array shape stays `[font, size]`. `PDExtendedGraphicsState.get_font_setting` / `set_font_setting` route through it; the existing raw `get_font` / `set_font` / `get_font_size` / `set_font_size` helpers are unchanged and operate on the same underlying COSArray.

## Wave 19 — BlendMode + tagged-content authoring + StructureNode insert_before

- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/pdfa_identification_schema.py` (NEW): typed `PDFAIdentificationSchema` wrapper for the PDF/A Identification XMP schema (`http://www.aiim.org/pdfa/ns/id/`, prefix `pdfaid`). Surfaces `part` (int), `conformance`, `amd`, `rev`, `corr` getters/setters; `set_*(None)` removes the entry. Wired into `DomXmpParser._SCHEMA_REGISTRY` for parser dispatch and `XMPMetadata.get_pdf_identification_schema()` for typed lookup. `get_part()` coerces parser-supplied string values back to `int` (returns `None` on garbage rather than raising).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/blend_mode.py` (NEW): typed `BlendMode` wrapper. 17 named singletons (12 separable per PDF 32000-1 §11.3.5.1 + 4 non-separable per §11.3.5.2 + Compatible-as-Normal alias). `BlendMode.from_cos(base)` accepts COSName (direct lookup) or COSArray of COSNames (returns the first recognised entry, falling back to the array's first name when none match — mirrors the PDF spec's fallback-chain shape). `PDExtendedGraphicsState.get_blend_mode()` now returns `BlendMode | None` (was `COSName | str | None`); `set_blend_mode` accepts `BlendMode | COSName | str | None`. **Behavior change**: `copy_into_graphics_state` now passes a `BlendMode` instance to the target's `set_blend_mode` callback (was: raw `COSName`). Consumers can call `BlendMode.get_cos_name()` for the round-trip name.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_content_stream.py`: marked-content authoring shipped — `begin_marked_content(tag)` / `begin_marked_content_with_dict(tag, prop_list)` / `end_marked_content()` / `add_marked_content_point(tag)` / `add_marked_content_point_with_dict(tag, prop_list)` emit `BMC` / `BDC` / `EMC` / `MP` / `DP`. The `_with_dict` overloads accept either a typed `PDPropertyList` (auto-registered under `/Resources/Properties` with a fresh `Prop<n>` key — re-uses the existing slot when the same property list is referenced twice), a `COSName`, or a `str` interpreted as a literal property-list key. `show_text(...)` now also accepts `bytes` for callers that have already encoded text through their font's encoder; bytes containing CR/LF/null/non-ASCII are emitted as hex form (`<...>`), the rest as literal-string form (`(...)`). Closes the BMC/BDC/EMC item from the wave-7 deferred list.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_structure_node.py`: added `insert_before(new_kid, before_kid)` returning `True` on success / `False` when the anchor kid is missing. Single-entry `/K` is auto-promoted to a `COSArray` when the insert lands a second sibling. Anchor matching reuses the same `_same_kid` predicate as `remove_kid` so int MCID anchors compare correctly against `COSInteger` `/K` slots.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/pd_function_type4.py`: added `clear_instruction_cache()` (no upstream counterpart) — defensive escape hatch for callers that mutate the underlying COSStream body via `pd_stream.set_data(...)` after the first `eval`, since pypdfbox now caches the parsed PostScript instruction sequence on the wrapper for shading-renderer hot-path performance.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/pd_function_type0.py`: `/Order = 3` (cubic-spline) interpolation now implemented per PDF 32000-1 §7.10.2 — Catmull-Rom Hermite over 4 surrounding samples per axis with edge-clamped neighbour lookups, folded one dim at a time (4^n samples per output dim, vs 2^n for linear). `/Order` values other than 1 or 3 fall back to linear with a `DEBUG` log line. Closes the cubic-spline deferral noted on the original Type-0 sampled-table eval entry.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_movie.py` (NEW): typed `PDAnnotationMovie` wrapper for `/Subtype /Movie` per PDF 32000-1 §12.5.6.17 Table 184. Surfaces `/T` (title), `/Movie` (raw `COSDictionary` — typed `PDMovie` per Table 271 still deferred), and `/A` (raw `COSBase` — boolean or activation dict; typed `PDMovieActivation` deferred). Wired into `PDAnnotation.create` factory dispatch. `PDActionMovie` now exposes `get_annotation()` returning the typed wrapper and `set_annotation()` accepting `PDAnnotationMovie | COSBase | None`; the legacy raw accessor is preserved as `get_annotation_dictionary()`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/optionalcontent/pd_optional_content_group.py`: `/Usage` typed accessor pairs added for the four most-used sub-categories per PDF 32000-1 §8.11.4.4 Table 102 — `get/set_usage_{view,print,export}_state`, `get/set_usage_creator`, `get/set_usage_language`, plus `USAGE_STATE_ON` / `USAGE_STATE_OFF` constants. **Behavior change vs upstream**: `set_*(None)` removes the targeted leaf entry and additionally prunes the containing sub-dict and the `/Usage` dict itself when they become empty, so cleared OCGs do not retain empty `/Usage` husks. Reads return Python `str` (uppercase for state names) instead of `COSName`.

## Wave 20 — typed action surfaces

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_launch.py`: full PDF 32000-1 §12.6.4.5 Table 196 surface — `get/set_file` now resolves `/F` through `PDFileSpecification.create_fs(...)` (returns `PDSimpleFileSpecification` for COSString form, `PDComplexFileSpecification` for COSDictionary form — matches upstream `getFile()` typed return); added `get/set_d` (`/D` Solaris/Mac launch command), `get/set_o` (`/O` operation — Win only), `get/set_p` (`/P` parameters — Win only) text-string accessors; `get/set_open_in_new_window` (`/NewWindow` boolean, defaults False when absent); `get/set_win_launch_params` returning the `/Win` sub-dict (Table 197) as raw `COSDictionary`. **Deferred**: typed `PDWindowsLaunchParams` wrapper around the `/Win` sub-dict — callers currently work directly with the `COSDictionary`. **API change vs prior pypdfbox lite surface**: `set_file` previously accepted `str`; now accepts `PDFileSpecification | None`, mirroring upstream. Existing callers wrap their string in `PDSimpleFileSpecification`.

## Wave 22 — 18 parallel agent items: parity round-out across pdmodel/font/text/rendering

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/taggedpdf/pd_layout_attribute_object.py`: 12 new accessor pairs reaching ~80% parity with upstream Layout — `b_box`, `block_align`, `border_colors` (polymorphic 3-tuple OR `PDFourColours`), `border_style` (single name OR 4-name array), `border_thickness`, `column_count`, `column_gap`, `column_widths`, `padding`, `inline_align`, `height` / `width` (number OR `"Auto"`). Added enum constants for each name-typed attribute. Pre-existing `get/set_border_color` retained for back-compat.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/image/pd_image_x_object.py`: 9 new accessor pairs — `mask` (typed `PDImageXObject` for stream form, `None` when color-key array), `color_key_mask` (returns `list[int]` for the array form), `soft_mask`, `decode`, `is_interpolate` / `is_image_mask`, `struct_parent` (default `-1`), `metadata` (typed `PDMetadata`), `oc` (typed `PDPropertyList`). Mask vs color-key are mutually exclusive on read.
- `pypdfbox/text/text_position.py`: parity expansion — added `dir`, `text_matrix` fields; new methods `get_x_directional_adj`, `get_y_directional_adj`, `get_x_scale`, `get_y_scale`, `get_height_dir`, `get_dir`, `get_individual_widths`, `get_visible_text`, `contains_diacritic`, `is_diacritic`, `merge_diacritic`, `get_text_matrix`, `get_end_x`, `get_end_y`. All new fields default-initialised — existing `pdf_text_stripper.py` call sites unchanged. Round-out adds `set_unicode`, `get_visually_ordered_unicode` (string reversed when any code point is bidi class `R` / `AL`, mirroring upstream's RTL-detection branch), `get_height` (returns `font_size`, agreeing with `get_height_dir` since the lite port has no per-glyph max-height tracking), `get_character_codes` (returns Unicode code points of decoded text — upstream returns the original PDF byte codes captured at decode time; lite port decodes through `/ToUnicode` + `/Differences` and doesn't retain raw codes), and `completely_contains` (strict bounding-box containment using `get_height_dir` as the height proxy).
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/true_type_font.py`: 13 parity accessors — `get_name` (PostScript name, nameID 6), `get_family_name` (1), `get_full_name` (4), `get_version` (5), `get_font_bbox`, `get_italic_angle`, `get_underline_position` / `_thickness`, `is_fixed_pitch`, `get_weight` (`OS/2 usWeightClass`, default 400), `get_width` (default 5), `get_capabilities` (table-presence map), `has_table(tag)`. Delegates to the existing fontTools `TTFont` instance.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_color_space.py`: base `get_default_decode(bpc)` declared; `pd_device_gray.py` / `pd_device_rgb.py` / `pd_device_cmyk.py` implement concrete `[0.0, 1.0]` × N component arrays. `get_initial_color` was already declared abstract.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_embedded_go_to.py`: 6 upstream-named accessor aliases — `get/set_destination` (alias of `get/set_d`), `get/set_open_in_new_window` (`/NewWindow`, default `False`), `get/set_target_directory` (alias of `get/set_target`). Legacy `get_d` / `set_d` / `is_new_window` / `set_new_window` / `get_target` / `set_target` retained.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_field_factory.py`: full `/FT` dispatch was already implemented (`/Tx → PDTextField`, `/Btn` with bit 17 → `PDPushButton`, bit 16 → `PDRadioButton`, else `PDCheckBox`, `/Ch` with bit 18 → `PDComboBox` else `PDListBox`, `/Sig → PDSignatureField`); 13 new dispatch tests added. CHANGES.md prior wave-7 wording calling out "all terminal fields currently return PDFieldStub" was stale.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type3_font.py`: 13 accessors round-out — `get_char_proc(name)` single-glyph lookup, redesigned `get_font_matrix() -> list[float]` with default `[0.001, 0, 0, 0.001, 0, 0]` per PDF 32000-1 §9.2.4, typed `get/set_font_bbox` returning `PDRectangle`, plus inherited `get_first_char` / `get_last_char` / `get_widths` / new `set_widths` / `set_first_char` / `set_last_char`. **Behavior change**: `get_font_matrix` no longer returns `COSArray | None`; legacy test updated.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_lab.py`: confirmed already-shipped `get/set_white_point` / `_black_point` / `_range` per §8.6.5.4; added 7 explicit parity tests.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/destination/pd_destination_name_tree_node.py`: now subclasses generic `PDNameTreeNode[PDPageDestination]` (closes the wave-19 deferred adoption note). `get_value(name)` traverses balanced `/Kids` trees; `get_names()` returns `dict[str, PDPageDestination]` (was `list[str]`); `set_value(name, dest|None)` and `names()` retained as back-compat shims. Legacy test updated.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/taggedpdf/pd_user_attribute_object.py`: 4 upstream-named methods — `get_owner_properties` (alias of legacy `get_property`), `set_owner_properties`, `add_owner_property(name, value, formatted=None, hidden=False)`, `remove_owner_property(name)`. `/H` is omitted when False.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_simple_font.py`: 10 PDF-32000-1 §9.8.1 flag accessors — `is_symbolic` / `is_italic` / `is_bold` / `is_fixed_pitch` / `is_serif` / `is_script` / `is_force_bold` / `is_all_cap` / `is_small_cap` / `is_standard_14`. `is_bold` is derived from `/FontWeight ≥ 700` (PDF spec uses /FontWeight, not a /Flags bit; `is_force_bold` is the actual /Flags bit 19).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_terminal_field.py`: typed `get_widgets() -> list[PDAnnotationWidget]` (was raw `list[COSDictionary]`), `set_widgets(widgets)` writes `/Kids` and wires each widget's `/Parent` back; `set_actions(typed)` typed override; `apply_change()` / `construct_appearances()` no-op + debug log (appearance regeneration deferred). **Consumer fix-ups**: `pd_acro_form.py::flatten` and `pd_variable_text.py::set_default_appearance` now call `widget.get_cos_object()` to drill down to the COSDictionary.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_cid_font.py`: 10 parity accessors — `is_embedded`, `get_program` (decodes the first present FontFile/2/3 stream via PDStream.create_input_stream), `get_bounding_box` (PDRectangle from /FontDescriptor /FontBBox), `get_average_font_width` (mean of positive /W or /DW), `has_glyph`, `get_displacement`, `get_position_vector`, `get_height`, `code_to_cid` (identity at base; subclasses do real mapping).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/optionalcontent/pd_optional_content_group.py`: added `get_intent() / set_intent(value)` — `/Intent` accepts string or `list[str]`, defaults to `"View"`. The pre-existing `get_intents()` plural form (returning `list[COSName]`) is preserved alongside.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_tree.py`: confirmed already-shipped `index_of`, `add`, `insert_after`, `insert_before`, `remove`; 6 new parity tests added.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_go_to.py`: typed `get_destination` / `set_destination` — `/D` returns `PDDestination` for COSArray, `str` for COSString or COSName (named destination form). `set_destination` accepts `PDDestination | str | None`. **Behavior change**: previously named-destination forms returned a `PDNamedDestination` wrapper; now they return a plain `str`. Sole in-tree consumer (`PDOutlineItem.find_destination_page`) gates on `isinstance(d, PDPageDestination)` and is unaffected.
- `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py`: 7 upstream-named API additions — `is_page_image_with_annotations(page_index)`, `set_subsampling_allowed` / `is_subsampling_allowed`, `set_default_destination` / `get_default_destination` (default `"View"`), `set_image_downscaling_optimization_threshold` / `get_image_downscaling_optimization_threshold` (default `0.5`). All store-only flags — render loop unchanged.
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py`: 4 parity accessors — `get_document()` returns the parsed `COSDocument` (None before parse), `get_pd_document()` lazy-builds + caches a `PDDocument` wrapper, `set_lenient(b)` / `is_lenient()` toggle (default True; pypdfbox already runs lenient).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/shading/pd_shading_type6.py` + `pd_shading_type7.py`: typed `get_decode() -> list[float] | None` (was raw COSArray), `get_function() -> PDFunction | None` (dispatched through `PDFunction.create`); setters accept iterables / typed wrappers / None. `get_bits_per_*` now returns `-1` when absent (matches upstream Java `int` default).

Closes the CID-keyed CFF deferred note from wave 17.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_cid_font_type2.py`: 9 parity accessors — `get_cid_to_gid_map_bytes` (decoded stream payload, None for /Identity), `is_identity_cid_to_gid_map`, `get_true_type_font` (lazy-parses /FontFile2 via fontbox, cached), `set_true_type_font`, `is_embedded` (narrowed to /FontFile2 only — Type2's only legal embedding form), `has_glyph` (TTF-aware override), `get_glyph_path` (cid→gid → fontTools `glyph_set[name].draw(pen)`), `code_to_cid` identity. Naming deviation: `get_cid_to_gid_map_bytes` (not `get_cid_to_gid_map`) so the parent's existing `get_cid_to_gid_map() -> COSStream | str | None` accessor is preserved for back-compat.
- `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper.py`: 17 PDFBox-named extraction options — `set/is_sort_by_position` (wired into `_format_positions`), `set/is_suppress_duplicate_overlapping_text`, `is_should_separate_by_beads`, `set/get_drop_threshold`, `set/get_indent_threshold`, `set/get_spacing_tolerance`, `set/get_average_char_tolerance`, `set/get_add_more_formatting`, `set/is_lenient_stream_parsing`. - `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_information.py`: 17 hand-written parity tests (no source change — already had full upstream-named surface).

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_font_descriptor.py`: 25 parity additions — full /Flags bit predicates (`is/set_serif/symbolic/script/non_symbolic/all_cap/small_cap/force_bold` plus existing fixed_pitch/italic), generic `get_flag(bit)` / `set_flag(bit, value)` helpers, missing numeric metric setters (`set_stem_h`, `get/set_avg_width` / `max_width` / `missing_width` / `leading`), `get_font_bounding_box() -> PDRectangle | None` typed.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/outline/pd_outline_item.py`: 11 hand-written parity tests (no source change — full upstream surface already present per wave 8).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_viewer_preferences.py`: 8 parity additions — `is_hide_toolbar` / `is_hide_menubar` / `is_hide_window_ui` / `is_fit_window` / `is_center_window` / `is_display_doc_title` / `is_pick_tray_by_pdf_size` boolean accessors, `get/set_direction` upstream-named aliases. Plus 13 string constants for enum-valued options (NON_FS_*, DIRECTION_*, PRINT_SCALING_*, DUPLEX_*, BOUNDARY_*).
- `pypdfbox/filter/filter.py` + `pypdfbox/filter/filter_factory.py`: 6 parity additions — `Filter.decode_result` static convenience constructor, `Filter.get_decode_params(parameters, index)` static helper resolving /DecodeParms or /DP, `Filter.is_decompression_input_size_known()` (default True), `FilterFactory.INSTANCE` singleton, `FilterFactory.get_filter(name)` / `get_filter_by_short_name(short_name)` (Fl/Ah/etc. abbreviations).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/form/pd_form_x_object.py`: 10 parity additions — `get/set_struct_parents` (default -1), `get/set_oc` typed PDPropertyList, `get/set_group/ref/pieceinfo` raw COSDictionary, `get/set_last_modified` typed datetime via `_parse_pdf_date` / `_format_pdf_date`, `get/set_name`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/destination/*`: 15 hand-written parity tests for PDPageXYZDestination + PDPageFitHeight/Width/Rectangle (no source changes — full upstream surface already present, including upstream-correct `FitV`/`FitH` literal mismatch in PDPageFit{Height,Width}Destination.TYPE).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_structure_element.py`: 27 hand-written parity tests (no source change — full upstream surface present).

## Wave 25 — 20 parallel agent items: deeper parity round-out (font/cos/graphics/annotation)

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type1c_font.py`: 11 parity additions — `get_cff_font` / `get_cff_type1_font` aliases, `is_embedded` (overrides parent: only checks `/FontFile3`), `is_damaged` (true only when CFF parse fails), `get_path(name)` name-keyed + `has_glyph(name)` charset check, `code_to_name` / `code_to_gid` encoding-driven lookups, `get_units_per_em` (default 1000), `get_height(code)` cached glyph bbox, `get_average_font_width` override (/Widths → CFF `defaultWidthX` → AFM → 0.0). **Deviation from upstream**: upstream hardcodes 500 for unknown average; we fall back to AFM/Standard14 metrics first.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_labels.py` + `pd_page_label_range.py`: 4 parity additions — `find_label_range_containing(page_index)` (greatest start_index <= page_index), `get_number_of_pages` / `set_number_of_pages` overrides (validates non-negative), `format_label_index(index)` alias for `compute_label_for_offset`.

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/shading/pd_shading_type3.py`: typed accessors aligned with wave-22 PDShadingType6/7 pattern — `get_coords` / `set_coords` (`/Coords` 6-element required), `get_domain` / `set_domain` returning typed COSArray with default `[0.0, 1.0]`, `get_function` / `set_function` typed via `PDFunction.create()`, `get_extend` / `set_extend(start, end)` typed `tuple[bool, bool]` with default `(False, False)`.

## Wave 27 — 3 parallel agents: 3 new typed XMP schemas

- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_media_management_schema.py` (NEW): `XMPMediaManagementSchema` (`xmpMM:` namespace `http://ns.adobe.com/xap/1.0/mm/`). 10 typed text-property accessors — `document_id`, `instance_id`, `original_document_id`, `version_id`, `rendition_class`, `rendition_params`, `manage_to`, `manage_ui`, `manager`, `manager_variant`. `DerivedFrom` / `Ingredients` deferred (need ResourceRef typed wrapper). Wired into `XMPMetadata.get/add_xmp_media_management_schema` + `DomXmpParser._SCHEMA_REGISTRY`.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_rights_management_schema.py` (NEW): `XMPRightsManagementSchema` (`xmpRights:` namespace `http://ns.adobe.com/xap/1.0/rights/`). Accessors — text `certificate` / `web_statement`, boolean `marked` (stored as upstream-style "True"/"False" text; reader accepts both capitalised and lowercase forms; None ≠ False), Bag-of-text `owners` (with `add_owner` helper), LangAlt `usage_terms(lang="x-default")`. Wired into XMPMetadata + parser registry.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/pdfa_extension_schema.py` (NEW): `PDFAExtensionSchema` (`pdfaExtension:` namespace + nested `pdfaSchema:` / `pdfaProperty:` / `pdfaType:` namespaces auto-registered on construction). Lite surface — `get_extension_schemas()` returns `list[dict[str, str]]` with `schema`/`namespaceURI`/`prefix` per declared extension; `add_extension_schema(schema, namespace_uri, prefix)` appends a Bag struct; `get_schemas_element()` raw passthrough; `get_count()`. Replaces the wave-24 placeholder in `XMPMetadata.get_pdfa_extension_schema` (was returning None). Full nested-struct typing for `pdfaSchema:property` + `pdfaSchema:valueType` deferred. Existing `test_xmp_metadata_parity::test_pdf_basic_schema_placeholders_return_none_when_absent` narrowed to AdobePDF-only since the PDF/A-extension placeholder is now real.

## Wave 28 — 20 parallel agents: XMP schemas, measurement / OCG-state / PDF 2.0 actions, fontbox tables, signature properties

- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/adobe_pdf_schema.py` (NEW): `AdobePDFSchema` (`pdf:` namespace `http://ns.adobe.com/pdf/1.3/`). Typed accessors for `Keywords`, `PDFVersion`, `Producer`. Replaces `XMPMetadata.get_adobe_pdf_schema` / `add_adobe_pdf_schema` / `create_and_add_adobe_pdf_schema` placeholders (with `get_pdf_schema` / `add_pdf_basic_schema` aliases). Registered in `DomXmpParser._SCHEMA_REGISTRY`. **Deviation**: the `setKeywordsProperty` / `setPDFVersionProperty` / `setProducerProperty` `TextType`-typed accessors are deferred until the `AbstractField` hierarchy lands; string-valued setters/getters provide full functional parity. Upstream `AdobePDFSchema` in PDFBox 3.0.x does not declare a `Trapped` property despite the Adobe `pdf:` namespace including it — mirroring upstream verbatim. The previously-deferred parity test asserting placeholder-returns-None was replaced with a real round-trip test.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_basic_job_ticket_schema.py` (NEW): `XMPBasicJobTicketSchema` (`xmpBJ:` namespace `http://ns.adobe.com/xap/1.0/bj/`) + co-located lite `JobType` (upstream is in `org.apache.xmpbox.type.JobType`). `JobRef` Bag entries are stored as plain dicts keyed by `id`/`name`/`url`; `get_jobs()` materialises typed `JobType` wrappers on demand. `JobType` is a lite value object (no `AbstractStructuredType` base) with `as_dict`/`from_dict` round-trip helpers. Registered with `XMPMetadata.add_xmp_basic_job_ticket_schema` / `create_and_add_basic_job_ticket_schema`.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_paged_text_schema.py` (NEW): `XMPageTextSchema` (`xmpTPg:` namespace `http://ns.adobe.com/xap/1.0/t/pg/`). Class name kept verbatim from upstream (`XMPageTextSchema`, not `XMPagedTextSchema`). `NPages` exposed as Python `int` via `get_n_pages` / `set_n_pages` (cluster #1 stores as string, coerces on read). `MaxPageSize` / `Colorants` / `Fonts` accept either struct-shaped dicts or plain strings — typed `Dimensions` / `Colorant` / `Font` struct wrappers deferred. Registered in `XMPMetadata` + parser registry.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/photoshop_schema.py` (NEW): `PhotoshopSchema` (`photoshop:` namespace `http://ns.adobe.com/photoshop/1.0/`) — 18 properties. Typed accessors return Python primitives (`str`, `int | None`, `list[str]`) rather than upstream `TextType` / `IntegerType` / `URIType` / `ProperNameType` / `DateType`; typed `*Property` getters/setters and `addProperty(AbstractField)` overloads deferred. `set_urgency` collapses upstream's `(String)` and `(Integer)` overloads into a single `int | str | None` setter. `TextLayers` (Seq<LayerType>) round-trip is deferred; constant mirrored, accessors not ported. Registered in `XMPMetadata` + parser registry.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/measurement/pd_measure_dictionary.py` + `pd_rectlinear_measure_dictionary.py` (NEW): typed `PDMeasureDictionary` (`/Type=Measure`) + `PDRectlinearMeasureDictionary` (`/Subtype=RL` with R/X/Y/D/A/T/S/O/CYX number-format-array accessors). Number-format arrays return `list[PDNumberFormatDictionary] | None` (Python has no `float[]`/array-type). `PDAnnotationPolygon.measure` / `PDAnnotationPolyline.measure` upgraded from raw `COSDictionary` to typed `PDMeasureDictionary` (replaces the wave-9 "deferred" placeholder; setters accept either form for back-compat).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/measurement/pd_number_format_dictionary.py` (NEW): typed `PDNumberFormatDictionary` (entries `U`/`C`/`F`/`D`/`FD`/`RT`/`RD`/`PS`/`SS`/`O`). Class constants `TYPE`, `LABEL_SUFFIX_TO_VALUE`, `LABEL_PREFIX_TO_VALUE`, `FRACTIONAL_DISPLAY_DECIMAL/FRACTION/ROUND/TRUNCATE`. `setFractionalDisplay` / `setLabelPositionToValue` raise Python `ValueError` instead of `IllegalArgumentException`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/measurement/pd_viewport_dictionary.py` (NEW): typed `PDViewportDictionary` (`/Type=Viewport`, `BBox` typed `PDRectangle`, `Name`, `Measure` typed `PDMeasureDictionary`). 1:1 port — setters accept `None` to remove (consistent with sibling measurement classes).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_set_ocg_state.py` (NEW): typed `PDActionSetOCGState` (`SUB_TYPE = "SetOCGState"`, `State` array of names + OCG refs, `PreserveRB`). No upstream PDFBox 3.0.x equivalent — added so factory yields a typed instance for `S = SetOCGState` instead of `PDActionUnknown`. Wired into `pd_action.py` factory dispatch.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_go_to_dp.py` (NEW): typed `PDActionGoToDp` (`SUB_TYPE = "GoToDp"`) — PDF 2.0 / ISO 32000-2 §12.6.4.4 action with `/Dp` accessor. Class name spelled `GoToDp` (lowercase `p`) to match the spec sub-type. No upstream PDFBox 3.0.x or trunk equivalent.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_rich_media_execute.py` (NEW): typed `PDActionRichMediaExecute` (`SUB_TYPE = "RichMediaExecute"`) — PDF 2.0 / ISO 32000-2 §13.6.4 action with `/TA`, `/TI`, `/CMD` accessors plus `/CMD/N` and `/CMD/A` convenience methods. No upstream PDFBox 3.0.x or trunk equivalent.
- `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper_by_area.py` (NEW): `PDFTextStripperByArea` extends `PDFTextStripper` with `add_region(name, rect)` / `remove_region` / `get_regions` / `get_text_for_region` / `extract_regions(page)`. Rectangle is in **PDF user space** (y-up, lower-left) — upstream uses Java AWT (y-down, top-left), the lite extractor stores positions in PDF user space already so we keep the rectangle in the same frame to avoid a per-call inversion that would surprise Python callers. Built on the lite `PDFTextStripper`, which does not yet reproduce upstream's reading order for composite-font / multi-column real-world PDFs; the ported `testSomeMethod` exercises the API surface against `eu-001.pdf` but defers exact-string assertions. `extract_regions` does the per-region binning directly via `_format_positions` rather than overriding `write_page`, since the lite stripper has no streaming `writePage` cycle. The lite base stripper invokes `process_text_position` from BOTH the parser walk and the per-region format walk (the latter is a lite-mode-only convenience re-emit; upstream's `writeString` doesn't re-fire `processTextPosition`). To preserve upstream binning semantics without double-counting, `process_text_position` is gated by an internal `_binning_active` flag set only across the parser-walk routing pass.
- `pypdfbox/text/text_metrics.py` (NEW): `TextMetrics` data holder constructed from a `TextPosition`; ascent/descent seeded from font size with the upstream-documented 0.7 / -0.2 ratios; `get_x` / `get_y` / `get_height` / mutators for ascent/descent. **No direct upstream Java source** — shape conforms to upstream-documented contract.
- `pypdfbox/text/word_with_text_positions.py` (NEW): `WordWithTextPositions` data holder. Promoted from upstream's `private static final` inner class of `PDFTextStripper` (lines 2171-2191 of the 3.0 branch) to a top-level public class so external callers can consume the structure directly.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/glyph_table.py` + `glyph_data.py` (NEW): `GlyphTable(TTFTable)` and `GlyphData` wrappers around fontTools' `glyf` table. `GlyphData.get_path()` returns a `fontTools.pens.recordingPen.RecordingPen` rather than a `java.awt.geom.GeneralPath` — callers replay `pen.value` onto any pen. `GlyphRenderer`, `GlyfSimpleDescript`, `GlyfCompositeDescript` are intentionally not ported — fontTools handles composite resolution and contour decoding. `BoundingBox` inlined into `glyph_data.py` (the wider `fontbox.util` package is not yet ported); will be moved when `fontbox.util` lands. `TTFTable.read` overridden to call `_bind(ttf)` since fontTools is itself the parser. `get_glyphs()` materialises `list[GlyphData]` rather than upstream's mutable array. Cache policy preserved (MAX_CACHE_SIZE=5000 / MAX_CACHED_GLYPHS=100). `TrueTypeFont.get_glyph_table()` + `get_glyph(gid)` lazy-cached convenience accessors added.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/kerning_table.py` + `kerning_subtable.py` (NEW): `KerningTable` + `KerningSubtable` wrappers around fontTools' `kern` table. Public `get_kerning(left, right)` / `get_kerning(glyphs)`, `is_horizontal_kerning(cross)`, `get_subtables()`, `get_horizontal_kerning_subtable(cross)` semantics match upstream. Format-1 / format-2 / Apple AAT subtables are exposed but report 0 adjustment (same effective behaviour as upstream's "unsupported subtable" log). `TrueTypeFont.get_kerning_table()` lazy-cached accessor added (no direct upstream equivalent — upstream exposes via `getTableMap`).
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/vertical_header_table.py` + `vertical_metrics_table.py` (NEW): `VerticalHeaderTable` (vhea) + `VerticalMetricsTable` (vmtx) wrappers. Structural read-from-stream is preserved (so `read()`-direct unit tests still work), but when accessed via `TrueTypeFont.get_vertical_header()` / `get_vertical_metrics()` the typed snapshots are populated from `fontTools.ttLib`'s parsed `vhea` / `vmtx` rather than from the raw byte stream. Both return `None` when the font lacks the table.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/glyph_positioning_table.py` (round-out): `GlyphPositioningTable(TTFTable)` wrapper around fontTools' `GPOS` table now exposes structural OT accessors `get_script_list` / `get_feature_list` / `get_lookup_list` / `get_lookup(index)` / `get_lookup_subtables(index)` / `get_feature_record(index)` / `get_lookup_indices_for_feature(tag)` returning the underlying `fontTools.ttLib.tables.otTables` objects (ScriptList / FeatureList / LookupList / Lookup / FeatureRecord). **Not present on upstream** — Apache PDFBox 3.0's `GlyphPositioningTable` keeps these structures private and exposes only `TAG` plus the GPOS-Header `read()` slot. pypdfbox surfaces them so positioning-engine ports / OpenType introspection tools don't have to reach into `get_raw_table()`. Lookup-type-2 pair-adjustment kerning (`get_kerning(left_gid, right_gid)`) covers both Format 1 (per-glyph PairSet) and Format 2 (Class1×Class2 matrix) subtables; types 1, 3-9 are surfaced via the structural accessors but not engine-applied — same stop-short shape as upstream's hypothetical `GposData` projection. **No upstream `GlyphPositioningTableTest.java` exists** — the upstream port file is a placeholder mirroring spirit-port shape used by `GlyphSubstitutionTableTest`.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/glyph_substitution_table.py` (NEW): `GlyphSubstitutionTable(TTFTable)` wrapper around fontTools' `GSUB` table. **`get_gsub_data()` always returns `None`** — upstream's `GsubData` projection is built atop a bespoke `org.apache.fontbox.ttf.model.{GsubData, Language, ScriptFeature, MapBackedScriptFeature}` value-class graph not ported here; callers needing structured access use `get_raw_table()` to reach the fontTools GSUB instance. **`get_substitution()` applies single-substitution lookups only** (lookup type 1) — types 2-4 (multiple/alternate/ligature) and 5-8 (contextual/extension) are skipped (upstream supports type 7 wrap-and-redispatch; pypdfbox does not since fontTools inlines extension subtables). `selectScriptTag()` lacks `OpenTypeScript.INHERITED` / `TAG_DEFAULT` constants — approximated with literal `"DFLT"` check until `OpenTypeScript` is ported. Upstream `GlyphSubstitutionTableTest.testGetGsubData` is ported in spirit only — the original asserts `GsubData` shape against `Lohit-Bengali.ttf` + golden tables; pypdfbox port asserts `get_supported_script_tags` / `get_supported_feature_tags` against the existing `LiberationSans-Regular.ttf` fixture.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/digital_signature_table.py` (NEW): `DigitalSignatureTable(TTFTable)` wrapper around fontTools' `DSIG` table. Exposes a richer accessor surface than upstream (`get_version`, `get_num_signatures`, `get_flag`, `get_signature_blocks`, `get_signature_block`, `populate_from_fonttools`) — upstream is a near-empty placeholder declaring only `TAG`. `TrueTypeFont.get_dsig()` lazy + cached, mirrors `get_header()` pattern.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/cff/type2_char_string.py` (NEW): `Type2CharString` thin wrapper around `fontTools.misc.psCharStrings.T2CharString`. Constructor signature mirrors upstream (`font, font_name, glyph_name, gid, sequence, default_width_x, nominal_width_x`); accepts a fontTools `T2CharString`, raw bytecode, a program-token list, or `None`. Public surface: `get_gid` / `get_name` / `get_font_name` / `get_default_width_x` / `get_nominal_width_x` / `get_width` (via `T2WidthExtractor`) / `get_path` (via fontTools' BasePen) / `get_bounds` / `t2` property. All opcode interpretation, subroutine recursion, hint masks, flex/hflex/hflex1/flex1 expansion delegated to fontTools — the private `convertType1ToType2`, `convertType2Command`, `clearStack`, `expandStemHints`, `markPath`, `closeCharString2Path`, `addAlternatingLine/Curve`, `addCurve`, `addCommandList`, `split` helpers are intentionally not ported. `get_path()` returns draw-command tuples rather than `java.awt.geom.GeneralPath`; `get_width()` returns `float`. `CFFFont.get_type2_char_string(out_of_range_gid)` returns an empty wrapper rather than throwing — ergonomic deviation; callers detect via empty path.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/pd_prop_build.py` + `pd_prop_build_data_dict.py` (NEW): typed `PDPropBuild` (`/Filter`, `/PubSec`, `/App` sub-dict accessors) + `PDPropBuildDataDict` (Name/Date/REx-Version/R-Revision/V-MinimumRevision/PreRelease/OS/NonEFontNoWarn/TrustedMode). Setters accept `None` to remove (Python-side convenience, behavior-compatible when given a value). `get_revision()` / `get_minimum_revision()` return Python `int` (unbounded, vs upstream `long`); missing-key default `-1`. `PDSignature.get_prop_build()` / `set_prop_build()` wired in.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/image/pd_image_x_object.py`: `is_stencil()` / `set_stencil(b)` upstream-`PDImage`-interface aliases added on top of existing `is_image_mask` / `set_image_mask`. `get_mask()` / `set_mask()` / `get_color_key_mask()` / `set_color_key_mask()` / `get_soft_mask()` / `set_soft_mask()` confirmed already present (prior wave) — `get_mask()` returns `None` for the COSArray (color-key) form; `get_color_key_mask()` returns `None` for the COSStream form. `getStencilMaskColorSpace` does not exist in upstream PDFBox 3.0.x — correctly skipped.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/optionalcontent/pd_optional_content_group_usage.py` (NEW): typed `PDOptionalContentGroupUsage` wrapper for the OCG `/Usage` sub-dict per PDF 32000-1 §8.11.4.4 Table 102 — no direct upstream class (Apache PDFBox returns the raw `COSDictionary`). Per-sub-dict wrappers `PDUsageCreatorInfo`, `PDUsageLanguage`, `PDUsageExport`, `PDUsageZoom`, `PDUsagePrint`, `PDUsageView`, `PDUsageUser`, `PDUsagePageElement` alias the underlying `COSDictionary` (no copying) so writes round-trip through the parent OCG dict; legacy `PDOptionalContentGroup.set_usage_view_state()` etc. and the new typed wrapper see the same state. State setters validate `ON` / `OFF` and normalise lowercase. `PDUsageZoom.min` / `max` surface `None` when missing rather than baking in PDF-spec defaults (0 / +∞). `PDUsageUser.name` handles both string and array-of-string forms (Table 102 allows either). `PDOptionalContentGroup.get_usage()` returns the new typed wrapper or `None`; `get_usage_dict()` exposes the raw upstream-shaped accessor; `get_or_create_usage()` materialises `/Usage` lazily for write-side ergonomics.

## Wave 29 — 20 parallel agents: structure attribute objects, PDF 2.0 catalog plumbing, fontbox cmap promotion, signature seed-values, tools, content-stream engine, inline images

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_structure_class_map.py` (NEW): typed `PDStructureClassMap` extracted from the upstream-inline `getClassMap`/`setClassMap` block on `PDStructureTreeRoot`. `get_class_definitions()` returns `dict[str, list[PDAttributeObject]]`; `get_class(name)` returns `[]` for missing keys (uniform iteration); `add_class()` promotes a single-`COSDictionary` entry to a `COSArray` automatically when a second attribute is added under the same name. `PDStructureTreeRoot.get_class_map()` now returns `PDStructureClassMap | None` (was `dict[str, Any]`); setter accepts the typed wrapper, a `dict`, or `None`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/taggedpdf/pd_user_property.py` (NEW): typed `PDUserProperty` wrapper around `/N` / `/V` / `/F` / `/H`. Located in `taggedpdf` for proximity to `PDUserAttributeObject` (upstream sits in `logicalstructure`). `set_name` stores `/N` as `COSString` rather than upstream's `COSName` — ISO 32000-1 §14.8.5 specifies user-property name as a *text string*; reader accepts either form for back-compat. `__hash__` is identity-based since the underlying dictionary is mutable. `PDUserAttributeObject` gained typed `get_owner_user_properties()` / `set_user_properties` / `add_user_property` / `remove_user_property` / `user_property_changed`; the existing dict-form surface is preserved unchanged for back-compat.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/markedcontent/pd_marked_content.py` + `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/taggedpdf/pd_artifact_marked_content.py` (NEW, fallback target): substitute for the requested `PDOwnerProperties` (verified absent in upstream — concept is just `/O` name in attribute objects, already covered by `PDStandardAttributeObject` / `PDUserAttributeObject`). `PDMarkedContent` accepts `Any` for `add_text(text)` / `add_x_object(xobject)` since the `text` cluster (TextPosition) and graphics-XObject cluster (PDXObject) have not landed yet. `PDArtifactMarkedContent.get_b_box` (camelCase→snake_case mapping `getBBox` → `get_b_b_ox` collapsed to `get_b_box`).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_developer_extension.py` (NEW): typed `PDDeveloperExtension` wrapper for catalog `/Extensions` per PDF 32000-1 §7.12.2 / ISO 32000-2 §7.12.3. **No upstream Java class in PDFBox 3.0 or trunk** — only the COSName constants `BASE_VERSION` / `EXTENSION_LEVEL` / `EXTENSIONS` exist upstream. Wired into `PDDocumentCatalog.get_developer_extensions()` / `set_developer_extensions()` / `add_developer_extension()` / `remove_developer_extension()`. The `/URL` field is ISO 32000-2-only.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_default_attribute_object.py` + `pd_parent_tree_value.py` (NEW, fallback target): substitute for the requested `PDDocumentRequirements` (verified absent in upstream — `/Requirements` is left as raw COSArray with no helper class upstream). `PDDefaultAttributeObject.get_attribute_value(name)` collapses upstream's public/protected `getAttributeValue(name)` and `getAttributeValue(name, default)` overloads into a single Python method with default kwarg. `PDParentTreeValue` validates the constructor argument as `COSArray | COSDictionary` and raises `TypeError` (upstream uses overloaded constructors for compile-time enforcement).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/page_layout.py` + `page_mode.py` (NEW): `PageLayout` and `PageMode` ported as `enum.StrEnum` (upstream uses Java typed enum). The `StrEnum` choice is the deliberate deviation that lets enum members compare equal to their underlying PDF name strings — required for back-compat with existing pre-typed callers/tests that pass and assert plain strings. `PDDocumentCatalog.get_page_layout()` / `get_page_mode()` return type widened from `str | None` to `PageLayout | None` / `PageMode | None`; setters accept the enum or the raw PDF name string. `from_string()` raises `ValueError` instead of `IllegalArgumentException`. Unrecognised dictionary names map to `None` (tolerant catalog read posture matching upstream).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_appearance_content_stream.py` (NEW): `PDAppearanceContentStream` extends the lite `PDPageContentStream` rather than a separate `PDAbstractContentStream` base; constructor bypasses parent's PDPage/PDFormXObject branching because `PDAppearanceStream` does not yet inherit from `PDFormXObject` (deferred to rendering cluster). `PDAppearanceStream` gained `get_stream()` / `get_resources()` / `set_resources()` to support the writer; full `PDFormXObject` inheritance still deferred. Adds `set_stroking_color_on_demand`, `set_non_stroking_color_on_demand`, `set_stroking_color(components)`, `set_non_stroking_color(components)`, `set_border_line` (BS dashed/solid + array dash with PDFBOX-5266 fallback), `set_line_width_on_demand`, `draw_shape`, `get_appearance`. Located under `interactive/annotation` for cohesion with `PDAppearanceStream` (upstream sits at the `pdmodel` root).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pd_destination_or_action.py` (NEW): concrete marker class with static `create(value)` dispatcher (Python has no interface-only construct). Arrays/names/strings → `PDDestination.create`; dicts → `PDAction.create`; `None` / other → `None`. `PDDestination` and `PDAction` do not subclass `PDDestinationOrAction` to keep their inheritance chains intact — use `is_destination_or_action(value)` for the upstream `instanceof` idiom. `PDDocumentCatalog.get_open_action` now delegates to this dispatcher (was inlining the dispatch); behaviour unchanged.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/pd_seed_value_certificate.py` + `pd_seed_value_mdp.py` (NEW): typed `PDSeedValueCertificate` (`/Cert` sub-dict — `/Subject` array, `/SubjectDN`, `/KeyUsage` with `add_key_usage` + `add_key_usage_chars` (renamed from upstream's char-overload), `/Issuer`, `/OID`, `/URL`, `/URLType`, six `/Ff`-flag pairs, `FLAG_*` constants) + typed `PDSeedValueMDP` (`/MDP` — `get_p` / `set_p` range-validated 0..3 raising `ValueError`). `PDSeedValue.get_seed_value_certificate()` and `get_mdp()` return typed wrappers (was raw `COSDictionary`); setters accept either form. Added short aliases `get_certificate()` / `set_certificate()` on `PDSeedValue` (not present upstream); also `set_mpd()` mirroring upstream's typo'd `setMPD`.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/cmap/cid_range.py` (NEW; promoted from private `_CIDRange`): public typed `CIDRange` class. Backwards-compat alias `_CIDRange = CIDRange` retained in `cmap.py`. `pypdfbox/fontbox/cmap/bf_char_entry.py` and `bf_char_range.py` (NEW, original): typed value objects for ToUnicode `bfchar` / `bfrange` triples — **no upstream counterparts** (upstream `CMapParser` inlines these into `CMap.addCharMapping`). `BFCharRange` supports both forms (single target with last-codepoint increment, or explicit per-code list); iterable, materialises into `BFCharEntry`s.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_font_descriptor.py`: enrichment — added `set_font_bounding_box(PDRectangle)`, `get_average_width` / `set_average_width` upstream-named aliases for `get/set_avg_width`, `set_character_set` alias, `has_widths()` / `has_missing_width()` predicates, `get_cid_set` / `set_cid_set` (`/CIDSet` stream), `get_panose()` returning a new `PDPanose` 10-byte wrapper (`/Style/Panose`), `get_lang` / `set_lang` (PDF 32000-1 Table 122 — *not present in upstream PDFBox 3.0*, surfaced as a deliberate pypdfbox extension). Applied PDFBOX-429 `abs()` workaround to `get_cap_height` / `get_x_height` (was returning raw value, now matches upstream Java behaviour). New public class `PDPanose` (mirrors upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.font.PDPanose`) — minimal port: 10-byte payload, `get_bytes`, `get_family_class`, `get_serif_style`. Per-byte category accessors deferred to font-subsetting cluster.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_viewer_preferences.py`: no changes required — existing implementation already exceeds upstream PDFBox 3.0 surface (upstream has no `PickTrayByPDFSize` / `NumCopies` / `PrintPageRange` / `Enforce` accessors; pypdfbox already exposes them as PDF 32000-1 §12.2 / 32000-2 enrichment).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_output_intent.py`: enrichment — added `(document, color_profile)` constructor mirroring upstream `PDOutputIntent(PDDocument, InputStream)` (auto-derives `/N` from ICC colour-space signature bytes 16–19 per ICC.1:2010 §7.2 Table 18 with optional `num_components` override; embeds the ICC blob as flate-encoded `PDStream` under `/DestOutputProfile`). Added `get_dest_output_intent()` upstream-named alias returning the raw `COSStream`. Added PDF 2.0 / ISO 32000-2 §14.11.5 typed accessors `get_dest_output_profile_ref()` / `set_dest_output_profile_ref()` (not in upstream 3.0). Internal `_configure_output_profile()` mirrors upstream private helper; `_icc_num_components()` parses the ICC colour-space signature.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/exif_schema.py` (NEW, lite): `ExifSchema` (`exif:` namespace `http://ns.adobe.com/exif/1.0/`). Simple-typed properties only. Rational-typed properties (CompressedBitsPerPixel, ExposureTime, FNumber, ShutterSpeedValue, ApertureValue, BrightnessValue, ExposureBiasValue, MaxApertureValue, SubjectDistance, FlashEnergy, FocalLength, FocalPlaneXResolution, FocalPlaneYResolution, ExposureIndex, DigitalZoomRatio, GPSAltitude, GPSDOP, GPSSpeed, GPSTrack, GPSImgDirection, GPSDestBearing, GPSDestDistance) — constants exposed; accessors omitted until `RationalType` lands. GPSCoordinate properties (GPSLatitude, GPSLongitude, GPSDestLatitude, GPSDestLongitude) — constants only. Typed-struct properties (OECF, SpatialFrequencyResponse, CFAPattern, Flash, DeviceSettingDescription) — constants only. Wired into `XMPMetadata` + parser registry.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/tiff_schema.py` (NEW, substitute target): `TiffSchema` (`tiff:` namespace `http://ns.adobe.com/tiff/1.0/`). Substitute for the requested `CameraRawSchema` — verified absent in PDFBox 3.0.x's xmpbox. Simple-typed properties; Rational properties (XResolution / YResolution / WhitePoint / PrimaryChromaticities / YCbCrCoefficients / ReferenceBlackWhite) stored as upstream's `"num/den"` text form pending a `RationalType` typed-struct port. Wired into `XMPMetadata` + parser registry.
- `pypdfbox/tools/extracttext.py` (NEW): port of upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.tools.ExtractText` (PicoCLI → argparse). Surfaces `-i/--input`, `-o/--output`, `-password`, `-encoding`, `-startPage`, `-endPage`, `-sort`, `-console`, `-addFileName`, `-append`. Permission gate via `get_current_access_permission().can_extract_content()`. Omitted upstream flags: `-html`, `-md`, `-rotationMagic`, `-debug`, `-alwaysNext`, `-ignoreBeads`, embedded-PDF extraction (needs `PDDocumentNameDictionary` enumerable).
- `pypdfbox/tools/encrypt.py` (NEW): port of upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.tools.Encrypt`. Default `-keyLength=256`. PicoCLI's "boolean defaulting to true" `-canX` flags surfaced as paired `-canX` / `--no-canX` argparse switches (semantics unchanged). `-canPrintFaithful` maps to `AccessPermission.set_can_print_degraded` (the spec bit underpinning faithful/high-quality printing — same as upstream). Cert loading uses `cryptography.x509.load_der_x509_certificate` with PEM fallback (Java `CertificateFactory.generateCertificate` sniffs both). Re-encrypting an already-encrypted file emits the upstream "Document is already encrypted" message and exits 0.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/pdf_graphics_stream_engine.py` (NEW): abstract `PDFGraphicsStreamEngine` subclass of `PDFStreamEngine` registering all standard graphics/path/clip/paint/state/colour/text/marked-content/image operator processors and forwarding path-construction (`m`, `l`, `c`, `v`, `y`, `re`, `h`), painting (`S`, `s`, `f`, `F`, `f*`, `B`, `B*`, `b`, `b*`, `n`), clip (`W`, `W*`), shading (`sh`), and graphics-state save/restore (`q`, `Q`) to abstract hook methods (`move_to`, `line_to`, `curve_to`, `append_rectangle`, `close_path`, `stroke_path`, `fill_path`, `fill_and_stroke_path`, `end_path`, `clip`, `shading_fill`, `draw_image`, `get_current_point`). `WIND_NON_ZERO` / `WIND_EVEN_ODD` exposed as plain int constants (no `java.awt.geom.Path2D` dependency). Added `get_page()` and an overridable `transformed_point(x, y)` helper. `PDFRenderer` left untouched — it overrides `process_operator` entirely with its own dispatch table; rewiring would force it to provide stubs for hooks that never fire. `PDFGraphicsStreamEngine` is in place for future use by tools/extractors and a future renderer rewrite.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/pd_property_list.py`: enrichment — fixed `create()` to return a bare `PDPropertyList(dictionary)` for unknown / missing `/Type` (was returning `None`), matching upstream's `else` branch. Added re-export module `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/markedcontent/pd_property_list.py` aliasing the implementation at the upstream-canonical Java package path. `get_metadata()` / `set_metadata()` accessors **deliberately not added** — upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.documentinterchange.markedcontent.PDPropertyList` (3.0 branch) has no such methods; CLAUDE.md rule "Do not invent abstractions" overrides the task wording.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/image/pd_inline_image.py` (NEW): port of upstream `PDInlineImage`. Constructor takes `(parameters, data, resources)` with eager filter-chain decode through `FilterFactory.INSTANCE.get_filter(...)` and `parameters.add_all(decode_result.parameters)` repair step. Two-key (short/long) lookups for `/W /Width`, `/H /Height`, `/BPC /BitsPerComponent`, `/CS /ColorSpace`, `/F /Filter`, `/D /Decode`, `/IM /ImageMask`, `/I /Interpolate`. `get_color_space()` with short-name expansion (`/G→/DeviceGray`, `/RGB→/DeviceRGB`, `/CMYK→/DeviceCMYK`) + `/I` and `/Indexed` array rebuild; stencil fallback to `PDDeviceGray.INSTANCE`; raises `OSError` (project Java `IOException` mapping) when missing on non-stencil. `get_image()` / `get_stencil_image()` / `get_raw_raster()` / `get_raw_image()` not ported — replaced with `to_pil_image()` (DCT/JPX + raw 8-bit DeviceGray/DeviceRGB only); full sampled-image decoding lands with the rendering cluster. **BI/ID/EI operator stubs left as no-ops** — full engine integration of inline-image construction (the `show_inline_image` hook on the stream engine) deferred to the rendering-cluster wave.

## Wave 30 — 20 parallel agents: marked-content extractor, multipdf, function eval round-out, font mappers, threads, renderer text, more tools

- `pypdfbox/text/pdf_marked_content_extractor.py` (NEW): `PDFMarkedContentExtractor` subclasses `PDFTextStripper` rather than upstream's `LegacyPDFStreamEngine` — pypdfbox's stripper already owns the parser walk and font/CMap caches. `process_page` returns `""` (upstream returns `void`) so subclassing is type-stable; call `get_marked_contents()` to retrieve results. BDC/DP property operand resolution: inline `COSDictionary` used directly; `COSName` operand resolved through `PDResources.get_property_list(name).get_cos_object()`. Constructor accepts an optional `encoding` argument for API parity but ignores it — pypdfbox decodes via `/ToUnicode` + `/Differences` rather than Java's encoding-name conversion path.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/pd_function_type3.py`: stale "selection / eval is deferred" docstring replaced — the eval was already implemented (partition selection, encode interpolation, single-function degenerate case, input/output clipping, multi-output dispatch all match upstream). 14 new hand-written eval tests added.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/pd_function_type4.py`: opcode coverage round-out — fixed `_op_not` to arithmetic-negate ints (matching upstream PDFBox 3.0's `BitwiseOperators$Not`) instead of bitwise complement; deliberate spec divergence in favour of upstream parity per CLAUDE.md "Behavior over style". 66 new hand-written tests + 33 ported from `TestOperators.java` (skipping Java integer-overflow checks since Python ints are unbounded, and `instanceof Float` vs `Integer` type-distinction checks since pypdfbox collapses to `float` on output).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_content_stream.py`: 6 text-positioning operators added — `move_text_position_by_amount(x, y)` → `Td` (alias for existing `new_line_at_offset`), `move_text_position_and_set_leading(x, y)` → `TD`, `move_to_next_line()` → `T*` (alias for existing `new_line`), `move_to_next_line_show_text(text)` → `'`, `set_spacings_show_text(word_spacing, char_spacing, text)` → `"`, `show_text_with_positioning(items)` → `[...] TJ` (accepts `list[str | bytes | int | float]`; numbers emit position adjustments in 1/1000 em). `show_text` decomposed into `_show_text_internal` helper mirroring upstream's `showTextInternal`. PDFBox 1.x / 2.x legacy method names (`move_text_position_by_amount` etc.) added alongside the 3.0 canonical names (`new_line_at_offset` etc.) so callers porting from any PDFBox era find a working name.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/font_box_font.py` + `font_mapping.py` + `font_mappers.py` + `font_mapper.py` (NEW): FontMapper cluster. `FontBoxFont` is a runtime-checkable Protocol. `FontMapping[T]` exposes both snake_case and camelCase getters (`get_font` / `getFont`, `is_fallback` / `isFallback`). `FontMappers` static registry with `instance()`, `set(...)`, `setMapper(...)`, `reset()` — `set(None)` and `reset()` are pypdfbox extensions for test isolation. **Default mapper trimmed to Standard 14** — upstream `FontMapperImpl` (~1500 LOC) walks system font directories via `FileSystemFontProvider`. The pypdfbox default returns `None` from `get_true_type_font` / `get_open_type_font` and resolves `get_font_box_font` against the bundled AFMs only (with a style-flag fallback). Apps wanting full system-font enumeration plug a custom mapper via `FontMappers.set(...)`. **Package layout deviation**: upstream Java puts `FontMapper` / `FontMapping` / `FontMappers` under `org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.font`; only `FontBoxFont` is genuinely fontbox-side. pypdfbox hosts all four under `pypdfbox/fontbox/` since Python has no module-cycle problem between fontbox and pdmodel. `PDFontFactory` gained `get_font_mapper()` / `set_font_mapper(...)` / `find_font_box_font(base_font, font_descriptor)` wired through `FontMappers.instance()`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/pdfdoc_encoding.py` (NEW): full 256-entry PDFDocEncoding ↔ Unicode tables per ISO 32000-1 §D.3 Table D.2. Module-level functions `decode_bytes`, `encode_bytes`, `contains_char`, `get_char_code`, plus a `PDFDocEncoding` class with classmethod parity for upstream-name calls. Relocated from upstream's `cos` package to `pdmodel/common` per task brief; upstream class is package-private. **`COSString` integration**: `COSString.__init__(str)` now mirrors upstream — PDFDocEncoding when all chars are representable, else UTF-16BE with FE FF BOM. `get_string()` decodes via real PDFDocEncoding (was latin-1 approximation per the now-removed comment).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/encoding/built_in_encoding.py` (NEW): `BuiltInEncoding(Encoding)`. Constructor takes `dict[int, str]` and seeds the parent encoding via `add()` (preserves `Map.putIfAbsent` reverse-mapping semantics). `get_encoding_name()` returns `"built-in (TTF)"`. `get_cos_object()` raises `NotImplementedError("Built-in encodings cannot be serialized")` — closest Python analogue to upstream's `UnsupportedOperationException`. Integration into `PDSimpleFont` / `PDType1Font` / `PDType3Font` deferred to a follow-up wave that touches font-program parsing.
- `pypdfbox/multipdf/__init__.py` + `overlay.py` (NEW): full port of `Overlay`. Mirrors upstream's `Position` enum, all setters, `overlay()` / `overlay_documents(map)` entry points, `Closeable` semantics. `calculate_affine_transform` overridable and uses **real lower-left corner** of both page and overlay MediaBoxes (PDFBOX-6048 alignment per CLAUDE.md), not (0, 0). Page rotation handling via `_create_adjusted_layout_page` (PDFBOX-6049). Library-first I/O via `pypdfbox.io.io_utils.copy` and stdlib `logging`. Three rendering-comparison tests from `OverlayTest.java` skipped — depend on bundled fixture PDFs (`OverlayTestBaseRot0.pdf`, `rot{0,90,180,270}.pdf`, `PDFBOX-6049-*.pdf`) and the rendering cluster (PRD §6.12) which isn't yet built.
- `pypdfbox/multipdf/pdf_clone_utility.py` (NEW): `PDFCloneUtility(dest_doc)` with `clone_for_new_document()`, `get_destination()`, `clone_merge()`, plus private `_has_self_reference()` and per-type cloners. **Identity-keyed maps**: upstream uses `HashMap<COSBase, COSBase>` with object-identity semantics; pypdfbox uses `id(obj)` as the key to avoid relying on `COSBase.__eq__` overrides (`COSObject` is value-equal by `(num, gen)`). **Cycle protection**: destination clone registered in `_cloned_version[id(src)]` *before* iterating children, mirroring upstream's early `clonedVersion.put(...)` inside `cloneCOSDictionary`/`cloneCOSStream`. **Stream body copy**: `pypdfbox.io.copy()` over `create_raw_input_stream` / `create_raw_output_stream`, guarded with `stream.has_data()` because pypdfbox's `create_raw_input_stream` raises `OSError` on empty streams (upstream Java permits zero-length read silently). **Logging**: stdlib `logging.getLogger(__name__)` instead of commons-logging (CLAUDE.md PDFBox 4.0 alignment). `clone_merge` accepts duck-typed objects exposing `get_cos_object()` since pypdfbox doesn't have a `COSObjectable` base class.
- `pypdfbox/multipdf/layer_utility.py` (NEW): full port of `LayerUtility`. `wrap_in_save_restore`, `import_page_as_form` (both int and `PDPage` overloads), `append_form_as_layer(target_page, form, transform, layer_name)`. **Java's `AffineTransform` replaced** with inline 6-tuple helpers (`_at_translate`, `_at_scale`, `_at_quadrant_rotate`) — no float drift via `sin`/`cos` on quadrant rotates. Upstream calls `targetDoc.getDocument().createCOSStream()`; pypdfbox constructs `COSStream(scratch_file)` directly since `COSDocument` doesn't expose a `create_cos_stream()` factory. Upstream test's full save-then-reload + Standard14 font path simplified — fonts and `CompressParameters.NO_COMPRESSION` not yet ported, so the upstream test asserts directly on in-memory COS graphs (catalog `/OCProperties` + page `/Resources/Properties`) rather than disk round-trip. PDFBOX-5232 ("never-ended marked content") still exercised by re-running `import_page_as_form` on the just-modified document.
- `pypdfbox/multipdf/page_extractor.py` (NEW): `PageExtractor(source_doc, start_page=1, end_page=None)` with `extract() -> PDDocument`. Mirrors upstream clamping (`startPage<1 → 1`, `endPage>N → N`, `start>end → empty doc`). **Splitter delegation deferred**: upstream delegates to `Splitter` (not yet ported); pypdfbox falls back to direct page-tree append via existing `PDDocument.import_page`. User-visible contract — page counts, clamping rules, blank-doc-on-degenerate-range — matches upstream exactly.
