- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/taggedpdf/pd_layout_attribute_object.py`: Wave 41 round-out — full §14.8.5.4 typed surface. Added 32 upstream-parity public dictionary-key constants (`PLACEMENT`, `WRITING_MODE`, `BACKGROUND_COLOR`, …, `COLUMN_WIDTHS`) and the value-constant clusters for `LineHeight` (`LINE_HEIGHT_NORMAL`/`LINE_HEIGHT_AUTO`), `TextDecorationType` (4 values), `RubyAlign` (5 values), `RubyPosition` (4 values), and `GlyphOrientationVertical` (8 values). Eight new accessor pairs reach 100% parity with upstream Layout: `t_border_style` (single name OR 4-name array), `t_padding` (number OR 4-number array), `line_height` (number OR "Normal"/"Auto" sentinel — `set_line_height_normal`/`set_line_height_auto` convenience setters), `text_decoration_color` (RGB tuple), `text_decoration_thickness` (number, `UNSPECIFIED` default), `text_decoration_type`, `ruby_align` (default `Distribute`), `ruby_position` (default `Before`), `glyph_orientation_vertical` (default `Auto`). Upstream-parity setter aliases (`set_all_border_styles`/`set_border_styles`, `set_all_border_thicknesses`/`set_border_thicknesses`, `set_all_paddings`/`set_paddings`, `set_all_t_border_styles`/`set_t_border_styles`, `set_all_t_paddings`/`set_t_paddings`, `set_all_column_widths`, `set_column_gaps`) collapse Java's overloaded `setAllXxx(scalar)` / `setXxxs(array)` pair onto Python while preserving both upstream names. `OWNER_LAYOUT` constant added alongside the existing pypdfbox-style `OWNER`. The legacy polymorphic single-arg setters (`set_border_style`, `set_t_padding`, etc.) are preserved unchanged for prior callers.
- `pypdfbox/multipdf/pdf_merger_utility.py` + `tests/multipdf/test_merger_struct_tree.py` (NEW): Wave 41 round-out — structure-tree edge-case hand-tests covering the upstream `PDFMergerUtility` policies that aren't exercised by the broader happy-path suite. New tests pin down: (1) **/RoleMap conflict** — same key, different mapping → destination wins, one warning emitted (verifies upstream `mergeRoleMap`); identical-value collisions stay silent. (2) **MCID-indexed parent-tree leaves** — when a source page's parent-tree leaf is a `COSArray` keyed by MCID (the page-typed shape per ISO 32000-1 §14.7.4.4), the array is cloned wholesale into the destination at the offset key with each child's `/Pg` rewritten to the destination page (`_update_page_references_array` → `_update_page_references_dict`). (3) **/Pg rewriting** — every cloned struct-elem dict points at the destination page dictionary, never the (now-closed) source page. (4) **`set_destination_document_information` / `set_destination_metadata`** — caller-provided overrides win over /Info / /Metadata carried in from the first source. (5) **`set_acro_form_merge_mode(JOIN_FORM_FIELDS_MODE | PDFBOX_LEGACY_MODE)`** — `LEGACY` renames same-named fields to `dummyFieldNameN`; `JOIN` keeps both names verbatim (verifies the `_merge_acro_form` dispatch). (6) **/IDTree collision** — same `/ID` in both sources → dest wins, source dropped, warning logged (mirrors upstream `mergeIDTree`). **MCID renumbering is intentionally NOT performed** — MCIDs are per-page-local indices; each imported page becomes a new destination page with its own MCID space, so existing MCID values in /K children remain valid as long as /Pg references are rewritten (which they are). The merger implementation didn't change in this round-out — only test coverage was extended; the upstream-test file `tests/multipdf/upstream/test_pdf_merger_utility.py` has its `test_structure_tree_merge_*` skip reasons updated to point at the synthetic equivalents.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/pd_seed_value.py` + `pd_seed_value_time_stamp.py`: Wave 41 round-out — PDSeedValue cluster parity. **PDSeedValue**: `get_v` / `set_v` switched from `int` to `float` to match upstream `getV()` / `setV(float)` (PDF 32000-1 §12.7.4.5 — `/V` is a number, written via `setFloat` upstream; the original lite port stored an integer). New `is_v_required()` / `set_v_required()` flag-bit pair (was missing despite the corresponding `_FLAG_V` bit position already being defined). `FLAG_FILTER` / `FLAG_SUBFILTER` / `FLAG_V` / `FLAG_REASON` / `FLAG_LEGAL_ATTESTATION` / `FLAG_ADD_REV_INFO` / `FLAG_DIGEST_METHOD` constants exposed on the class for upstream parity. No-arg constructor now calls `set_direct(True)` on the wrapped dictionary, mirroring upstream's `dictionary.setDirect(true)`. **PDSeedValueTimeStamp**: added `is_timestamp_required()` / `set_timestamp_required()` aliases matching upstream's exact method names — semantics differ subtly from the existing `is_url_required` / `set_url_required` bit-mask pair: `set_timestamp_required(True)` writes `/Ff = 1` (or `0` for false) per upstream's `getInt(COSName.FF, 0) != 0` / `setInt(COSName.FF, flag ? 1 : 0)`, treating `/Ff` as a single boolean integer rather than a bitfield. Both pairs are kept; the bitfield API is the original pypdfbox surface and the integer API is the upstream-named alias. **Tests**: hand-written coverage extended (V-required bit position, `set_v` float / int round-trip / None-clear, FLAG_* constants matching upstream, default Type=SV+direct check, timestamp_required round-trip, nonzero-Ff timestamp_required semantics, both flag pairs reading the same `/Ff`). PDFBox 3.0 ships no `PDSeedValue*Test.java` upstream — verified 2026-04-27 against the `apache/pdfbox` `3.0` branch — so `tests/.../upstream/test_pd_seed_value.py` is a sentinel stub.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/optionalcontent/pd_optional_content_configuration.py` (NEW) + `pd_optional_content_properties.py`: Wave 41 round-out — split the /D (and /Configs) configuration shape onto a typed `PDOptionalContentConfiguration` wrapper (no upstream class — Apache PDFBox inlines the same accessors on `PDOptionalContentProperties`). New typed surface: `get_name`/`set_name`, `get_creator`/`set_creator`, `get_base_state`/`set_base_state`, `get_intent`/`set_intent` (string OR list, default "View"), `get_intents` (raw list), `get_on`/`get_off` (typed OCG lists), `get_order`/`set_order`, `get_rbgroups`/`add_rbgroup`/`get_rbgroup_for(group)`, `get_locked`/`is_locked`/`set_locked`/`add_locked`, `get_as_array`/`add_as_entry(event, categories, ocgs)`. **Behaviour change** vs upstream: `PDOptionalContentProperties.set_group_enabled(group, True)` now enforces /RBGroups — turning one OCG ON forces every sibling in the same radio-button group to OFF (PDF 32000-1 Table 101). Apache PDFBox stores /RBGroups but does not actively enforce the toggle in `setGroupEnabled`; pypdfbox does because Acrobat does. Disabling does *not* trigger sibling enforcement. Also new on `PDOptionalContentProperties`: `get_default_configuration()` (typed wrapper around /D), `get_configurations()` / `get_configuration(name)` / `add_configuration(cfg)` for /Configs, `get_intent`/`set_intent`, `get_rbgroups`/`add_rbgroup`, `get_locked`/`is_locked`/`set_locked`/`add_locked`, `is_group_visible(name_or_group)` alias for `is_group_enabled`. New tests under `tests/pdmodel/graphics/optionalcontent/test_pd_optional_content_configuration.py` + `test_pd_optional_content_rbgroups.py` (hand-written) and `tests/pdmodel/graphics/optionalcontent/upstream/test_optional_content_groups.py` (state-assertion subset of upstream `TestOptionalContentGroups.java` — content-stream + image-diff render phases skipped per per-test comment).
- `pypdfbox/multipdf/splitter.py`: Wave 41 round-out — signature widget filter and AcroForm scrub. New private static `_is_signature_widget(ann_dict)` classifies a Widget annotation as a signature widget when (a) the widget itself carries `/FT /Sig` (merged widget+field), (b) its `/Parent` chain ends in a `/FT /Sig` field, or (c) its `/V` resolves to a `/Type /Sig` dictionary or one carrying `/ByteRange`. Detected widgets are dropped from the cloned `/Annots` array in `_process_annotations` (split documents have a different byte range than the source so any contained signature would be invalid). New `_scrub_acroform(destination_document)` post-pass clears `/SigFlags`, removes `/FT /Sig` entries from `/AcroForm /Fields`, and drops `/AcroForm` entirely when nothing useful remains — defensive against subclasses that inject `/AcroForm` via an overridden `create_new_document`; the default chunk catalog still does not carry `/AcroForm` (matches upstream). CID font subset programs (`/FontFile2` / `/FontFile3`) survive the split unchanged: `PDDocument.import_page` already deep-copies the `/Resources` chain raw-bytes-verbatim via `COSStream.set_raw_data`, so no font-specific code is needed in the splitter (verified by new tests). Existing `set_split_at_page` / `set_split` / `set_start_page` / `set_end_page` setters confirmed already present from Wave 31. New tests: `tests/multipdf/test_splitter_signatures.py` (9 cases — merged widget / parent-chain / `/V` signature dict / `/V` byte-range / non-sig parent retention / AcroForm scrub via subclass / sig-field filtered from `/Fields` / default catalog has no AcroForm / save-reload round-trip), `tests/multipdf/test_splitter_cid_fonts.py` (4 cases — `/FontFile2` byte-equality after split, multi-chunk independence, save-reload round-trip, source-doc isolation after chunk mutation). Upstream-test placeholders under `tests/multipdf/upstream/test_splitter_{signatures,cid_fonts}.py` (PDFBox 3.0 has no dedicated `SplitterSignatureTest.java` / `SplitterCIDFontTest.java` — coverage is via `PDFMergerUtilityTest` fixtures we do not carry).
- `pypdfbox/tools/extracttext.py`: Wave 41 round-out — `-html`, `-md`, `-ignoreBeads`, `-debug` flags landed. Upstream's `-html` / `-md` route through `PDFText2HTML` / `PDFText2Markdown` subclasses of `PDFTextStripper`; pypdfbox does not ship those subclasses, so we collect the plain extracted text and wrap it in a minimal HTML (`<html><head><meta charset="UTF-8">…</head><body><pre>{escaped}</pre></body></html>`) or Markdown (fenced triple-backtick block) document. Default output extension follows the chosen wrapper (`.html` / `.md` / `.txt`). `-ignoreBeads` calls `PDFTextStripper.set_should_separate_by_beads(False)` (matches upstream verbatim now that the underlying knob is wired). `-debug` prints a single `debug: extracttext finished in {secs}s` line to stderr after the document closes (upstream uses a JUL `Logger` for per-page timings; we do not log per-page). **Behavioral note**: upstream's `-html` injects per-tag font-size / colour / fill annotations driven by the underlying glyph stream; pypdfbox's wrapper preserves whitespace via `<pre>` only — visual fidelity intentionally limited to the textual layer. `-rotationMagic` and the per-page extraction loop also accept `ignore_beads` end-to-end.
- `pypdfbox/tools/info.py`: Wave 41 round-out — `-password`, `-metadata` (XMP), `-output txt|json` flags landed. The Java upstream has no equivalent class (the existing `PDFInfo` / `PDFDebugger` flow is GUI), so the surface is pypdfbox-original. `-password` opens password-protected files (returns rc=1 on a wrong password). `-metadata` reads `PDDocumentCatalog.get_metadata()` and dumps the XMP packet via `PDMetadata.get_metadata_as_string()` (falls through to a raw-bytes UTF-8 decode if the XML decoder rejects the packet). `-output json` emits a deterministic single-object JSON document (sorted keys, indent=2) carrying `file` / `header_version` / `catalog_version` / `effective_version` / `pages` / `encrypted` / `info` (standard /Info keys with values populated) / `custom` (non-standard /Info keys) / `xmp` (only when `-metadata` is set). The `txt` path is unchanged for back-compat with the earlier `info` command output.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_output_intent.py`: Wave 41 round-out — new `get_n_for_profile()` helper reads `/N` from the embedded `/DestOutputProfile` (preferring the explicit integer entry, falling back to decoding the ICC header colour-space signature at bytes 16-19 — same answer upstream's `ICC_Profile.getNumComponents()` returns on a freshly-parsed profile). Existing `(PDDocument, profile)` constructor (already shipping the flate-compressed `PDStream` embed with `/N` from the ICC header) and the `/DestOutputProfileRef` PDF 2.0 typed accessors verified against upstream `PDOutputIntent.java` 3.0.x line-by-line — no other deltas. New parity-shaped `tests/.../upstream/test_pd_output_intent.py` (PDFBox 3.0 ships no dedicated `PDOutputIntentTest.java`, so the file targets the documented Java API contract: `/Type` + `/S = GTS_PDFA1`, flate filter on `/DestOutputProfile`, `/N` from header, string accessors round-trip).
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/pdfa_identification_schema.py`: Wave 41 round-out — typed accessor parity with upstream `PDFAIdentificationSchema.java`. `set_conformance(value)` now validates against `{A, B, U, e, f}` and raises new `BadFieldValueException` (subclass of `ValueError`) on invalid values, matching upstream PDFBOX-6088 (PDF/A-4 added `e` and `f`). New upstream-named methods: `set_part_value_with_int(int)`, `set_part_value_with_string(str)` (raises `ValueError` on garbage — mirrors upstream `IllegalArgumentException`), `set_rev_value_with_int(int)`, `set_rev_value_with_string(str)`, `set_rev(int)`, `get_rev()` (returns `int` post-PDFBOX-6088 — typed as `Integer` upstream); `get_amd` / `set_amd` aliases of `get_amendment` / `set_amendment`; `get_corr` / `set_corr` aliases of `get_correction` / `set_correction`. The string-flavoured `get_revision()` / `set_revision()` are kept for back-compat — `get_revision()` now stringifies a numeric int stored via `set_rev`. New `BadFieldValueException` exposed at `pypdfbox.xmpbox` package level. Upstream-ported tests in `tests/xmpbox/upstream/test_pdfa_identification_schema.py` translate `PDFAIdentificationOthersTest` (round-trip + bad-conformance + bad-version-id) and `PDFAIdentificationTest`'s parameterised value channel; the typed-field property accessors (`getPartProperty().getStringValue()`) and the `XmpSerializer` round-trip remain deferred — pypdfbox does not yet ship an upstream-shaped serializer, so the round-trip test path uses a hand-rolled XMP packet through the existing `DomXmpParser`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/pd_signature.py` + `sig_utils.py` + `pkcs7_signature.py`: Wave 41 round-out — digital-signature cluster parity. **PDSignature**: new `get_type` / `set_type` accessors (parity with upstream `getType` / `setType`) and `get_cert` / `set_cert` accessors for `/Cert` (used by `adbe.x509.rsa_sha1`); `set_cert` accepts either a single `str` (stored as COSString) or a `list[str]` (stored as COSArray of COSStrings) — `get_cert` always returns `list[str] | None` regardless of underlying storage. **`verify(document_bytes)` now performs a real digest-match check** rather than returning a deferred-feature stub: it recomputes the sha256/sha1 digest over `/ByteRange`, recovers the `messageDigest` signed-attribute (OID `1.2.840.113549.1.9.4`) from the PKCS#7 SignedData via a minimal hand-rolled DER walker, and sets `result.is_valid = True` only when the two digests match — flips to `False` with a `"digest mismatch"` error otherwise. **TODO** (deliberately deferred): full signature math over the signed-attributes + chain trust (cryptography's high-level `pkcs7` API is signing-only; we deliberately do not depend on `asn1crypto` per the §3.7.1 dep policy). `verify()` also `rstrip(b"\x00")`s the `/Contents` blob before parsing — real PDF writers zero-pad up to the placeholder width and the previous code emitted a `cryptography` BER-fallback warning on every verify call. **sig_utils**: three new pure helpers — `compute_byte_range(document_bytes, contents_open, contents_close)` (returns the four-tuple `[start1, len1, start2, len2]` for a `/Contents <…>` placeholder per ISO 32000-1 §12.8.1, including the angle brackets in the hashed range), `compute_signed_digest(document_bytes, byte_range, *, algorithm="sha256")` (concatenates the two slices and hashes them), `extract_pkcs7_message_digest(pkcs7_der)` (DER scanner returning the SHA digest the PKCS#7 SignedData was signed over, or `None` when malformed). **Pkcs7Signature**: top-level `cryptography` import replaced with a lazy `_import_cryptography()` helper that re-throws `ImportError` as `RuntimeError` with an actionable install hint, so `import pypdfbox.pdmodel.interactive.digitalsignature` does not fail on a stripped install (signing requires `cryptography`; verification's cert-extraction path also requires it but is now guarded inline). New tests across `test_pd_signature.py` (Type/Cert/SignDate/byte-range-validation), `test_sig_utils.py` (`compute_byte_range` brackets-inclusive math + edge cases, `compute_signed_digest` sha256/sha1 + wrong-size rejection, `extract_pkcs7_message_digest` short-form / long-form / indefinite-length / truncated-blob cases) and `test_signature_verification.py` (end-to-end PKCS#7 sign-then-verify happy path + tampering-detected mismatch path using a self-signed RSA key). Upstream-test placeholders under `tests/.../digitalsignature/upstream/test_pd_signature.py` / `test_pd_prop_build.py` / `test_signature_verification.py` (PDFBox 3.0 ships no JUnit class for any — verified 2026-04-27 against `apache/pdfbox` `3.0`; verification path is exercised upstream via `pdfbox-examples`'s `ShowSignatureTest.java`).
- `tests/multipdf/test_pdf_clone_utility.py`: Wave 42 round-out — `PDFCloneUtility` parity-test suite extended with five hand-tests targeting the upstream-task scope items not previously covered by direct assertions. (1) **/Resources subdict recursion** — building a synthetic `/Resources` dict carrying `/Font`, `/XObject`, `/Pattern`, `/Shading`, `/ColorSpace`, `/ExtGState`, `/Properties` subdictionaries and asserting each is independently cloned and reachable from the cloned root (the generic `_clone_cos_dictionary` recursion handles every Resources subtype — no bespoke per-key codepath needed, matching upstream `PDFCloneUtility.java` which is also purely structural). (2) **/AP appearance dict** — annotation with `/AP` carrying `/N` + `/R` + `/D` Form-XObject streams; cloned streams are distinct instances with body bytes preserved. (3) **/A action + /Dest** — annotation with action-dict + named-dest array; both clone deeply with their inner shape preserved. (4) **Stream raw-bytes preservation** — a stream tagged `/Filter /FlateDecode` with hand-crafted zlib bytes round-trips byte-for-byte through `clone_for_new_document`, confirming the cloner copies *raw* (already-filtered) body bytes via `create_raw_input_stream → io.copy → create_raw_output_stream` rather than re-encoding through any filter pipeline (matches upstream `PDFCloneUtility.cloneCOSStream`'s `IOUtils.copy(rawInputStream, rawOutputStream)`). (5) **Shared indirect-ref dedup** — two parents sharing the same `COSObject(11, 0, resolved=target)` end up sharing the same cloned target on the destination side (cycle-cache lookup keyed by source identity). No production code change — `pdf_clone_utility.py` already implements every scope item naturally through structural recursion; this round-out only widens test coverage. Test count: 17 → 22 (`tests/multipdf/test_pdf_clone_utility.py -k clone`).
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/pdfua_identification_schema.py`: Wave 42 round-out — PDF/UA-2 (ISO 14289-2) typed-accessor surface. **Behavioural change**: `set_conformance(value)` now validates against `{"A", "B", "U", "Acc"}` (ISO 14289-2 §7 reuses the PDF/A A/B/U triad; `"Acc"` accepted for legacy PDF/UA-1 emitter parity) and raises `BadFieldValueException` (re-used from `pdfa_identification_schema.py`, subclass of `ValueError`) on anything else — previously accepted any string. New accessors: `get_part_value()` (alias of `get_part`), `set_part_property(int)` (upstream-API alias of `set_part`), `is_known_part()` (returns `True` iff stored part ∈ `{1, 2}` per ISO 14289), `is_pdf_ua_1()` / `is_pdf_ua_2()` predicates. `_KNOWN_PARTS` / `_VALID_CONFORMANCE` frozensets surface the ISO-defined value spaces. No upstream `PDFUAIdentificationSchema.java` / `PDFUAIdentificationSchemaTest.java` exists in PDFBox 3.0.x (verified 2026-04-28 via `gh api repos/apache/pdfbox/contents/xmpbox/src/main/java/org/apache/xmpbox/schema?ref=3.0` — only 15 schema classes shipped, none for pdfuaid); the entire class is a pypdfbox enrichment modelled on `PDFAIdentificationSchema`. New hand-written tests in `tests/xmpbox/test_pdfua_identification_schema.py` cover every new accessor (4 valid conformance values × set/get round-trip, invalid + lowercase rejection, BadFieldValueException ⊂ ValueError, all three predicates × {part-1, part-2, absent, future-part-99}, both new aliases). Test count: 15 → 29.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/cff/cff_font.py` + `cff_type1_font.py` + `cff_cid_font.py` + `fd_array.py`: Wave 41 round-out — CFFFont/CFFType1Font/CFFCIDFont API parity with upstream. **CFFFont** new accessors: `add_value_to_top_dict(name, value)` (Top-DICT mutation overlay; layered over fontTools's parsed Top DICT in `get_top_dict` / `get_property`), `get_font_matrix()` (method form of the existing `font_matrix` property), `get_font_b_box()` / `get_font_bbox` alias (returns 4-element `[xMin, yMin, xMax, yMax]` defaulting to `[0,0,0,0]` when `/FontBBox` is missing — upstream throws `IOException`, we diverge for ergonomics), `get_data()` (raw CFF bytes — ``from_bytes`` now stashes the input payload), `get_global_subr_index()` (list of bytecode `bytes`), `get_char_string_bytes()` (per-glyph charstring bytes in GID order), `get_string(sid)` / `get_sid(name)` / `get_name_for_gid(gid)` / `get_sid_for_gid(gid)` / `get_gid_for_sid(sid)` / `get_cid_for_gid(gid)` / `get_gid_for_cid(cid)` (charset SID/CID/GID/name lookups via `fontTools.cffLib.cffStandardStrings` + the font's STRING INDEX). **Tolerance fix**: `get_default_width_x` / `get_nominal_width_x` / `get_private_dict` / `get_local_subrs` / `get_width` now degrade gracefully when the Top DICT carries no `/Private` entry (CIDKeyed CFF — the real Private DICTs live in `/FDArray`); `get_width` additionally consults `cs.private` (the FD-resolved Private DICT fontTools attaches to each CharString) before falling back to the Top-DICT view, so per-FD widths decode correctly. **CFFType1Font**: `code_to_name(code)` now resolves predefined StandardEncoding via `pypdfbox.fontbox.encoding.StandardEncoding.INSTANCE` (e.g. code 65 → "A") and ExpertEncoding via the new static table at `_expert_encoding.py` (e.g. code 65 → "asuperior" per Adobe Technote #5176 Appendix B). New accessors: `name_to_code(name)` (inverse), `get_type1_char_string(name)` (alias of `get_type2_char_string` — upstream's historical name; CFF actually carries Type 2 charstrings), `has_glyph(name)` / `get_path(name)` / `get_width(name)` overrides. **Behavioural change**: previously `code_to_name` returned `".notdef"` for predefined encodings (caller-resolves contract); now resolves directly. **CFFCIDFont**: new `get_font_dicts()` / `get_priv_dicts()` (full /FDArray as `list[dict]`); selector-keyed `has_glyph(selector)` / `get_path(selector)` / `get_width(selector)` (selector is a CID `int` or string of form `"NNN"` / `"cidNNNNN"`); `get_type2_char_string(cid)` overrides base — parameter is now a CID per upstream contract, internally CID→GID via `gid_for_cid`; `get_default_width_x(gid=-1)` / `get_nominal_width_x(gid=-1)` per-GID overrides routing through /FDSelect when `gid >= 0`. **FDArray**: new `font_dicts()` / `private_dicts()` bulk views. New `_expert_encoding.py` table module: code→name resolution for the predefined ExpertEncoding (CFF EncodingId 1) — table built from `CFFExpertEncoding.java`'s `cffExpertEncodingTable` plus the canonical CFF Standard Strings. New tests cover all additions in `tests/fontbox/cff/test_cff_font_parity.py`, `test_cff_type1_font.py`, `test_cff_cid_font.py`. No upstream `CFFFontTest` / `CFFType1FontTest` / `CFFCIDFontTest` / `FDSelectTest` exists in PDFBox 3.0.x to port — those classes are exercised indirectly through `CFFParserTest`.

## Wave 43 — PDFBox parity expansion across fonts, graphics, annotations, catalog/content stream, debugger, XMP

- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/glyph_positioning_table.py` + `kerning_subtable.py` + `naming_table.py`: GPOS structural accessors and pair-adjustment extraction widened, kerning format coverage expanded, and name-table round-out tests added. Parsing continues to delegate to fontTools where that is the more robust format engine; pypdfbox exposes PDFBox-shaped accessors over the parsed data.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/type1/type1_parser.py`: Type 1 parsing now captures a broader top-level dictionary and `FontInfo` surface. This remains a lite parser relative to upstream's full lexer/parser stack, but the public dictionary fields used by the current font consumers are preserved.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_go_to_3d_view.py` (NEW) + `pd_uri_dictionary.py` (NEW) + `pd_action_sound.py`: GoTo3DView, URI dictionary, and sound-action accessors round out the existing action cluster. The richer media/3D annotation payloads still expose raw COS objects where the corresponding typed PDFBox wrappers are not yet ported.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_{printer_mark,redact,three_d,trap_net,watermark}.py` (NEW): typed wrappers for five PDF annotation subtypes. These cover subtype constants and dictionary accessors; rendering, redaction application, trap-network interpretation, and 3D activation semantics remain outside pypdfbox's current non-rendering annotation model.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_cal_gray.py` + `pd_cal_rgb.py` + `pd_device_n.py` + `pd_separation.py`: colour-space accessor parity tightened, including DeviceN/Separation tint-transform and component helpers. Full colour conversion remains delegated to the rendering/color-engine surfaces already documented elsewhere.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/form/pd_form_x_object.py` + `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/pattern/*`: form and pattern accessor parity expanded for struct parents, optional content, grouping/raw dictionaries, tiling constants, bounding boxes, shading typing, and extended-graphics-state hooks.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/logicalstructure/pd_object_reference.py`: OBJR handling now has broader typed accessors and upstream-shaped tests for object-reference kid behavior.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type0_font.py`: Type 0 font consumer wiring now uses the parsed glyph substitution/positioning tables when present, while preserving the existing raw-font fallback behavior.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/outline/pd_outline_item.py` + `pd_document_catalog.py` + `pd_page_content_stream.py`: additional upstream-named accessors and page-content writer operators landed, including more outline state, catalog dictionary hooks, and content-stream drawing/text/path operations.
- `pypdfbox/tools/pdfdebugger.py`: CLI debugger surface expanded. It remains a pypdfbox CLI substitute for upstream PDFBox's Swing debugger rather than a GUI port.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/type/version_type.py` (NEW) + `type_mapping.py`: `VersionType` implements the XMP `stVer` structured type. Wave 43 added the type body; Wave 44 registers and exports it through the public type mapping.

## Wave 44 — five-agent continuation after CHANGES/PROVENANCE audit

- `pypdfbox/contentstream/pdf_graphics_stream_engine.py` + `pdf_stream_engine.py`: text-state operators `Tc`, `Tw`, `Tz`, `TL`, `Tr`, `Ts`, and `T*` now register engine-bound handlers instead of lite no-op stubs. The base engine exposes stable hooks for leading lookup, horizontal scaling, rendering mode, and rise; concrete consumers can override them without replacing parser dispatch.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation.py`: the annotation factory now dispatches the Wave 43 annotation wrappers for `/Redact`, `/3D`, `/Watermark`, `/PrinterMark`, and `/TrapNet`, and the package exports those classes.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/type/type_mapping.py` + package exports: `VersionType` is registered as a structured XMP type and exported from both `pypdfbox.xmpbox.type` and `pypdfbox.xmpbox`.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/horizontal_header_table.py`: exposes `get_reserved1()` through `get_reserved5()` for the parsed `hhea` reserved shorts, matching the existing vertical-header accessor shape.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_content_stream.py`: append mode with `reset_context=True` now mirrors upstream PDFBox by prefixing preserved existing content with `q` and starting the appended stream with `Q`, preventing prior graphics-state changes from leaking into new appended operators.

## Wave 45 — resource, color-operator, XMP versions, GSUB, parser continuation

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_resources.py`: upstream-style `PDResources` round-out — constructor accepts a positional resource cache plus `direct_font_cache`, `get_resource_cache()`, `get_ext_g_state_names()`, `get_properties_names()`, `get_properties()`, `has_color_space()`, and `is_image_x_object()` landed. `get_x_object_names()` now returns `COSName` entries for upstream parity. `add(...)` and `put(...)` support both pypdfbox's explicit-category form and upstream-style typed-resource overloads, including existing-resource key reuse and Form/Image XObject prefixes.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/color/*` + `pdf_graphics_stream_engine.py`: device colour operators `G/g`, `RG/rg`, and `K/k` now build `PDColor` values in DeviceGray, DeviceRGB, and DeviceCMYK and notify engine hooks (`set_stroking_color` / `set_non_stroking_color`) when run through an engine. Standalone registry use and malformed operands remain tolerant no-ops. `_device_color.py` is an original helper shared by the six operator ports.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_media_management_schema.py`: typed `xmpMM:Versions` support landed as an ordered sequence of `VersionType` snapshots, with namespace registration, `VERSIONS`, `add_version()`, and `get_versions()` that filters untyped legacy entries.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/glyph_substitution_table.py`: added `get_lookup_indices_for_feature(feature_tag)`, a pypdfbox structural helper mirroring the existing GPOS helper shape. It walks duplicate GSUB feature records, preserves first-seen lookup order, and deduplicates repeated lookup indices.
- `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py`: `get_xref_offset()` now mirrors the inherited upstream parser accessor: it returns `-1` before parse and the parsed `startxref` byte offset after parse, sharing the same value stored on the existing `COSParser` surface and `COSDocument.start_xref`.

## Wave 46 — names, movie annotations, shading wrappers, PDF/A extension structs, glyph reverse lookup

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_name_dictionary.py`: `/Names /Dests` now returns the modern `PDDestinationNameTreeNode` wrapper, matching PDFBox 3.x. The legacy direct catalog `/Dests` fallback is preserved as `PDDocumentNameDestinationDictionary` so older pypdfbox callers still see the flat dictionary when the entry lives outside `/Names`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_movie.py` (NEW) + `pd_movie_activation.py` (NEW) + `pd_annotation_movie.py`: movie annotations now expose typed `PDMovie` and `PDMovieActivation` wrappers for `/Movie` and dictionary-form `/A`. Raw compatibility accessors remain (`get_movie_dictionary()` and `get_activation_entry()`); boolean activation still round-trips as a Python bool.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/shading/pd_shading_type4.py` + `pd_shading_type5.py`: Type 4/5 mesh shading wrappers now expose `/Decode` as `list[float] | None` while preserving caller-supplied `COSArray` storage, and `/Function` is typed through `PDFunction.create()` with setters accepting `PDFunction`, raw COS values, or `None`.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/type/pdfa_schema_type.py`: `PDFASchemaType` gained typed nested PDF/A extension helpers for `pdfaSchema:property` (`add_property_description()` / `get_property_descriptions()`) and `pdfaSchema:valueType` (`add_value_type_description()` / `get_value_type_descriptions()`), backed by Seq arrays and defensive type filtering.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/encoding/glyph_list.py`: `unicode_to_name()` now aliases the existing reverse sequence lookup and returns `.notdef` for misses, including `None`.

## Wave 47 — field tree, ICC decode, writer xref ranges, PDF/A typed fields, TrueType glyph helpers

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_field_tree.py` (NEW) + `pd_acro_form.py`: `PDAcroForm.get_field_tree()` now returns a `PDFieldTree` iterable wrapper instead of a bare list, matching upstream's read-side shape. The wrapper still implements Python `Sequence` behavior (`len`, indexing, slicing, iteration) so existing list-style callers continue to work.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_icc_based.py`: `PDICCBased.get_default_decode(bits_per_component)` now returns the ICC component `/Range` pairs, falling back to `[0.0, 1.0]` for missing or partial range entries.
- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py`: added `get_x_ref_ranges(entries)`, an upstream-shaped helper that groups sparse xref entries into flattened `first, count` subsection pairs.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/pdfa_identification_schema.py`: PDF/A identification now has typed property accessors for `part`, `amd`, `conformance`, and `rev` (`IntegerType` / `TextType`), and existing scalar getters read through typed fields while preserving validation and legacy scalar storage.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/true_type_font.py`: TrueType font glyph helpers now satisfy the broader `FontBoxFont` protocol: `get_path()` accepts a GID or glyph name, `has_glyph(name)` detects real non-.notdef glyphs, `get_width(name)` returns glyph advance width while preserving the no-arg OS/2 width-class helper, and `get_font_matrix()` / `get_font_b_box` were added.

## Wave 48 — dictionary nulls, catalog dests, AFM metrics, XMP thumbnails, stream depth

- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_dictionary.py`: `set_item(key, None)` and `set_name(key, None)` now remove the entry, and `get_dictionary_object(...)` resolves direct or indirect `COSNull.NULL` to `None` while preserving raw `get_item(...)` behavior.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_catalog.py`: added `set_dests(...)` for the legacy catalog-level `/Dests` dictionary, including `None` removal, while keeping modern `/Names /Dests` name-tree handling on `PDDocumentNameDictionary`.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/afm/font_metrics.py`: added `set_char_metrics(...)`, replacing the full AFM char-metric list and rebuilding the glyph-name lookup map used by width/height helpers.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_basic_schema.py`: XMP Basic `Thumbnails` now exposes the upstream-shaped Alt array of `ThumbnailType` structs through `get_thumbnails()`, `add_thumbnails()`, `set_thumbnails(...)`, and typed property accessors.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/pdf_stream_engine.py`: added public `increase_level()` / `decrease_level()` recursion-depth helpers and routed `process_stream()` through them; underflow now logs and clamps at zero like upstream.

## Wave 49 — COS long helpers, free-text aliases, resource aliases, name constants, rights owner removal

- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_dictionary.py`: added `set_long(...)` / `get_long(...)` helpers, sharing `COSInteger` storage with existing integer accessors while returning Python `int` values and PDFBox-style defaults.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_free_text.py`: free-text annotations now expose upstream-shaped aliases for callout lines, line-ending style, and rectangle differences; `IT_FREE_TEXT` was added as the canonical intent constant while `IT_FREE_TEXT_PLAIN` remains an alias.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_resources.py`: added `get_ext_g_state(...)` as the upstream-spelled alias for the existing extended-graphics-state lookup.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/name_record.py`: restored FontBox 2.x's misspelled `LANGUGAE_*` language-id constants as compatibility aliases while keeping the correctly spelled constants canonical.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_rights_management_schema.py`: added `remove_owner(...)` for `xmpRights:Owner`, supporting both list-backed and typed `ArrayProperty` owner bags.

## Wave 50 — writer constants, page contents, tiling stream parsing, PostScript setters, ASCIIHexFilter

- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/content_stream_writer.py` + `cos_standard_output_stream.py`: exposed upstream-shaped class constants for content-stream spacing and output-stream line endings (`SPACE`, `EOL`, `CRLF`, `LF`).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page.py`: added `has_contents()`, matching upstream's absent/empty stream handling and non-empty `/Contents` array behavior.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/pattern/pd_tiling_pattern.py`: added `get_contents_for_stream_parsing()`, delegating to the random-access content stream like upstream `PDContentStream`.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/post_script_table.py`: added scalar setters for PostScript table metrics and memory fields, plus `set_mim_mem_type1(...)` for upstream typo compatibility.
- `pypdfbox/filter/ascii_hex_filter.py` (NEW) + package exports: added the upstream-named `ASCIIHexFilter` alias and registry entry without changing existing `/ASCIIHexDecode` or `/AHx` resolution.

## Wave 51 — COS null arrays, widget actions, page BBox, OS/2 setters, DCT decode

- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_array.py`: `get_object(index)` now resolves direct or indirect `COSNull.NULL` to `None`, matching the dictionary lookup behavior and upstream `COSArray.getObject`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_widget.py`: widget `/AA` now returns and accepts `PDAnnotationAdditionalActions`, matching the annotation additional-actions wrapper used upstream.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page.py`: added `get_b_box()` / `get_bbox()` for the page content-stream bounding box and tightened `set_user_unit(...)` to reject non-positive values.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/os2_windows_metrics_table.py`: added upstream-shaped setters for OS/2 metric fields including version, weight/width class, Panose, Unicode ranges, typo/win metrics, and code-page ranges.
- `pypdfbox/filter/dct_decode.py` (NEW) + package exports: added `/DCTDecode` JPEG decoding via Pillow, DecodeResult image parameters, long-name and `/DCT` short-name registry wiring, and explicit decode-only `encode()`.

## Wave 52 — xref singleton, FlateFilter, image suffixes, widget parents, header setters

- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer_xref_entry.py`: exposed upstream's `COSWriterXRefEntry.NULLENTRY` singleton and routed `get_null_entry()` through it.
- `pypdfbox/filter/flate_filter.py` (NEW) + package exports: added the upstream-named `FlateFilter` alias and registry entry without changing existing `/FlateDecode` or `/Fl` resolution.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/image/pd_image_x_object.py`: added `is_empty()` and `get_suffix()` mapping image filters to upstream-style export suffixes.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_widget.py`: `set_parent(...)` now accepts `PDTerminalField` and rejects the shared-dictionary single-widget case, matching upstream's typed parent contract.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/header_table.py`: added upstream-shaped setters for parsed `head` table fields including version, revision, checksum, dates, bounding box, style flags, loca format, and glyph data format.

## Wave 53 — dictionary fallback lookup, user-unit parsing, shading extend overloads, TTF table helpers, XMP derived-from aliases

- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_dictionary.py`: `get_dictionary_object(first, second)` now supports PDFBox's fallback-key overload when the second argument is a `COSName` or string, while preserving non-name default values.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page.py`: malformed non-positive parsed `/UserUnit` values now read as the upstream default `1.0`, while setters still reject non-positive values.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/shading/pd_shading_type3.py`: `set_extend(...)` now accepts upstream's single `COSArray` form and single `None` clearing form, in addition to the existing two-boolean form.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/true_type_font.py`: added `get_tables()` and extended `get_table_bytes(...)` to accept a `TTFTable` entry while preserving string-tag lookup.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_media_management_schema.py`: added upstream-shaped `set_derived_from_property(...)` and `get_resource_ref_property()` aliases for the `DerivedFrom` resource reference.

## Wave 54 — output-stream aliases, annotation appearance hook, ProcSet, vertical metrics aliases, ASCII filter sizing

- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_standard_output_stream.py`: added PDFBox-spelled aliases for line writing and state helpers (`writeCRLF`, `writeLF`, `writeEOL`, `getPos`, `isOnNewLine`, `setOnNewLine`).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation.py`: added base `construct_appearances(document=None)` as an upstream-shaped no-op override point for annotation subclasses.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_resources.py`: added legacy `/ProcSet` support via `get_proc_set()` and `set_proc_set(...)`, storing names as a `COSArray` and tolerating malformed read-side entries.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/vertical_metrics_table.py`: added PDFBox-style camelCase aliases `getAdvanceHeight(...)` and `getTopSideBearing(...)` over the existing vertical metrics helpers.
- `pypdfbox/filter/ascii85_decode.py` + `ascii_hex_decode.py`: ASCII85 and ASCIIHex now report unknown decompression input size, matching upstream filter sizing semantics.

## Wave 55 — COS typed helpers, markup popup, device color defaults, naming aliases, LangAlt ordering

- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_dictionary.py`: added typed `get_cos_dictionary(...)` and `get_cos_array(...)` helpers that reuse resolved lookup semantics and return `None` for missing, `COSNull`, or wrong-type values.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_markup.py`: markup annotations now expose `/Popup` through `get_popup()` / `set_popup(...)` and raw rich contents through `get_rich_contents()` / `set_rich_contents(...)`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_resources.py`: device color-space lookup now falls back to built-in `DeviceGray`/`DeviceRGB`/`DeviceCMYK` singletons and honors `/DefaultGray`, `/DefaultRGB`, and `/DefaultCMYK` overrides with the upstream recursion guard.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/naming_table.py`: added PDFBox-style camelCase aliases for name lookup, name records, and common metadata accessors.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_schema.py`: LangAlt writes now keep `x-default` first when the default language value is set or updated, matching upstream ordering.

## Wave 56 — array object lookup, markup external data, XObject key reuse, TTF setters, XMP removal parity

- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_array.py`: added `index_of_object(...)`, matching PDFBox's resolved-entry lookup by finding either a direct value or an indirect `COSObject` whose target equals the requested object.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_markup.py`: markup annotations now expose raw `/ExData` through `get_external_data()` / `set_external_data(...)` until a typed external-data wrapper lands.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_resources.py`: `add_x_object(...)` now accepts a custom prefix and returns the existing key when the same XObject COS object is already registered.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/maximum_profile_table.py` + `horizontal_header_table.py`: added upstream-shaped setters for `numGlyphs` and `numberOfHMetrics`.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_schema.py`: removing a Bag or Seq value now removes all matching entries, matching upstream array-property removal semantics.

## Wave 57 — array float helpers, caret aliases, indirect XObject reuse, maxp version setter, XMP language removal

- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_array.py`: added `set_float(...)` / `get_float(...)` typed helpers with PDFBox-style defaults and integer-to-float read compatibility.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/pd_annotation_caret.py`: added `get_rect_differences()` / `set_rect_differences(...)` aliases over the existing rectangle-difference accessors.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_resources.py`: duplicate resource-key detection now recognizes an existing indirect `COSObject` entry whose resolved target is the XObject being added.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/maximum_profile_table.py`: added `set_version(...)` for the parsed `maxp` table version field.
- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/xmp_schema.py`: added `remove_unqualified_language_property_value(...)` for removing a single LangAlt language entry while preserving other languages.

- `pypdfbox/cos/cos_array.py`: added `set_boolean(...)` / `get_boolean(...)` typed helpers with PDFBox-style default handling.

- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/type/lang_alt.py`: setting a language value now removes all existing entries for that language before appending the replacement, preventing duplicate malformed LangAlt children from surviving.

## Wave 199 — PDType1Font path / width / Standard 14 constants round-out

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type1_font.py`:
  - Added 14 PostScript ``BaseFont`` string constants directly on ``PDType1Font`` (``HELVETICA``, ``HELVETICA_BOLD``, ``HELVETICA_OBLIQUE``, ``HELVETICA_BOLD_OBLIQUE``, ``TIMES_ROMAN``, ``TIMES_BOLD``, ``TIMES_ITALIC``, ``TIMES_BOLD_ITALIC``, ``COURIER``, ``COURIER_BOLD``, ``COURIER_OBLIQUE``, ``COURIER_BOLD_OBLIQUE``, ``SYMBOL``, ``ZAPF_DINGBATS``) — values match upstream ``Standard14Fonts.FontName`` ``getName()`` exactly so callers can spell ``PDType1Font.HELVETICA`` ergonomically without reaching for the upstream enum.
  - Added ``SUBSTITUTE_NOTDEF_WIDTH = 250.0`` named constant for the PDFBOX-1900 sentinel previously hardcoded inline by upstream's ``getWidthFromFont``.
  - ``get_path(name)`` now mirrors upstream ``PDType1Font.getPath(String)`` — short-circuits to ``[]`` for ``.notdef`` on non-embedded fonts (PDFBOX-2421) and routes the program lookup through ``get_name_in_font`` so ``ALT_NAMES`` ligature fallbacks (``ff`` → ``f_f``, ArialMT ``ellipsis`` → ``elipsis``) reach the program.
  - Added ``get_path_for_code(code)`` mirroring upstream ``PDType1Font.getPath(int)`` — encoding-keyed path lookup.
  - Added ``get_normalized_path_for_code(code)`` mirroring upstream ``PDType1Font.getNormalizedPath(int)`` — falls back to the ``.notdef`` glyph path when the primary lookup yields ``[]``.
  - Added ``get_width_from_font(code)`` mirroring upstream ``PDType1Font.getWidthFromFont`` — returns ``SUBSTITUTE_NOTDEF_WIDTH`` for substituted ``.notdef`` (PDFBOX-1900), otherwise the program advance, otherwise the Standard 14 AFM advance, otherwise ``0.0``.

## Wave 71 — Filter parity (ASCII85 alias, deflate-level configuration)

- `pypdfbox/filter/ascii85_filter.py`: new upstream-named alias module mirroring `org.apache.pdfbox.filter.ASCII85Filter`, registered alongside the existing `ASCII85Decode` codec.
- `pypdfbox/filter/filter.py`: added upstream-parity statics `SYSPROP_DEFLATELEVEL`, `SYSPROP_CCITTFAX_MAXBYTES`, and `get_compression_level()`. Java reads these as system properties (`-D...`); the Python port reads them from `os.environ` because Python lacks an equivalent property facility.
- `pypdfbox/filter/flate_decode.py`: `encode` now honours `Filter.get_compression_level()`, matching upstream's `Deflater(getCompressionLevel())` behaviour. Default (`-1`, zlib default) preserves prior output.

## PDType1Font — name-resolution / glyph-probe round-out

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type1_font.py`: added `ALT_NAMES` ligature-fallback table and `PFB_START_MARKER` constants, `code_to_name(code)`, `get_name_in_font(name)`, `has_glyph(name)`, `has_glyph_for_code(code)`, `read_code(stream | bytes)`, and `get_type1_font()` (alias of `get_font_program`). **Behavior deviation**: upstream `getNameInFont` always has a generic substitute font in hand, so it can return `".notdef"` when neither the embedded program nor the substitute carries the name. The Python port has no built-in system-font substitution path; when there is no embedded program at all, `get_name_in_font` returns the input name unchanged rather than `".notdef"` — we have no negative evidence to remap on. Once an embedded program (or an injected `set_font_program`) is available, behavior matches upstream.

## Action cluster — set_destination validation, URI UTF-8 fallback, JS string ctor

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_go_to.py`: `set_destination(PDPageDestination)` now mirrors upstream `PDActionGoTo#setDestination` validation — raises `ValueError` (Python equivalent of `IllegalArgumentException`) when the supplied page-destination array's first element is not a `COSDictionary`. Two pre-existing tests that built local-GoTo destinations via `set_page_number` (a remote-only setter) were updated to call `set_page(<page dict>)` instead.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_uri.py`: `get_uri()` now matches upstream `PDActionURI.getURI()` byte handling — UTF-16 BE/LE when a BOM is present; otherwise UTF-8 (was previously decoded via `COSDictionary.get_string`, which falls back to PDFDocEncoding and produced mojibake for valid UTF-8 URIs).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/action/pd_action_java_script.py`: added the upstream string-constructor overload — `PDActionJavaScript("...")` constructs the action and immediately writes the source to `/JS`, matching `PDActionJavaScript(String js)` upstream.

## PDFMergerUtility — stream-cache / compress-parameters parity round-out

- `pypdfbox/multipdf/pdf_merger_utility.py`: added `get_stream_cache_create_function` / `set_stream_cache_create_function` and `get_compress_parameters` / `set_compress_parameters` accessor pairs, mirroring upstream's `mergeDocuments(StreamCacheCreateFunction)` and `mergeDocuments(StreamCacheCreateFunction, CompressParameters)` overloads. `merge_documents` and `merge_documents_random_access_read` now accept `stream_cache_create_function` / `compress_parameters` keyword arguments and stage them on the instance for the duration of the run. Both arguments are advisory only — destination ``PDDocument`` construction in this port does not yet thread them through, matching the existing `memory_usage_setting` parity placeholder.

## Outline cluster — equality / hashing, /Type normalization, iterator cycle-aware hasNext

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/outline/pd_outline_node.py`: added `__eq__` / `__hash__` mirroring upstream `PDDictionaryWrapper#equals` / `#hashCode` — two outline wrappers compare equal when (and only when) they wrap the same `COSDictionary` instance, so fresh wrappers returned by `get_next_sibling` / `get_first_child` compare equal to the original. `PDOutlineItemIterator.has_next` is now cycle-aware (matches upstream `PDOutlineItemIterator#hasNext`): returns `False` once the cursor would revisit a previously yielded node, instead of returning `True` followed by a synthetic `StopIteration` from `__next__`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/outline/pd_document_outline.py`: constructor now unconditionally writes `/Type /Outlines` on the wrapped dictionary (previously skipped when `/Type` was already present). Mirrors upstream `PDDocumentOutline(COSDictionary)` exactly, normalising stale or wrong `/Type` markers on wrap.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/outline/pd_outline_item.py`: added `set_previous_sibling` public alias for the internal `_set_previous_sibling` setter, paired with the existing public `set_next_sibling` for hand-built test fixtures.

## Text operator round-out — MoveText null text-line-matrix guard

- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/text/move_text.py`: added the upstream `LOG.warn("TextLineMatrix is null, ...")` guard from `org.apache.pdfbox.contentstream.operator.text.MoveText`. Because cluster #2's base `PDFStreamEngine.get_text_line_matrix` returns `None` unconditionally (no real text-state tracking yet), the guard is gated on the engine subclass having actually overridden `get_text_line_matrix` — base-engine callers see no behavior change, rendering / text-extraction subclasses pick the guard up automatically. Mirrors upstream behavior without breaking cluster #2 callers that drive Td without a real text-state object yet.

## Text operator round-out — TD single-leading notification, T* uses COSFloat.ZERO

- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/text/move_text_set_leading.py`: ``TD`` now fires the leading change exactly once. Previously the handler invoked `ctx.set_text_leading(...)` directly *and* dispatched a synthetic ``TL`` op when a ``TL`` handler was registered — yielding a double notification (the registered ``SetTextLeading`` handler also calls `ctx.set_text_leading`). The handler now uses the synthetic ``TL`` dispatch when a ``TL`` handler is registered (mirroring upstream's `processOperator(SET_TEXT_LEADING, ...)`) and falls back to a direct engine notification only when no ``TL`` handler exists, so cluster #2 subclasses without a registered ``TL`` still observe the change.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/text/next_line_op.py`: ``T*`` synthesizes its inner ``Td`` using the interned `COSFloat.ZERO` constant for the ``tx`` operand instead of constructing a fresh `COSFloat(0.0)`, mirroring upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.contentstream.operator.text.NextLine`'s use of `COSFloat.ZERO`.

## Viewer-prefs / page-labels round-out — None-clearing setters and convenience accessors

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_viewer_preferences.py`: name-valued setters (`set_non_full_screen_page_mode`, `set_reading_direction` / `set_direction`, `set_view_area`, `set_view_clip`, `set_print_area`, `set_print_clip`, `set_duplex`, `set_print_scaling`) now treat `None` as a clear (`remove_item`) instead of writing the literal `/None` token. Java upstream's enum-typed setters can't accept null, so the previous `str(None)` path was a latent bug; pattern matches `PDPageLabelRange.set_style(None)`. Added `get_enforce_names()` / `set_enforce_names(list[str] | None)` typed-list helpers around the existing raw `/Enforce` accessors (PDF 32000-2 §12.4.4) — Python convenience layer; not in upstream PDFBox 3.0.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_page_labels.py`: added `has_label_range(start_page) -> bool`, `remove_label_range(start_page) -> bool`, `get_first_page_index() -> int | None`, and `get_last_page_index() -> int | None`. The first / last accessors mirror Java's `NavigableSet.first()` / `last()` on the result of `getPageIndices()`; the has/remove pair fills in the obvious counterparts to upstream's `setLabelItem`. None of these are in upstream PDFBox 3.0 — Python convenience layer.

## tools/decrypt + tools/encrypt parity round-out

- `pypdfbox/tools/decrypt.py`: now matches upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.tools.Decrypt#call` exit codes — returns 1 (with `Error: Document is not encrypted.`) when the input has no `/Encrypt`, and returns 1 (with `Error: You are only allowed to decrypt a document with the owner password.`) when the supplied password unlocks the document but only with user-level permissions. IO errors are formatted as `Error decrypting document [<class>]: <msg>` to match upstream's stderr line. Adds `-keyStore`/`--keyStore` and `-alias`/`--alias` CLI flags for PKCS#12-keystore-based public-key recipients (CLI surface parity); the end-to-end public-key decryption pipeline is not yet wired into `PDDocument.decrypt`, so passing `-keyStore` surfaces a parity-shaped `Error decrypting document [NotImplementedError]: …` message and exits 4. The library helper `decrypt_pdf` keeps the previous tolerant pass-through (no error gates) — the gates live on the CLI, mirroring upstream's split between `Decrypt#call` and `Loader.loadPDF`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/standard_security_handler.py`: `prepare_for_decryption` now sets the `current_access_permission` after a successful key derivation — owner-path matches set `AccessPermission.get_owner_access_permission()`, user-path matches set `AccessPermission(perms).set_read_only()`. R5/R6 default to /P-derived permissions (an owner-vs-user discriminator there is left as future work — none of the existing tests rely on it). Mirrors upstream `StandardSecurityHandler#prepareForDecryption` lines 245-272.
- `pypdfbox/loader.py` + `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document.py`: `Loader.load_pdf`'s auto-decrypt path now stashes the prepared `_security_handler` and `_encryption` on the returned `COSDocument`; `PDDocument.__init__` picks them up so a caller-visible wrapper (built via `PDDocument.load`, which re-wraps the loader's result) reports `get_current_access_permission()` correctly without re-running PBKDF2. Previously the handler attached to a transient decrypt-time `PDDocument` was discarded.
- `pypdfbox/tools/encrypt.py`: `-canPrintFaithful` now drives `AccessPermission.set_can_print_faithful` (the canonical name for the high-quality print bit) instead of the legacy `set_can_print_degraded` alias. Behavior identical (both target the same FAITHFUL_PRINT_BIT); only the call-site name changes.

## PDFunction parity round-out (Type 2 / Type 3 + base aliases)

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/pd_function_type2.py`: `eval` now sizes the result by `min(len(/C0), len(/C1))` to match upstream `PDFunctionType2.eval` (`new float[Math.min(c0.size(), c1.size())]`). Previously the port sized by `len(/C0)` and padded a short `/C1` with zeros — a defensive divergence that had no actual call-site dependency. Restoring upstream parity makes shading/tint output dimensions match Java byte-for-byte. Added `__str__` matching upstream `toString()` format `"FunctionType2{C0: <c0> C1: <c1> N: <n>}"` (the base class still falls through to `"FunctionType<n>"` for Types 0, 3, 4 — upstream only overrides on Type 2).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/pd_function_type3.py`: added `get_functions_array() -> COSArray | None` (raw-array accessor mirroring upstream `getFunctions()` which returns `COSArray`; the existing `get_functions()` continues to return a materialised `list[PDFunction]` for the typical eval path) and `get_encode_for_parameter(n) -> tuple[float, float] | None` (publicly exposed counterpart to upstream's private `getEncodeForParameter(int)`).
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/function/pd_function.py`: added `get_domain_values()` / `get_range_values()` / `set_domain_values()` / `set_range_values()` upstream-named aliases (PDFBox `getDomainValues` is private and `setDomainValues`/`setRangeValues` are public; we expose all four for symmetry).

## graphics operator parity (DrawObject / ShadingFill validation + upstream-name aliases)

- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/graphics/shading_fill.py`: `process` now raises `MissingOperandException` when called with an empty operand list, matching upstream `ShadingFill.process` (`if (operands.isEmpty()) throw new MissingOperandException(...)`). When operand 0 is not a `COSName` the operator silently returns rather than upstream's second `MissingOperandException` throw — pypdfbox follows the leniency precedent established by the path operators (`MoveTo`, `LineTo`, `CurveTo`, `AppendRectangleToPath`) which silently skip type-mismatched operands in malformed content streams.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/graphics/invoke_named_xobject.py`: `process` now raises `MissingOperandException` on an empty operand list (upstream `DrawObject.process` first guard) and silently returns when operand 0 is not a `COSName` (upstream `if (!(base0 instanceof COSName)) return;` early-return). The existing test that asserted the lite-stub no-op behaviour ("engine layer will validate") was updated to assert the new upstream-parity behaviour.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/graphics/__init__.py`: added upstream-name aliases re-binding the existing concrete handlers — `DrawObject = InvokeNamedXObject`, `FillNonZeroRule = FillPathNonZeroWinding`, `FillEvenOddRule = FillPathEvenOdd`, `ClipNonZeroRule = ClipNonZeroWinding`, `ClipEvenOddRule = ClipEvenOdd`, `EndPath = EndPathNoOp`. Code ported from upstream PDFBox can keep its original imports (`from pypdfbox.contentstream.operator.graphics import FillNonZeroRule`); `DrawObject is InvokeNamedXObject` etc. so registry lookups and `isinstance` checks continue to work unchanged. `StrokePath` and `ClosePath` are also re-exported from the graphics package (they already use their upstream names in `path/`) so all upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.contentstream.operator.graphics` class identifiers resolve via this package.

## PDFileSpecification family parity round-out

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/filespecification/pd_file_specification.py`: `create_fs` now dereferences a `COSObject` indirect reference before classification — when given an unresolved indirect ref it returns `None` (matches the `null` outcome upstream gets after parser dereferencing); when resolved to a `COSString` or `COSDictionary` it dispatches as if called with the dereferenced value. Upstream Java relies on the parser having already auto-dereffed by the time `createFS(COSBase)` is called, so this is a small behavioural extension to avoid surprising `OSError("Unknown file specification …")` in pypdfbox callers that pass through raw refs.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/filespecification/pd_embedded_file.py`: added `get_mac_res_fork()` / `set_mac_res_fork()` mechanical-name aliases delegating to the existing `get_mac_resource_fork()` / `set_mac_resource_fork()` methods. Upstream `getMacResFork` / `setMacResFork` are typed `String`; the type deviation to `COSStream` (PDF spec `/ResFork` is a stream) is the one previously documented under this file's enrichment entry — these aliases cover the upstream method names verbatim.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/common/filespecification/pd_embedded_file.py`: added `get_check_sum_string()` / `set_check_sum_string()` string-form aliases mirroring upstream `getCheckSum()` / `setCheckSum(String)` verbatim (upstream return type is `String`). The byte-form `get_check_sum()` / `set_check_sum()` introduced earlier (with hex-form encoding for non-printable bytes) remains the primary pypdfbox API; the string-form aliases are provided for callers that prefer the upstream-typed surface. Added class-level Type-name constants `PDComplexFileSpecification.FILESPEC` (`"Filespec"`) and `PDEmbeddedFile.EMBEDDED_FILE` (`"EmbeddedFile"`) matching upstream `COSName.FILESPEC` / `COSName.EMBEDDED_FILE`.

## XMP simple-type parity round-out (URLType / RenditionClassType)

- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/type/type_mapping.py`: the `"URL"` short type-name now resolves to the new `URLType` class (was previously aliased to `URIType` while the dedicated class was unported), matching upstream `Types.URL(true, Text, URLType.class)`. `create_url(...)` now returns `URLType`; a new `create_rendition_class(...)` factory mirrors upstream `TypeMapping.createRenditionClass`. The `"RenditionClass"` short type-name is registered for `instanciate_simple_property`.

## Name-tree subclass parity round-out

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/documentnavigation/destination/pd_destination_name_tree_node.py`: `convert_cos_to_value` now mirrors upstream `convertCOSToPD` — when the leaf COS value is a `COSDictionary`, the `/D` entry is dereferenced before dispatch (named-destination indirection inlined into the leaf). Invalid leaf entries return `None` instead of raising, matching PDFBOX-5975. Previous pypdfbox behaviour raised `OSError` on any non-`PDPageDestination` result.

## XObject factory parity (PDXObject.create_x_object)

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/pd_x_object.py`: added `PDXObject.create_x_object(base, resources)` static factory mirroring upstream `PDXObject.createXObject(COSBase, PDResources)`. Dispatches `/Subtype /Image` → `PDImageXObject`, `/Subtype /Form` → `PDFormXObject` (the `PDTransparencyGroup` form subclass is not yet ported — the plain `PDFormXObject` is returned, with the group dictionary still discoverable via `get_group_attributes()`). `/Subtype /PS` raises `OSError("PDPostScriptXObject is not yet supported")` instead of returning a `PDPostScriptXObject` instance because that subclass is not yet ported. Other subtype values raise `OSError` matching upstream's `IOException("Invalid XObject Subtype: …")`. Non-stream `base` raises `OSError("Unexpected object type: …")`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/form/pd_form_x_object.py`: added typed `get_group_attributes() / set_group_attributes(PDTransparencyGroupAttributes)` mirroring upstream `getGroup() / setGroup(PDTransparencyGroupAttributes)`. The pre-existing raw `get_group() / set_group(COSDictionary)` accessors are retained for backward compatibility with call sites that already store the dictionary directly. `set_group(...)` invalidates the typed cache so a subsequent `get_group_attributes()` re-wraps the freshly installed dict.

## tools/split + tools/merge CLI parity round-out

- `pypdfbox/tools/split.py`: added `-password` / `--password` flag (passes through to `PDDocument.load(..., password=...)`) — matches upstream `PDFSplit.java`'s `@Option(names = "-password", interactive = true)`. Page-range default behaviour now matches upstream: when `-startPage` and/or `-endPage` are supplied without an explicit `-split`, the entire range is emitted as a SINGLE output file (upstream calls `setSplitAtPage(numberOfPages)` / `setSplitAtPage(endPage)` in this branch — see `PDFSplit.java#call`). Previously pypdfbox always defaulted `-split` to 1 and produced one file per page in the range — a behavioural deviation from upstream PDFSplit. The `-split` argument now uses `-1` as the upstream "not supplied" sentinel; an explicit `0` or negative value still exits 2 with the existing `-split must be >= 1` message.
- `pypdfbox/tools/merge.py`: load / save errors now emit upstream `PDFMerger.java`'s user-visible error format `"Error merging documents [<ExcClass>]: <message>"` and exit 4, instead of bubbling the `OSError` up to the cli-level catch-all. The minimum-two-inputs guard (a deliberate pypdfbox UX deviation; upstream picocli accepts arity >= 1) is retained.

## SetStrokingColorN / SetNonStrokingColorN / SetStrokingColorSpace / SetNonStrokingColorSpace parity round-out

- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/color/set_stroking_color_n.py`, `set_non_stroking_color_n.py`: lifted from registry-only stubs to full upstream parity. `SCN` / `scn` now subclass `SetStrokingColor` / `SetNonStrokingColor` (matching the upstream hierarchy) and override `process` to also handle `PDPattern` colour spaces -- for non-Pattern spaces the operand-count and `COSNumber`-type checks mirror upstream `SetColor.process`, including the PDFBOX-5851 invalid-`PDColor([], None)` fallback on type mismatch. The pre-existing leniency deviation from upstream -- `SetColor.process` returns silently on too-few operands instead of upstream raising `MissingOperandException` -- is inherited from the parent `SetStrokingColor` / `SetNonStrokingColor` operator family.
- `pypdfbox/contentstream/operator/color/set_stroking_color_space.py`, `set_non_stroking_color_space.py`: lifted from registry-only stubs. `CS` / `cs` now resolve the operand `COSName` through `PDFStreamEngine.get_resources().get_color_space(name)`, install the resolved `PDColorSpace` on the graphics state via `set_stroking_color_space` / `set_non_stroking_color_space`, and reset the corresponding stroking / non-stroking colour to the new colour space's `get_initial_color()` (matching upstream). Honours `is_should_process_color_operators()` for Type3 charprocs / uncoloured tiling patterns. Standalone (no engine) and malformed operand lists remain tolerant no-ops, matching the existing leniency precedent for content-stream operators in pypdfbox.

## DateConverter port — xmpbox utility for ISO 8601 / PDF date strings

- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/date_converter.py` (NEW): port of `org.apache.xmpbox.DateConverter`. Surfaces `DateConverter.to_calendar(str | None) -> datetime | None` and `DateConverter.to_iso8601(datetime, print_millis=False) -> str` (also exposed as module-level functions). Returns timezone-aware `datetime` instead of `java.util.Calendar`; naive ISO 8601 strings are anchored to UTC (matches upstream `fromISO8601` `LocalDateTime.atZone(ZoneId.of("UTC"))` fallback). Year 0 input is rejected with `OSError` because Python `datetime` does not support year 0 — upstream `0000-01-01` round-trips to `0001-01-01` via `GregorianCalendar` BCE handling. The constructor raises `TypeError` to mirror upstream `private DateConverter()`. Wired into `pypdfbox.xmpbox.__init__` for re-export.

## ContentStreamWriter — write_tokens iterable acceptance

- `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/content_stream_writer.py`: `write_tokens(...)` now accepts any iterable (generator, `deque`, `map`, custom `Iterable`) as the single-argument `List<?>` overload, not just `list` / `tuple`. Token / bytes-like single-argument calls (`write_tokens(cos_array)`, `write_tokens(b"raw")`) keep their varargs semantics. Upstream's Java signature is `writeTokens(List<?>)` only; this is a Pythonic ergonomic extension — output bytes are unchanged for any input upstream would have accepted.

## PDFontDescriptor — mask-based flag accessors + set_panose writer

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_font_descriptor.py`: round-out additions. New public `is_flag_bit_on(mask)` / `set_flag_bit(mask, value)` mask-based flag accessors mirror upstream's *private* `isFlagBitOn(int)` / `setFlagBit(int, boolean)` helpers — exposed publicly here because the `FLAG_*` constants are part of the pypdfbox public surface; complements the existing `get_flag(bit)` / `set_flag(bit, value)` 1-based-index accessors. New `set_panose(PDPanose | bytes | bytearray | None)` writer is a pypdfbox extension — upstream PDFBox 3.0 `PDFontDescriptor` exposes only the read side (`getPanose()`); the new writer lazily creates the `/Style` dict, stores the 12-byte buffer as a `COSString`, and on `None` removes `/Panose` (and the now-empty `/Style` dict). Accepts a `PDPanose` wrapper or raw 12-byte buffer. No upstream method renamed or behaviour changed.

## PDDocumentCatalog — get_acro_form fixup overload + auto-create /AA, /Threads parity

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_catalog.py`: `get_acro_form()` now accepts an optional `acro_form_fixup` argument (mirrors upstream `getAcroForm(PDDocumentFixup)` overload). When supplied, the fixup's `apply()` is invoked once, the cached wrapper is invalidated, and the same fixup instance on subsequent calls is treated as already applied (matches upstream `acroFormFixupApplied` tracking). pypdfbox does not yet ship `AcroFormDefaultFixup`, so the no-arg `get_acro_form()` continues to return the unfixed AcroForm — passing `None` is the documented way to request that behaviour, parity with upstream's `getAcroForm(null)` contract.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_catalog.py`: `get_actions()` now auto-creates an empty `/AA` sub-dictionary when absent (mirrors upstream's `if (addAction == null) { addAction = new COSDictionary(); root.setItem(COSName.AA, addAction); }` pattern). Always returns a non-`None` `PDDocumentCatalogAdditionalActions`. Previous behaviour returned `None` when `/AA` was absent.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_catalog.py`: `get_threads()` now auto-creates an empty `/Threads` array when absent (mirrors upstream `if (array == null) { array = new COSArray(); ... root.setItem(COSName.THREADS, array); }`). Returned list is always empty when no threads are present, but the catalog now records `/Threads` as a side effect — matches upstream so callers that mutate the returned list-like value write back into the catalog. Java's `array.setDirect(false)` flag has no Python analogue and is omitted.

## PDSignature.__str__ + PDSignatureField parity round-out

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/pd_signature.py`: new `__str__` returns a compact `PDSignature(name=..., reason=..., location=..., date=..., contact=...)` summary of the populated identity fields. Java's `Object.toString()` is `ClassName@hashcode` which is not useful for end users; upstream `PDSignatureField.getValueAsString()` calls `signature.toString()` so the lite port routes that through this populated-fields summary instead of the bare repr. Empty/absent entries are omitted; when nothing is populated the body is the placeholder `<empty>`.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_signature_field.py`: `get_value_as_string()` now returns `str(self.get_signature())` when `/V` is present (was: always `""`). Mirrors upstream `PDSignatureField.getValueAsString()` which delegates to `signature.toString()`. Empty when no signature is set, matching upstream's null-check.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_signature_field.py`: `set_value(PDSignature)` now invokes `self.apply_change()` after writing `/V`. Mirrors upstream `PDSignatureField.setValue(PDSignature)` which ends with `applyChange()` so subclasses overriding `apply_change` for cache invalidation get notified. The lite port's default `apply_change` is still a logging no-op (appearance regeneration deferred).

## ArrayProperty — complex-property surface round-out

- `pypdfbox/xmpbox/type/array_property.py`: added `get_property(field_name)`, `get_array_property(field_name)`, `get_properties_by_local_name(local_name)`, plus `add_namespace` / `get_namespace_prefix` / `get_all_namespaces_with_prefix` namespace-map accessors. Mirrors the `AbstractComplexProperty` surface that upstream's `ArrayProperty` inherits — the pypdfbox port skipped `AbstractComplexProperty` so these were missing on `ArrayProperty` directly. **Behavior deviation**: `get_array_property(field_name)` returns `None` when the named child exists but is not an `ArrayProperty`; upstream casts unconditionally and would raise `ClassCastException`. Returning `None` keeps the call site type-safe and matches the existing `get_array_property` shape on `AbstractStructuredType` in the pypdfbox port.

## FontMapper / FontInfo / FontProvider / CIDFontMapping — interface round-out

- `pypdfbox/fontbox/font_format.py` + `font_info.py` + `font_provider.py` + `cid_font_mapping.py` (NEW): port the missing pieces of the upstream FontMapper SPI. `FontFormat` is a plain enum (TTF/OTF/PFB). `FontInfo` is the abstract per-font descriptor returned by `FontProvider.get_font_info()`; the package-private upstream helpers `getWeightClassAsPanose` / `getCodePageRange` are surfaced as public methods (`get_weight_class_as_panose` / `get_code_page_range`) since Python has no equivalent visibility. `FontProvider` is the abstract enumeration source — pypdfbox does **not** ship a concrete `FileSystemFontProvider` (upstream's default scans system font directories via java.awt; bringing that to Python would require a new dep like fontconfig / matplotlib.font_manager). Apps wanting full system-font enumeration plug their own provider into a custom `FontMapper`.
- `pypdfbox/fontbox/font_mapper.py`: added the third interface method `get_cid_font(base_font, font_descriptor, cid_system_info) -> CIDFontMapping | None`. **Deviation**: upstream Java declares this `abstract` on the interface; pypdfbox keeps it concrete with a default `None` return so existing `FontMapper` subclasses (and the pypdfbox `DefaultFontMapper`, which has no system-font scanner) don't spontaneously become abstract. Real CID-aware mappers override it to return a `CIDFontMapping`.

## Overlay — `_load_pdfs` filename precedence parity

- `pypdfbox/multipdf/overlay.py`: `_load_pdfs` now mirrors upstream's load-order: when **both** a filename and a `PDDocument` are configured for the same overlay slot, the filename wins — the document is reloaded from disk and any previously-staged `PDDocument` is replaced. Previously the pypdfbox port short-circuited (`if filename is not None and document is None`) so a setter-supplied PDF blocked the file reload. Affects `set_input_file` / `set_input_pdf`, plus the parallel default / first / last / odd / even / all-pages overlay slots. Mirrors `Overlay.loadPDFs` in PDFBox 3.0.x.

## PDArtifactMarkedContent — `getNameAsString` parity for `/Type` and `/Subtype`

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/documentinterchange/taggedpdf/pd_artifact_marked_content.py`: `get_type()` and `get_subtype()` now resolve both `COSName` and `COSString` operands, mirroring upstream `COSDictionary.getNameAsString(COSName)`. The previous lookup went through pypdfbox's stricter `COSDictionary.get_name`, which only resolves `COSName` operands and silently returned `None` for `COSString`-encoded artifact types. Authoring tools occasionally store `/Type` and `/Subtype` as strings; the artifact accessors now match upstream's tolerant read. Added `get_bbox()` alias for `get_b_box()` matching the spelling already used by sibling pypdfbox wrappers (e.g. `PDPage.get_bbox`).

## PDAcroForm — set_fields(None) hardening + raw /SigFlags accessors

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_acro_form.py`: `set_fields()` now accepts `None` and treats it as "clear /Fields to an empty array" (mirrors the constructor's seeded shape). Upstream `setFields(null)` would NPE in `new COSArray(null)`; pypdfbox normalises so callers can reset the form to "no fields" with a single call. The cache is invalidated, matching the existing list-replacement path.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_acro_form.py`: new `get_signature_flags()` / `set_signature_flags(int)` raw `/SigFlags` accessors, plus public class-level `FLAG_SIGNATURES_EXIST` / `FLAG_APPEND_ONLY` constants. Upstream keeps the bit constants package-private and exposes only the typed `isSignaturesExist` / `setAppendOnly` bit-by-bit helpers; pypdfbox surfaces the raw integer too so callers can preserve reserved bits across round-trips. The typed setters continue to mask their bit only — unrelated bits round-trip untouched. Also fixed a Python-3 except-clause bug (`except AttributeError, TypeError:` was binding `AttributeError` as the variable named `TypeError`, never catching `TypeError` from numeric coercion in the form-XObject `/BBox` reader); now `except (AttributeError, TypeError):`.

## PDDocumentNameDictionary / PDDocumentNameDestinationDictionary — surface round-out

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_name_dictionary.py`: added `is_empty()` predicate and `__bool__`. Upstream PDFBox does not expose ``isEmpty()`` on the wrapper directly; callers reach through ``getCOSObject().isEmpty()``. pypdfbox surfaces it on the wrapper for symmetry with ``COSDictionary.is_empty()``. Also added `get_java_script()` as the strict snake_case translation of upstream ``getJavaScript()`` — the existing ``get_javascript()`` (lowercase ``script``) form is retained as the original spelling.
- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document_name_destination_dictionary.py`: added `is_empty()`, `get_names() -> list[str]`, `__contains__(name)` (string or COSName) and `__len__()`. Upstream ``PDDocumentNameDestinationDictionary`` exposes only ``getDestination(String)`` so callers cannot enumerate or test membership without constructing every destination wrapper; the new accessors delegate to ``COSDictionary.is_empty`` / ``key_set`` / ``contains_key`` / ``size``. ``__contains__`` distinguishes ``key missing`` from ``key present, value malformed`` (the latter still returns ``None`` from ``get_destination``).

## PDFontDescriptor — getNameAsString lenience + value-type dunders

- `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_font_descriptor.py`: `get_font_name()` and `get_font_stretch()` now resolve both `COSName` and `COSString` operands, mirroring upstream `COSDictionary.getNameAsString(COSName)`. The previous lookup went through pypdfbox's stricter `COSDictionary.get_name`, which only resolves `COSName` and silently returned `None` for `COSString`-encoded font names — a tolerance gap against upstream's `dic.getNameAsString(FONT_NAME)` / `getNameAsString(FONT_STRETCH)` calls. Also added a diagnostic `__repr__` on `PDFontDescriptor` (`PDFontDescriptor(font_name=..., flags=...)`) — pypdfbox extension; upstream inherits Java's default ``Object.toString``. `PDPanose` and `PDPanoseClassification` gained value-equality (`__eq__` / `__hash__`) and `__repr__` based on their underlying byte buffers — pypdfbox extensions; upstream relies on Java's default identity ``equals`` / ``hashCode``. Treating these immutable wrappers as value types lets callers compare and hash PANOSE blocks (e.g. as dict keys, in test assertions).

## PDFontDescriptor — class-level FLAG constants + has_font_file predicates + PDPanose.with_panose_classification
